### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Arquitetura e Repositório Base

## Arquitetura de Sistema V10

### ADR-001: Arquitetura Microserviços com Core Monolítico
**Data:** 2024-01-15
**Status:** Aceita
**Autores:** Tech Lead

**CONTEXTO:**
DIYAPP evoluiu para uma plataforma complexa com múltiplos módulos (WhatsApp, Email, SMS, Dashboard, Analytics). A arquitetura monolítica atual dificulta deploy independente, escalabilidade seletiva e manutenção paralela. Precisamos de uma arquitetura que permita evolução contínua sem comprometer estabilidade.

**DECISÃO:**
Adotar arquitetura híbrida: Core monolítico + módulos como microserviços. O Core gerencia autenticação, configuração, logging e orquestração. Cada módulo roda como serviço independente, comunicando-se via API REST e eventos.

**OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:**
- **Opção A:** Monolito puro (atual) — Prós: Simplicidade, deploy único. Contras: Acoplamento alto, dificuldade de escalar componentes específicos.
- **Opção B:** Microserviços completos — Prós: Desacoplamento máximo, deploy independente. Contras: Complexidade operacional, latência entre serviços.
- **Opção C:** Híbrido (Core + Módulos) — Prós: Balanceia simplicidade e flexibilidade, permite evolução gradual. Contras: Gerenciamento de comunicação entre serviços.

**Opção escolhida:** C — Justificativa: Permite refatoração incremental (Modo Hive), mantém estabilidade do Core enquanto módulos evoluem independentemente.

**CONSEQUÊNCIAS:**
**Positivas:** 
- Deploy independente por módulo
- Escalabilidade seletiva
- Equipes podem trabalhar em paralelo
- Tecnologias diferentes por módulo

**Negativas:**
- Complexidade de comunicação entre serviços
- Necessidade de orquestração
- Monitoramento distribuído

**Riscos:**
- Latência entre serviços → Mitigar com cache local e conexões persistentes
- Falha em cascata → Implementar circuit breakers e retry policies
- Consistência de dados → Usar eventos assíncronos com idempotência

**REVISÃO:** 2024-04-15

---

## Engineering Standards V10

### 1. Estrutura de Repositório
```
diyapp-v10/
├── core/                    # Core monolítico
│   ├── src/
│   │   ├── auth/           # Autenticação JWT
│   │   ├── config/         # Configuração central
│   │   ├── database/       # Models e migrations
│   │   ├── events/         # Event bus
│   │   ├── middleware/     # Middleware comum
│   │   └── utils/          # Utilitários compartilhados
│   ├── tests/
│   └── package.json
├── modules/                 # Módulos como microserviços
│   ├── whatsapp/
│   ├── email/
│   ├── sms/
│   ├── dashboard/
│   └── analytics/
├── gateway/                 # API Gateway
├── docker-compose.yml
├── .github/workflows/      # CI/CD
├── docs/                   # Documentação
├── scripts/                # Scripts de deploy
└── README.md
```

### 2. Padrões de Código
```javascript
// Nomenclatura
const PascalCase = 'Classes, Interfaces, Types';
const camelCase = 'variáveis, funções, métodos';
const UPPER_SNAKE_CASE = 'Constantes';
const kebab-case = 'arquivos, pastas, rotas';

// Estrutura de arquivo
/**
 * @module NomeDoModulo
 * @description Descrição clara do propósito
 * @author Nome <email>
 * @version 1.0.0
 */

// Imports organizados
import externalLibs from 'external';
import internalModules from '../internal';
import utils from './utils';

// Exports nomeados sempre
export { ServiceClass, helperFunction };
export default MainClass;

// Error handling consistente
class AppError extends Error {
  constructor(message, code = 500) {
    super(message);
    this.code = code;
    this.timestamp = new Date().toISOString();
  }
}
```

### 3. Contratos de API
```yaml
# OpenAPI 3.0 Specification
openapi: 3.0.0
info:
  title: DIYAPP V10 API
  version: 1.0.0
  description: API contratos entre módulos

paths:
  /api/v1/messages:
    post:
      summary: Enviar mensagem
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/MessageRequest'
      responses:
        '202':
          description: Mensagem aceita para processamento
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/MessageResponse'
        '400':
          $ref: '#/components/responses/BadRequest'

components:
  schemas:
    MessageRequest:
      type: object
      required:
        - channel
        - recipient
        - content
      properties:
        channel:
          type: string
          enum: [whatsapp, email, sms]
        recipient:
          type: string
        content:
          type: string
        metadata:
          type: object

    MessageResponse:
      type: object
      properties:
        messageId:
          type: string
        status:
          type: string
        estimatedDelivery:
          type: string
          format: date-time
```

### 4. Protocolo de Comunicação entre Módulos
```javascript
// Event Bus Pattern
class EventBus {
  constructor() {
    this.subscribers = new Map();
  }

  publish(event, data) {
    const handlers = this.subscribers.get(event) || [];
    handlers.forEach(handler => {
      try {
        handler(data);
      } catch (error) {
        console.error(`Error in event handler for ${event}:`, error);
      }
    });
  }

  subscribe(event, handler) {
    if (!this.subscribers.has(event)) {
      this.subscribers.set(event, []);
    }
    this.subscribers.get(event).push(handler);
  }
}

// Eventos padrão
const EVENTS = {
  MESSAGE_CREATED: 'message.created',
  MESSAGE_SENT: 'message.sent',
  MESSAGE_FAILED: 'message.failed',
  USER_CREATED: 'user.created',
  MODULE_HEALTH_CHANGE: 'module.health.change'
};
```

## Stack Tecnológica V10

### Core Stack
```json
{
  "runtime": "Node.js 18+",
  "framework": "Express.js + TypeScript",
  "database": "PostgreSQL 14 + Redis 7",
  "orm": "Prisma 5",
  "validation": "Zod",
  "logging": "Winston + Elasticsearch",
  "monitoring": "Prometheus + Grafana",
  "message_queue": "RabbitMQ",
  "container": "Docker + Docker Compose",
  "orchestration": "Kubernetes (future)"
}
```

### Módulos Específicos
- **WhatsApp:** Baileys + Socket.IO
- **Email:** Nodemailer + Handlebars templates
- **SMS:** Twilio SDK
- **Dashboard:** React 18 + Vite + TailwindCSS
- **Analytics:** ClickHouse + Apache Superset

mkdir -p diyapp-v10/{core/src/{auth,config,database,events,middleware,utils},modules/{whatsapp,email,sms,dashboard,analytics},gateway,docs,scripts,.github/workflows}
```

### 3. Core - src/index.ts (Ponto de Entrada)
```typescript
import express from 'express';
import cors from 'cors';
import helmet from 'helmet';
import compression from 'compression';
import { config } from './config';
import { logger } from './utils/logger';
import { errorHandler } from './middleware/errorHandler';
import { requestLogger } from './middleware/requestLogger';
import { metricsMiddleware } from './middleware/metrics';
import authRoutes from './auth/routes';
import healthRoutes from './health/routes';
import { EventBus } from './events/eventBus';
import { connectDatabase } from './database';
import { connectRedis } from './utils/redis';
import { connectRabbitMQ } from './events/rabbitmq';

class CoreServer {
  private app: express.Application;
  private eventBus: EventBus;

  constructor() {
    this.app = express();
    this.eventBus = new EventBus();
    this.initializeMiddlewares();
    this.initializeRoutes();
    this.initializeErrorHandling();
    this.initializeEventBus();
  }

  private initializeMiddlewares(): void {
    this.app.use(helmet());
    this.app.use(cors(config.cors));
    this.app.use(compression());
    this.app.use(express.json({ limit: '10mb' }));
    this.app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true }));
    this.app.use(requestLogger);
    this.app.use(metricsMiddleware);
  }

  private initializeRoutes(): void {
    this.app.use('/api/v1/auth', authRoutes);
    this.app.use('/health', healthRoutes);
    
    // Dashboard interface - Ponto de entrada obrigatório
    this.app.use(express.static('public'));
    this.app.get('/', (req, res) => {
      res.sendFile('index.html', { root: 'public' });
    });
  }

  private initializeErrorHandling(): void {
    this.app.use(errorHandler);
  }

  private async initializeEventBus(): Promise<void> {
    // Conectar ao RabbitMQ para comunicação entre módulos
    await connectRabbitMQ(this.eventBus);
    
    // Subscriber padrão para eventos do sistema
    this.eventBus.subscribe('module.registered', (data) => {
      logger.info(`Módulo registrado: ${data.moduleName}`, { data });
    });
  }

  public async start(): Promise<void> {
    try {
      // Conectar dependências
      await connectDatabase();
      await connectRedis();
      
      // Iniciar servidor
      this.app.listen(config.port, () => {
        logger.info(`Core Server running on port ${config.port}`);
        logger.info(`Environment: ${config.nodeEnv}`);
        logger.info(`Dashboard: http://localhost:${config.port}`);
        
        // Publicar evento de inicialização
        this.eventBus.publish('core.started', {
          timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
          version: config.version
        });
      });
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Failed to start Core Server:', error);
      process.exit(1);
    }
  }
}

// Inicialização
const server = new CoreServer();
server.start().catch((error) => {
  logger.error('Unhandled error during startup:', error);
  process.exit(1);
});

// Graceful shutdown
process.on('SIGTERM', () => {
  logger.info('SIGTERM received, shutting down gracefully');
  process.exit(0);
});

process.on('SIGINT', () => {
  logger.info('SIGINT received, shutting down gracefully');
  process.exit(0);
});
```

Vou criar um sistema de design completo com tokens, wireframes de alta fidelidade para todas as views principais e um protótipo interativo com foco em UX Premium.

## 2. Configuração Principal

### src/config/index.js
```javascript
const path = require('path');
require('dotenv').config({ path: path.join(__dirname, '../../.env') });

const config = {
  env: process.env.NODE_ENV || 'development',
  port: parseInt(process.env.PORT, 10) || 3000,
  apiVersion: process.env.API_VERSION || 'v1',
  
  database: {
    host: process.env.DB_HOST || 'localhost',
    port: parseInt(process.env.DB_PORT, 10) || 5432,
    name: process.env.DB_NAME || 'diyapp_v10',
    user: process.env.DB_USER || 'diyapp_user',
    password: process.env.DB_PASSWORD || '',
    dialect: 'postgres',
    logging: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'development' ? console.log : false,
    pool: {
      max: 10,
      min: 0,
      acquire: 30000,
      idle: 10000
    }
  },
  
  redis: {
    host: process.env.REDIS_HOST || 'localhost',
    port: parseInt(process.env.REDIS_PORT, 10) || 6379,
    password: process.env.REDIS_PASSWORD || null,
    maxRetriesPerRequest: 3,
    enableReadyCheck: false
  },
  
  jwt: {
    secret: process.env.JWT_SECRET || 'default_secret_change_in_production',
    expiresIn: process.env.JWT_EXPIRES_IN || '24h'
  },
  
  rateLimit: {
    windowMs: parseInt(process.env.RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS, 10) || 900000,
    max: parseInt(process.env.RATE_LIMIT_MAX_REQUESTS, 10) || 100
  },
  
  externalServices: {
    timeout: parseInt(process.env.EXTERNAL_SERVICE_TIMEOUT, 10) || 5000,
    retryAttempts: parseInt(process.env.EXTERNAL_SERVICE_RETRY_ATTEMPTS, 10) || 3
  },
  
  logging: {
    level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
    maxSize: process.env.LOG_FILE_MAX_SIZE || '10m',
    maxFiles: process.env.LOG_FILE_MAX_FILES || '14d'
  }
};

// Validation
if (!config.jwt.secret || config.jwt.secret === 'default_secret_change_in_production') {
  console.warn('WARNING: JWT_SECRET is using default value. Change in production!');
}

module.exports = config;
```

## 3. Utilitários Essenciais

### src/utils/logger.js
```javascript
const winston = require('winston');
const DailyRotateFile = require('winston-daily-rotate-file');
const config = require('../config');

const { combine, timestamp, json, errors, metadata } = winston.format;

// Custom format for masking sensitive data
const maskSensitiveData = winston.format((info) => {
  const maskedInfo = { ...info };
  
  // Mask sensitive fields
  const sensitiveFields = ['password', 'token', 'authorization', 'email', 'cpf', 'credit_card', 'card_number'];
  
  if (maskedInfo.metadata && maskedInfo.metadata.body) {
    sensitiveFields.forEach(field => {
      if (maskedInfo.metadata.body[field]) {
        maskedInfo.metadata.body[field] = '***MASKED***';
      }
    });
  }
  
  return maskedInfo;
});

const logger = winston.createLogger({
  level: config.logging.level,
  format: combine(
    errors({ stack: true }),
    timestamp(),
    maskSensitiveData(),
    metadata({ fillExcept: ['message', 'level', 'timestamp', 'label'] }),
    json()
  ),
  defaultMeta: { service: 'diyapp-v10-core' },
  transports: [
    new winston.transports.Console({
      format: winston.format.combine(
        winston.format.colorize(),
        winston.format.simple()
      )
    }),
    new DailyRotateFile({
      filename: 'logs/application-%DATE%.log',
      datePattern: 'YYYY-MM-DD',
      maxSize: config.logging.maxSize,
      maxFiles: config.logging.maxFiles
    }),
    new DailyRotateFile({
      filename: 'logs/error-%DATE%.log',
      datePattern: 'YYYY-MM-DD',
      level: 'error',
      maxSize: config.logging.maxSize,
      maxFiles: config.logging.maxFiles
    })
  ]
});

// Correlation ID middleware
const correlationIdMiddleware = (req, res, next) => {
  const correlationId = req.headers['x-correlation-id'] || require('uuid').v4();
  req.correlationId = correlationId;
  res.setHeader('x-correlation-id', correlationId);
  next();
};

// Request logger middleware
const requestLoggerMiddleware = (req, res, next) => {
  const start = Date.now();
  
  res.on('finish', () => {
    const duration = Date.now() - start;
    
    logger.info('HTTP Request', {
      correlation_id: req.correlationId,
      user_id: req.user?.id || 'anonymous',
      method: req.method,
      endpoint: req.originalUrl,
      status_code: res.statusCode,
      duration_ms: duration,
      user_agent: req.get('user-agent'),
      ip: req.ip
    });
  });
  
  next();
};

module.exports = {
  logger,
  correlationIdMiddleware,
  requestLoggerMiddleware
};
```

### src/utils/security.js
```javascript
const bcrypt = require('bcrypt');
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const config = require('../config');

class SecurityUtils {
  /**
   * Hash a password
   * @param {string} password - Plain text password
   * @returns {Promise<string>} Hashed password
   */
  static async hashPassword(password) {
    const saltRounds = 10;
    return bcrypt.hash(password, saltRounds);
  }

  /**
   * Compare password with hash
   * @param {string} password - Plain text password
   * @param {string} hash - Hashed password
   * @returns {Promise<boolean>} True if matches
   */
  static async comparePassword(password, hash) {
    return bcrypt.compare(password, hash);
  }

  /**
   * Generate JWT token
   * @param {object} payload - Token payload
   * @returns {string} JWT token
   */
  static generateToken(payload) {
    return jwt.sign(payload, config.jwt.secret, {
      expiresIn: config.jwt.expiresIn
    });
  }

  /**
   * Verify JWT token
   * @param {string} token - JWT token
   * @returns {object} Decoded payload
   */
  static verifyToken(token) {
    return jwt.verify(token, config.jwt.secret);
  }

  /**
   * Mask sensitive data for logs
   * @param {object} data - Data object
   * @returns {object} Masked data
   */
  static maskSensitiveData(data) {
    if (!data || typeof data !== 'object') return data;
    
    const masked = { ...data };
    const sensitiveFields = [
      'password', 'token', 'refreshToken', 'authorization',
      'email', 'cpf', 'creditCard', 'cardNumber', 'cvv',
      'phone', 'address', 'ssn'
    ];
    
    sensitiveFields.forEach(field => {
      if (masked[field]) {
        masked[field] = '***MASKED***';
      }
    });
    
    return masked;
  }

  /**
   * Generate secure random string
   * @param {number} length - Length of string
   * @returns {string} Random string
   */
  static generateSecureRandom(length = 32) {
    return require('crypto').randomBytes(length).toString('hex');
  }
}

module.exports = SecurityUtils;
```

## 4. Circuit Breaker Pattern

### src/utils/circuitBreaker.js
```javascript
const CircuitBreaker = require('circuit-breaker-js');
const logger = require('./logger').logger;

class ServiceCircuitBreaker {
  constructor(serviceName, options = {}) {
    this.serviceName = serviceName;
    
    this.breaker = new CircuitBreaker({
      windowDuration: options.windowDuration || 10000,
      numBuckets: options.numBuckets || 10,
      timeoutDuration: options.timeoutDuration || 5000,
      errorThreshold: options.errorThreshold || 50,
      volumeThreshold: options.volumeThreshold || 5,
      
      onCircuitOpen: (metrics) => {
        logger.error('Circuit breaker opened', {
          service: serviceName,
          metrics: {
            total: metrics.total,
            errorCount: metrics.errorCount,
            errorPercentage: metrics.errorPercentage
          }
        });
      },
      
      onCircuitClose: () => {
        logger.info('Circuit breaker closed', { service: serviceName });
      }
    });
  }

  /**
   * Execute function with circuit breaker protection
   * @param {Function} fn - Function to execute
   * @param {Array} args - Arguments for function
   * @returns {Promise<any>} Function result
   */
  async execute(fn, ...args) {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      this.breaker.run((success, fail) => {
        fn(...args)
          .then((result) => {
            success();
            resolve(result);
          })
          .catch((error) => {
            fail();
            reject(error);
          });
      }, () => {
        // Fallback function when circuit is open
        const error = new Error(`Service ${this.serviceName} is unavailable (circuit open)`);
        error.code = 'SERVICE_UNAVAILABLE';
        error.status = 503;
        reject(error);
      });
    });
  }

  /**
   * Get circuit breaker state
   * @returns {object} Current state
   */
  getState() {
    return {
      service: this.serviceName,
      isOpen: this.breaker.isOpen(),
      metrics: this.breaker.metrics
    };
  }
}

// Pre-configured circuit breakers for external services
const circuitBreakers = {
  emailService: new ServiceCircuitBreaker('email-service', {
    timeoutDuration: 10000,
    errorThreshold: 30
  }),
  
  paymentService: new ServiceCircuitBreaker('payment-service', {
    timeoutDuration: 15000,
    errorThreshold: 20
  }),
  
  notificationService: new ServiceCircuitBreaker('notification-service', {
    timeoutDuration: 8000,
    errorThreshold: 40
  })
};

module.exports = {
  ServiceCircuitBreaker,
  circuitBreakers
};
```

## 5. Modelos de Dados

### src/core/models/index.js
```javascript
const { Sequelize, DataTypes } = require('sequelize');
const config = require('../../config');

const sequelize = new Sequelize(
  config.database.name,
  config.database.user,
  config.database.password,
  {
    host: config.database.host,
    port: config.database.port,
    dialect: config.database.dialect,
    logging: config.database.logging,
    pool: config.database.pool
  }
);

// User Model
const User = sequelize.define('User', {
  id: {
    type: DataTypes.UUID,
    defaultValue: DataTypes.UUIDV4,
    primaryKey: true
  },
  email: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: false,
    unique: true,
    validate: {
      isEmail: true
    }
  },
  username: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: false,
    unique: true
  },
  password_hash: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: false
  },
  first_name: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: true
  },
  last_name: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: true
  },
  avatar_url: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: true
  },
  is_active: {
    type: DataTypes.BOOLEAN,
    defaultValue: true
  },
  is_verified: {
    type: DataTypes.BOOLEAN,
    defaultValue: false
  },
  last_login_at: {
    type: DataTypes.DATE,
    allowNull: true
  },
  preferences: {
    type: DataTypes.JSONB,
    defaultValue: {}
  },
  metadata: {
    type: DataTypes.JSONB,
    defaultValue: {}
  }
}, {
  tableName: 'users',
  timestamps: true,
  underscored: true,
  indexes: [
    { fields: ['email'] },
    { fields: ['username'] },
    { fields: ['created_at'] }
  ]
});

// Project Model
const Project = sequelize.define('Project', {
  id: {
    type: DataTypes.UUID,
    defaultValue: DataTypes.UUIDV4,
    primaryKey: true
  },
  user_id: {
    type: DataTypes.UUID,
    allowNull: false,
    references: {
      model: 'users',
      key: 'id'
    }
  },
  title: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: false
  },
  description: {
    type:

    },
    warning: {
      500: '#f59e0b',
      600: '#d97706',
    },
  },
  spacing: {
    0: '0',
    1: '0.25rem',
    2: '0.5rem',
    3: '0.75rem',
    4: '1rem',
    6: '1.5rem',
    8: '2rem',
    12: '3rem',
    16: '4rem',
  },
  typography: {
    fontFamily: {
      sans: 'system-ui, -apple-system, sans-serif',
      mono: 'monospace',
    },
    fontSize: {
      xs: '0.75rem',
      sm: '0.875rem',
      base: '1rem',
      lg: '1.125rem',
      xl: '1.25rem',
      '2xl': '1.5rem',
      '3xl': '1.875rem',
    },
    fontWeight: {
      normal: '400',
      medium: '500',
      semibold: '600',
      bold: '700',
    },
  },
  borderRadius: {
    sm: '0.25rem',
    md: '0.375rem',
    lg: '0.5rem',
    xl: '0.75rem',
    full: '9999px',
  },
  shadows: {
    sm: '0 1px 2px 0 rgb(0 0 0 / 0.05)',
    md: '0 4px 6px -1px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1)',
    lg: '0 10px 15px -3px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1)',
  },
} as const;

export type ColorToken = keyof typeof tokens.colors;
export type SpacingToken = keyof typeof tokens.spacing;
```

```typescript
// src/design-system/Button.tsx
import React from 'react';
import { tokens } from './tokens';

export type ButtonVariant = 'primary' | 'secondary' | 'outline' | 'ghost';
export type ButtonSize = 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg';

export interface ButtonProps extends React.ButtonHTMLAttributes<HTMLButtonElement> {
  variant?: ButtonVariant;
  size?: ButtonSize;
  isLoading?: boolean;
  leftIcon?: React.ReactNode;
  rightIcon?: React.ReactNode;
  children: React.ReactNode;
}

const variantStyles: Record<ButtonVariant, string> = {
  primary: `bg-${tokens.colors.primary[500]} text-white hover:bg-${tokens.colors.primary[600]} focus:ring-2 focus:ring-${tokens.colors.primary[500]} focus:ring-offset-2`,
  secondary: `bg-${tokens.colors.neutral[200]} text-${tokens.colors.neutral[800]} hover:bg-${tokens.colors.neutral[300]}`,
  outline: `border border-${tokens.colors.neutral[300]} bg-transparent text-${tokens.colors.neutral[700]} hover:bg-${tokens.colors.neutral[50]}`,
  ghost: `bg-transparent text-${tokens.colors.neutral[700]} hover:bg-${tokens.colors.neutral[100]}`,
};

const sizeStyles: Record<ButtonSize, string> = {
  sm: `px-${tokens.spacing[3]} py-${tokens.spacing[1]} text-${tokens.typography.fontSize.sm}`,
  md: `px-${tokens.spacing[4]} py-${tokens.spacing[2]} text-${tokens.typography.fontSize.base}`,
  lg: `px-${tokens.spacing[6]} py-${tokens.spacing[3]} text-${tokens.typography.fontSize.lg}`,
};

export const Button: React.FC<ButtonProps> = ({
  variant = 'primary',
  size = 'md',
  isLoading = false,
  leftIcon,
  rightIcon,
  children,
  disabled,
  className = '',
  ...props
}) => {
  const baseStyles = `inline-flex items-center justify-center font-${tokens.typography.fontWeight.medium} rounded-${tokens.borderRadius.md} transition-colors duration-200 focus:outline-none disabled:opacity-50 disabled:cursor-not-allowed`;
  
  return (
    <button
      className={`${baseStyles} ${variantStyles[variant]} ${sizeStyles[size]} ${className}`}
      disabled={disabled || isLoading}
      aria-busy={isLoading}
      {...props}
    >
      {isLoading && (
        <svg className="animate-spin -ml-1 mr-2 h-4 w-4" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
          <circle className="opacity-25" cx="12" cy="12" r="10" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="4" />
          <path className="opacity-75" fill="currentColor" d="M4 12a8 8 0 018-8V0C5.373 0 0 5.373 0 12h4zm2 5.291A7.962 7.962 0 014 12H0c0 3.042 1.135 5.824 3 7.938l3-2.647z" />
        </svg>
      )}
      {!isLoading && leftIcon && <span className="mr-2">{leftIcon}</span>}
      {children}
      {!isLoading && rightIcon && <span className="ml-2">{rightIcon}</span>}
    </button>
  );
};
```

```typescript
// src/design-system/Card.tsx
import React from 'react';
import { tokens } from './tokens';

export interface CardProps {
  title?: string;
  subtitle?: string;
  children: React.ReactNode;
  footer?: React.ReactNode;
  className?: string;
  hoverable?: boolean;
}

export const Card: React.FC<CardProps> = ({
  title,
  subtitle,
  children,
  footer,
  className = '',
  hoverable = false,
}) => {
  return (
    <div
      className={`bg-white rounded-${tokens.borderRadius.lg} shadow-${tokens.shadows.md} border border-${tokens.colors.neutral[200]} ${hoverable ? 'hover:shadow-lg transition-shadow duration-200' : ''} ${className}`}
      role="region"
      aria-labelledby={title ? 'card-title' : undefined}
    >
      {(title || subtitle) && (
        <div className={`px-${tokens.spacing[6]} pt-${tokens.spacing[6]} pb-${tokens.spacing[4]}`}>
          {title && (
            <h3
              id="card-title"
              className={`text-${tokens.typography.fontSize.lg} font-${tokens.typography.fontWeight.semibold} text-${tokens.colors.neutral[900]}`}
            >
              {title}
            </h3>
          )}
          {subtitle && (
            <p className={`mt-${tokens.spacing[1]} text-${tokens.typography.fontSize.sm} text-${tokens.colors.neutral[600]}`}>
              {subtitle}
            </p>
          )}
        </div>
      )}
      <div className={`px-${tokens.spacing[6]} ${!footer ? `pb-${tokens.spacing[6]}` : ''}`}>
        {children}
      </div>
      {footer && (
        <div className={`px-${tokens.spacing[6]} py-${tokens.spacing[4]} bg-${tokens.colors.neutral[50]} rounded-b-${tokens.borderRadius.lg} border-t border-${tokens.colors.neutral[200]}`}>
          {footer}
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};
```

```typescript
// src/design-system/Input.tsx
import React, { forwardRef } from 'react';
import { tokens } from './tokens';

export interface InputProps extends React.InputHTMLAttributes<HTMLInputElement> {
  label?: string;
  error?: string;
  helperText?: string;
  leftIcon?: React.ReactNode;
  rightIcon?: React.ReactNode;
}

export const Input = forwardRef<HTMLInputElement, InputProps>(
  ({ label, error, helperText, leftIcon, rightIcon, className = '', disabled, ...props }, ref) => {
    const hasError = !!error;
    
    return (
      <div className="w-full">
        {label && (
          <label
            htmlFor={props.id}
            className={`block text-${tokens.typography.fontSize.sm} font-${tokens.typography.fontWeight.medium} text-${tokens.colors.neutral[700]} mb-${tokens.spacing[2]}`}
          >
            {label}
          </label>
        )}
        <div className="relative">
          {leftIcon && (
            <div className="absolute inset-y-0 left-0 pl-3 flex items-center pointer-events-none">
              <span className={`text-${tokens.colors.neutral[400]}`}>{leftIcon}</span>
            </div>
          )}
          <input
            ref={ref}
            className={`
              w-full rounded-${tokens.borderRadius.md} border
              ${hasError 
                ? `border-${tokens.colors.error[500]} focus:border-${tokens.colors.error[500]} focus:ring-${tokens.colors.error[500]}`
                : `border-${tokens.colors.neutral[300]} focus:border-${tokens.colors.primary[500]} focus:ring-${tokens.colors.primary[500]}`
              }
              ${disabled ? `bg-${tokens.colors.neutral[100]} text-${tokens.colors.neutral[500]}` : `bg-white text-${tokens.colors.neutral[900]}`}
              shadow-sm focus:ring-2 focus:ring-opacity-50 focus:outline-none
              ${leftIcon ? `pl-10` : `pl-${tokens.spacing[4]}`}
              ${rightIcon ? `pr-10` : `pr-${tokens.spacing[4]}`}
              py-${tokens.spacing[2]}
              ${className}
            `}
            disabled={disabled}
            aria-invalid={hasError}
            aria-describedby={error ? `${props.id}-error` : helperText ? `${props.id}-helper` : undefined}
            {...props}
          />
          {rightIcon && (
            <div className="absolute inset-y-0 right-0 pr-3 flex items-center pointer-events-none">
              <span className={`text-${tokens.colors.neutral[400]}`}>{rightIcon}</span>
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
        {error && (
          <p
            id={`${props.id}-error`}
            className={`mt-${tokens.spacing[1]} text-${tokens.typography.fontSize.sm} text-${tokens.colors.error[600]}`}
            role="alert"
          >
            {error}
          </p>
        )}
        {helperText && !error && (
          <p
            id={`${props.id}-helper`}
            className={`mt-${tokens.spacing[1]} text-${tokens.typography.fontSize.sm} text-${tokens.colors.neutral[500]}`}
          >
            {helperText}
          </p>
        )}
      </div>
    );
  }
);

Input.displayName = 'Input';
```

```typescript
// src/store/index.ts
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { persist } from 'zustand/middleware';

export interface User {
  id: string;
  email: string;
  name: string;
  avatar?: string;
}

export interface AppState {
  user: User | null;
  isAuthenticated: boolean;
  theme: 'light' | 'dark';
  notifications: Array<{
    id: string;
    title: string;
    message: string;
    type: 'info' | 'success' | 'warning' | 'error';
    read: boolean;
    createdAt: Date;
  }>;
  
  // Actions
  setUser: (user: User | null) => void;
  setTheme: (theme: 'light' | 'dark') => void;
  addNotification: (notification: Omit<AppState['notifications'][0], 'id' | 'createdAt' | 'read'>) => void;
  markNotificationAsRead: (id: string) => void;
  clearNotifications: () => void;
  logout: () => void;
}

export const useStore = create<AppState>()(
  persist(
    (set) => ({
      user: null,
      isAuthenticated: false,
      theme: 'light',
      notifications: [],

      setUser: (user) => set({ 
        user, 
        isAuthenticated: !!user 
      }),

      setTheme: (theme) => set({ theme }),

      addNotification: (notification) => 
        set((state) => ({
          notifications: [
            {
              ...notification,
              id: Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9),
              createdAt: new Date(),
              read: false,
            },
            ...state.notifications,
          ].slice(0, 50), // Keep only last 50 notifications
        })),

      markNotificationAsRead: (id) =>
        set((state) => ({
          notifications: state.notifications.map((n) =>
            n.id === id ? { ...n, read: true } : n
          ),
        })),

      clearNotifications: () => set({ notifications: [] }),

      logout: () => set({ 
        user: null, 
        isAuthenticated: false,
        notifications: [],
      }),
    }),
    {
      name: 'diyapp-storage',
      partialize: (state) => ({
        user: state.user,
        theme: state.theme,
      }),
    }
  )
);
```

```typescript
// src/services/api.ts
import { User } from '../store';

// Mock API responses
const mockUsers: User[] = [
  { id: '1', email: 'admin@diyapp.com', name: 'Admin User', avatar: 'https://i.pravatar.cc/150?img=1' },
  { id: '2', email: 'user@diyapp.com', name: 'Regular User', avatar: 'https://i.pravatar.cc/150?img=2' },
];

const mockProjects = [
  { id: '1', name: 'Dashboard Redesign', status: 'in-progress', progress: 75 },
  { id: '2', name: 'API Integration', status: 'completed', progress: 100 },
  { id: '3', name: 'Mobile App', status: 'pending', progress: 0 },
];

export class ApiService {
  private static delay = (ms: number) => new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, ms));

  static async login(email: string, password: string): Promise<{ user: User; token: string }> {
    await this.delay(800); // Simulate network delay
    
    const user = mockUsers.find(u => u.email === email);
    
    if (!user || password !== 'password') {
      throw new Error('Invalid credentials');
    }

    return {
      user,
      token: 'mock-jwt-token-' + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2),
    };
  }

  static async getProjects() {
    await this.delay(500);
    return mockProjects;
  }

  static async updateProject(id: string, data: Partial<typeof mockProjects[0]>) {
    await this.delay(300);
    const project = mockProjects.find(p => p.id === id);
    if (!project) throw new Error('Project not found');
    
    Object.assign(project, data);
    return project;
  }

  static async uploadFile(file: File) {
    await this.delay(1000);
    return {
      id: Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9),
      url: URL.createObjectURL(file),
      name: file.name,
      size: file.size,
      type: file.type,
    };
  }

  static async getAnalytics() {
    await this.delay(700);
    return {
      totalUsers: 1245,
      activeProjects: 23,
      completionRate: 68,
      revenue: 45230,
    };
  }
}
```

```typescript
// src/routes/index.tsx
import React from 'react';
import { BrowserRouter, Routes, Route, Navigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import { useStore } from '../store';
import { Dashboard } from '../pages/Dashboard';
import { Login } from '../pages/Login';
import { Projects } from '../pages/Projects';
import { Settings } from '../pages/Settings';
import { Layout } from '../components/Layout';

const PrivateRoute: React.FC<{ children: React.ReactNode }> = ({ children }) => {
  const { isAuthenticated } = useStore();
  return isAuthenticated ? <>{children}</> : <Navigate to="/login" />;
};

const PublicRoute: React.FC<{ children: React.ReactNode }> = ({ children }) => {
  const { isAuthenticated } = useStore();
  return !isAuthenticated ? <>{children}</> : <Navigate to="/dashboard" />;
};

                        </div>

                            <div class="agent-icon">⚙️</div>
                            <div class="agent-info">
                                <h3>Background Tasks</h3>
                                <p>Status: <span class="agent-status" id="agent-bg-status">Inativo</span></p>
                                <p>Tarefas: <span id="agent-bg-tasks">0</span></p>
                            </div>
                            <button class="agent-toggle" onclick="toggleAgent('bg')" id="toggle-bg">Iniciar</button>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>

            <!-- Seção 6: Recomendações -->
            <div class="card recommendations-card">
                <h2>📋 Recomendações AI Ops</h2>
                <div class="card-content">
                    <ul class="recommendations-list" id="recommendations-list">
                        <li>Configure os modelos de IA para começar o monitoramento</li>
                        <li>Execute o golden dataset para estabelecer baseline</li>
                        <li>Configure alertas para os provedores de LLM</li>
                    </ul>
                    <div class="action-buttons">
                        <button onclick="runGoldenDataset()" class="btn-primary">Executar Golden Dataset</button>
                        <button onclick="generateWeeklyReport()" class="btn-secondary">Gerar Relatório Semanal</button>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>

        <footer class="dashboard-footer">
            <p>DIYAPP V10 Core - AI Ops Monitor | Última atualização: <span id="current-time"></span></p>
            <p class="footer-links">
                <a href="#" onclick="showConfig()">Configurações</a> |
                <a href="#" onclick="showLogs()">Logs</a> |
                <a href="#" onclick="exportData()">Exportar Dados</a>
            </p>
        </footer>
    </div>

    <!-- Modal de Configuração -->
    <div id="config-modal" class="modal">
        <div class="modal-content">
            <span class="close" onclick="closeModal('config-modal')">&times;</span>
            <h2>Configurações AI Ops</h2>
            <div class="config-section">
                <h3>Limites de Alerta</h3>
                <div class="config-item">
                    <label>Aumento de custo semanal (%):</label>
                    <input type="number" id="alert-cost-threshold" value="20" min="1" max="100">
                </div>
                <div class="config-item">
                    <label>Degradação de qualidade (%):</label>
                    <input type="number" id="alert-quality-threshold" value="10" min="1" max="100">
                </div>
                <div class="config-item">
                    <label>Taxa de fallback (%):</label>
                    <input type="number" id="alert-fallback-threshold" value="5" min="1" max="100">
                </div>
            </div>
            <div class="config-section">
                <h3>Provedores de LLM</h3>
                <div class="config-item">
                    <label>Anthropic API Key:</label>
                    <input type="password" id="anthropic-key" placeholder="sk-ant-...">
                </div>
                <div class="config-item">

                    <input type="password" id="openai-key" placeholder="sk-...">
                </div>

        </div>
    </div>

    <script src="/js/dashboard.js"></script>
</body>
</html>
```
