### [Sessão Paralela: Backend]
```python
# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core
# Core Engine Implementation
# Dev Backend Senior

"""
Arquitetura do Core Engine:
1. Message Broker (Pub/Sub) para comunicação entre agentes
2. State Service para estado compartilhado
3. API REST/GraphQL para dashboard
4. Data Models para tarefas e histórico
5. Observabilidade completa
"""

import asyncio
import json
import logging
import time
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from enum import Enum
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional, Set, Tuple, Union
from uuid import uuid4

import aiohttp
from aiohttp import web
from dataclasses import dataclass, field
from pydantic import BaseModel, Field, validator
from redis.asyncio import Redis
from sqlalchemy import Column, DateTime, Integer, String, Text, Boolean, JSON
from sqlalchemy.ext.asyncio import AsyncSession, create_async_engine
from sqlalchemy.ext.declarative import declarative_base
from sqlalchemy.orm import sessionmaker
from contextlib import asynccontextmanager
from circuitbreaker import circuit
from prometheus_client import Counter, Histogram, Gauge, generate_latest
import structlog

# ============================================================================
# 1. CONFIGURAÇÃO E OBSERVABILIDADE
# ============================================================================

# Configuração de logging estruturado
structlog.configure(
    processors=[
        structlog.processors.TimeStamper(fmt="iso"),
        structlog.processors.JSONRenderer()
    ],
    context_class=dict,
    logger_factory=structlog.PrintLoggerFactory(),
    wrapper_class=structlog.BoundLogger,
    cache_logger_on_first_use=True,
)

logger = structlog.get_logger()

# Métricas Prometheus
REQUEST_LATENCY = Histogram(
    'http_request_duration_seconds',
    'HTTP request latency in seconds',
    ['method', 'endpoint', 'status']
)
REQUEST_COUNT = Counter(
    'http_requests_total',
    'Total HTTP requests',
    ['method', 'endpoint', 'status']
)
ACTIVE_AGENTS = Gauge('active_agents', 'Number of active agents')
MESSAGES_PROCESSED = Counter('messages_processed_total', 'Total messages processed')
STATE_UPDATES = Counter('state_updates_total', 'Total state updates')

# ============================================================================
# 2. MODELOS DE DADOS (Pydantic + SQLAlchemy)
# ============================================================================

Base = declarative_base()

class TaskStatus(str, Enum):
    PENDING = "pending"
    RUNNING = "running"
    COMPLETED = "completed"
    FAILED = "failed"
    CANCELLED = "cancelled"

class AgentType(str, Enum):
    WORKER = "worker"
    COORDINATOR = "coordinator"
    MONITOR = "monitor"
    LLM = "llm"
    FRONTEND = "frontend"

# SQLAlchemy Models
class TaskModel(Base):
    __tablename__ = "tasks"
    
    id = Column(String(36), primary_key=True)
    name = Column(String(255), nullable=False)
    description = Column(Text)
    status = Column(String(20), default=TaskStatus.PENDING.value)
    agent_type = Column(String(50))
    payload = Column(JSON)
    result = Column(JSON)
    created_at = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)
    updated_at = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow, onupdate=datetime.utcnow)
    started_at = Column(DateTime)
    completed_at = Column(DateTime)
    error_message = Column(Text)
    retry_count = Column(Integer, default=0)
    max_retries = Column(Integer, default=3)
    timeout_seconds = Column(Integer, default=300)
    parent_task_id = Column(String(36))
    dependencies = Column(JSON, default=list)

class AgentModel(Base):
    __tablename__ = "agents"
    
    id = Column(String(36), primary_key=True)
    agent_type = Column(String(50), nullable=False)
    status = Column(String(20), default="active")
    last_heartbeat = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)
    capabilities = Column(JSON, default=list)
    metadata = Column(JSON, default=dict)
    created_at = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)

class MessageModel(Base):
    __tablename__ = "messages"
    
    id = Column(String(36), primary_key=True)
    topic = Column(String(255), nullable=False, index=True)
    sender_id = Column(String(36))
    receiver_id = Column(String(36))
    message_type = Column(String(50))
    payload = Column(JSON)
    created_at = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow, index=True)
    processed_at = Column(DateTime)
    ttl_seconds = Column(Integer, default=3600)

# Pydantic Models para API
class TaskCreate(BaseModel):
    name: str = Field(..., min_length=1, max_length=255)
    description: Optional[str] = None
    agent_type: AgentType
    payload: Dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict)
    timeout_seconds: int = Field(default=300, ge=1, le=3600)
    max_retries: int = Field(default=3, ge=0, le=10)
    dependencies: List[str] = Field(default_factory=list)
    parent_task_id: Optional[str] = None

class TaskResponse(BaseModel):
    id: str
    name: str
    status: TaskStatus
    agent_type: AgentType
    created_at: datetime
    updated_at: datetime
    started_at: Optional[datetime] = None
    completed_at: Optional[datetime] = None
    error_message: Optional[str] = None
    retry_count: int = 0
    
    class Config:
        orm_mode = True

class Message(BaseModel):
    topic: str
    sender_id: Optional[str] = None
    receiver_id: Optional[str] = None
    message_type: str
    payload: Dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict)
    ttl_seconds: int = Field(default=3600, ge=1, le=86400)

class AgentRegister(BaseModel):
    agent_type: AgentType
    capabilities: List[str] = Field(default_factory=list)
    metadata: Dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict)

class StateUpdate(BaseModel):
    key: str
    value: Any
    ttl_seconds: Optional[int] = None

# ============================================================================
# 3. MESSAGE BROKER (Pub/Sub)
# ============================================================================

class MessageBroker:
    """Broker de mensagens Pub/Sub com persistência e observabilidade"""
    
    def __init__(self, redis_url: str = "redis://localhost:6379"):
        self.redis = None
        self.redis_url = redis_url
        self.subscriptions: Dict[str, Set[str]] = {}
        self.message_handlers: Dict[str, List[callable]] = {}
        
    async def initialize(self):
        """Inicializa conexão com Redis"""
        self.redis = Redis.from_url(self.redis_url, decode_responses=True)
        await self.redis.ping()
        logger.info("message_broker_initialized")
        
    @circuit(failure_threshold=5, recovery_timeout=30)
    async def publish(self, topic: str, message: Message) -> str:
        """Publica mensagem em um tópico"""
        start_time = time.time()
        message_id = str(uuid4())
        
        try:
            # Persiste mensagem
            message_data = {
                "id": message_id,
                "topic": topic,
                "sender_id": message.sender_id,
                "receiver_id": message.receiver_id,
                "message_type": message.message_type,
                "payload": message.payload,
                "created_at": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
                "ttl_seconds": message.ttl_seconds
            }
            
            # Redis Pub/Sub
            await self.redis.publish(topic, json.dumps(message_data))
            
            # Persistência em banco (async)
            asyncio.create_task(self._persist_message(message_data))
            
            # Notifica handlers locais
            await self._notify_local_handlers(topic, message_data)
            
            MESSAGES_PROCESSED.inc()
            latency = time.time() - start_time
            
            logger.info(
                "message_published",
                message_id=message_id,
                topic=topic,
                message_type=message.message_type,
                latency_ms=round(latency * 1000, 2)
            )
            
            return message_id
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(
                "message_publish_failed",
                topic=topic,
                error=str(e),
                exc_info=True
            )
            raise
    
    async def subscribe(self, topic: str, agent_id: str, callback: callable):
        """Inscreve um agente em um tópico"""
        if topic not in self.subscriptions:
            self.subscriptions[topic] = set()
            self.message_handlers[topic] = []
            
        self.subscriptions[topic].add(agent_id)
        self.message_handlers[topic].append(callback)
        
        logger.info("agent_subscribed", agent_id=agent_id, topic=topic)
        
    async def unsubscribe(self, topic: str, agent_id: str):
        """Remove inscrição de um agente"""
        if topic in self.subscriptions:
            self.subscriptions[topic].discard(agent_id)
            logger.info("agent_unsubscribed", agent_id=agent_id, topic=topic)
    
    async def _persist_message(self, message_data: Dict):
        """Persiste mensagem no banco de dados (background task)"""
        try:
            async with Database.get_session() as session:
                message = MessageModel(
                    id=message_data["id"],
                    topic=message_data["topic"],
                    sender_id=message_data["sender_id"],
                    receiver_id=message_data["receiver_id"],
                    message_type=message_data["message_type"],
                    payload=message_data["payload"],
                    created_at=datetime.fromisoformat(message_data["created_at"]),
                    ttl_seconds=message_data["ttl_seconds"]
                )
                session.add(message)
                await session.commit()
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error("message_persistence_failed", error=str(e))
    
    async def _notify_local_handlers(self, topic: str, message_data: Dict):
        """Notifica handlers locais assincronamente"""
        if topic in self.message_handlers:
            for handler in self.message_handlers[topic]:
                try:
                    asyncio.create_task(handler(message_data))
                except Exception as e:
                    logger.error("handler_notification_failed", error=str(e))

# ============================================================================
# 4. STATE SERVICE
# ============================================================================

class StateService:
    """Serviço de estado compartilhado com TTL e versionamento"""
    
    def __init__(self, redis_url: str = "redis://localhost:6379"):
        self.redis = None
        self.redis_url = redis_url
        
    async def initialize(self):
        """Inicializa conexão com Redis"""
        self.redis = Redis.from_url(self.redis_url, decode_responses=True)
        await self.redis.ping()
        logger.info("state_service_initialized")
    
    @circuit(failure_threshold=5, recovery_timeout=30)
    async def set_state(self, key: str, value: Any, ttl_seconds: Optional[int] = None) -> bool:
        """Define um valor no estado compartilhado"""
        start_time = time.time()
        
        try:
            state_data = {
                "value": value,
                "version": str(uuid4()),
                "updated_at": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
                "ttl_seconds": ttl_seconds
            }
            
            if ttl_seconds:
                await self.redis.setex(
                    f"state:{key}",
                    ttl_seconds,
                    json.dumps(state_data)
                )
            else:
                await self.redis.set(
                    f"state:{key}",
                    json.dumps(state_data)
                )
            
            # Publica atualização de estado
            broker = get_message_broker()
            await broker.publish(
                "state:updated",
                Message(
                    topic="state:updated",
                    message_type="state_update",
                    payload={"key": key, "value": value}
                )
            )
            
            STATE_UPDATES.inc()
            latency = time.time() - start_time
            
            logger.info(
                "state_updated",
                key=key,
                value_type=type(value).__name__,
                latency_ms=round(latency * 1000, 2)
            )
            
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(
                "state_update_failed",
                key=key,
                error=str(e)
            )
            return False
    
    @circuit(failure_threshold=5, recovery_timeout=30)
    async def get_state(self, key: str) -> Optional[Any]:
        """Obtém um valor do estado compartilhado"""
        try:
            data = await self.redis.get(f"state:{key}")
            if data:
                state_data = json.loads(data)
                return state_data["value"]
            return None
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error("state_get_failed", key=key, error=str(e))
            return None
    
    async def delete_state(self, key: str) -> bool:
        """Remove um valor do estado compartilhado"""
        try:
            result = await self.redis.delete(f"state:{key}")
            logger.info("state_deleted", key=key, success=bool(result))
            return bool(result)
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error("state_delete_failed", key=key, error=str(e))
            return False

# ============================================================================
# 5. DATABASE LAYER
# ============================================================================

class Database:
    """Camada de acesso a dados com connection pooling"""
    
    _engine = None
    _session_factory = None
    
    @classmethod
    async def initialize(cls, database_url: str = "sqlite+aiosqlite:///./diyaap.db"):
        """Inicializa conexão com banco de dados"""
        cls._engine = create_async_engine(
            database_url,
            echo=False,
            pool_size=10,
            max_overflow=20,
            pool_pre_ping=True
        )
        
        cls._session_factory = sessionmaker(
            cls._engine,
            class_=AsyncSession,
            expire_on_commit=False
        )
        
        # Cria tabelas
        async with cls._engine.begin() as conn:
            await conn.run_sync(Base.metadata.create_all)
        
        logger.info("database_initialized", url=database_url)
    
    @classmethod
    @asynccontextmanager
    async def get_session(cls):
        """Context manager para sessões de banco de dados"""
        if not cls._session_factory:
            raise RuntimeError("Database not initialized")
        
        session = cls._session_factory()
        try:
            yield session
            await session.commit()
        except Exception:
            await session.rollback()
            raise
        finally:
            await session.close()
    
    @classmethod
    async def execute_migration(cls, migration_sql: str, rollback_sql: str):
        """Executa migração com rollback seguro"""
        async with cls.get_session() as session:
            try:
                await session.execute(migration_sql)
                await session.commit()
                logger.info("migration_executed")
            except Exception as e:
                await session.execute(rollback_sql)
                await session.commit()
                logger.error("migration_failed", error=str(e))
                raise

# ============================================================================
# 6. TASK SERVICE
# ============================================================================

class TaskService:
    """Serviço de gerenciamento de tarefas"""
    
    @staticmethod
    async def create_task(task_data: TaskCreate) -> TaskResponse:
        """Cria uma nova tarefa"""
        async with Database.get_session() as session:
            task_id = str(uuid4())
            
            # Verifica dependências
            if task_data.dependencies:
                for dep_id in task_data.dependencies:
                    dep_task = await session.get(TaskModel, dep_id)
                    if not dep_task:
                        raise web.HTTPBadRequest(
                            text=json.dumps({
                                "error": "Dependency not found",
                                "dependency_id": dep_id
                            }),
                            content_type="application/json"
                        )
            
            task = TaskModel(
                id=task_id,
                name=task_data.name,
                description=task_data.description,
                agent_type=task_data.agent_type.value,
                payload=task_data.payload,
                timeout_seconds=task_data.timeout_seconds,
                max_retries=task_data.max_retries,
                dependencies=task_data.dependencies,
                parent_task_id=task_data.parent_task_id
            )
            
            session.add(task)
            await session.commit()
            
            # Publica evento de nova tarefa
            broker = get_message_broker()
            await broker.publish(
                f"tasks:{task_data.agent_type.value}",
                Message(
                    topic=f"tasks:{task_data.agent_type.value}",
                    message_type="new_task",
                    payload={"task_id": task_id, "task_name": task_data.name}
                )
            )
            
            logger.info("task_created", task_id=task_id, task_name=task_data.name)
            
            return TaskResponse.from_orm(task)
    
    @staticmethod
    async def get_task(task_id: str) -> Optional[TaskResponse]:
        """Obtém uma tarefa por ID"""
        async with Database.get_session() as session:
            task = await session.get(TaskModel, task_id)
            if task:
                return TaskResponse.from_orm(task)
            return None
    
    @staticmethod
    async def update_task_status(
        task_id: str,
        status: TaskStatus,
        result: Optional[Dict] = None,
        error_message: Optional[str] = None
    ) -> bool:
        """Atualiza status de uma tarefa"""
        async with Database.get_session() as session:
            task = await session.get(TaskModel, task_id)
            if not task:
                return False
            
            task.status = status.value
            task.updated_at = datetime.utcnow()
            
            if status == TaskStatus.RUNNING and not task.started_at:

            className = '',

            const trendConfig = {
                up: { color: 'text-success-600', icon: '↗' },

        const LogEntry = ({ timestamp, level, message, agent, ...props }) => {
            const levelColors = {
                info: 'text-info-600 bg-info-50',
                warning: 'text-warning-600 bg-warning-50',
                error: 'text-error-600 bg-error-50',
                success: 'text-success-600 bg-success-50',
                debug: 'text-gray-600 bg-gray-50'
            };
            
            const formatTime = (date) => {
                return new Date(date).toLocaleTimeString('pt-BR', {
                    hour: '2-digit',
                    minute: '2-digit',
                    second: '2-digit'
                });
            };
            
            return (
                <div className="border-b border-gray-100 last:border-0 py-3 px-4 hover:bg-gray-50 transition-colors" {...props}>
                    <div className="flex items-start justify-between mb-1">
                        <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                            <Badge variant={level === 'error' ? 'error' : level === 'warning' ? 'warning' : 'info'}>
                                {level.toUpperCase()}
                            </Badge>
                            <span className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">{agent}</span>
                        </div>
                        <span className="text-xs text-gray-500 font-mono">
                            {formatTime(timestamp)}
                        </span>
                    </div>
                    <p className="text-sm text-gray-700 font-mono">{message}</p>
                </div>
            );
        };
        
        // Main Dashboard Component
        const Dashboard = () => {
            const [agents, setAgents] = useState([]);
            const [logs, setLogs] = useState([]);
            const [metrics, setMetrics] = useState({});

                { id: 'agent-4', name: 'QA Engineer', status: 'online', cpu: 32, memory: 55, lastActive: new Date(), tasks: 2 },
                { id: 'agent-5', name: 'LLM Specialist', status: 'loading', cpu: 90, memory: 75, lastActive: new Date(), tasks: 4 },
                { id: 'agent-6', name: 'Tech Lead', status: 'offline', cpu: 0, memory: 10, lastActive: new Date(Date.now() - 600000), tasks: 0 }

                { id: 'log-1', timestamp: new Date(Date.now() - 5000), level: 'info', message: 'Componente UserProfileCard implementado com sucesso', agent: 'Dev Frontend' },

# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Infraestrutura como Código

## Estrutura do Projeto

## 1. Arquivo Principal: docker-compose.yml

```yaml
version: '3.8'

x-logging: &default-logging
  driver: "json-file"
  options:
    max-size: "10m"
    max-file: "3"

x-healthcheck: &default-healthcheck
  interval: 30s
  timeout: 10s
  retries: 3
  start_period: 40s

services:
  # --- AGENTES DA SQUAD ---
  agent-sre:
    build:
      context: ./agents/agent-sre
      dockerfile: Dockerfile
    container_name: diyapp-agent-sre
    restart: unless-stopped
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=production
      - LOG_LEVEL=info
      - AGENT_NAME=SRE
      - REDIS_HOST=redis
      - POSTGRES_HOST=postgres
    ports:
      - "3001:3000"
    healthcheck:
      <<: *default-healthcheck
      test: ["CMD", "sh", "./health-check.sh"]
    depends_on:
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy
    logging: *default-logging
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  agent-aiops:
    build:
      context: ./agents/agent-aiops
      dockerfile: Dockerfile
    container_name: diyapp-agent-aiops
    restart: unless-stopped
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=production
      - LOG_LEVEL=info
      - AGENT_NAME=AI_OPS
      - REDIS_HOST=redis
      - LLM_GATEWAY_URL=http://llm-gateway:8080
    ports:
      - "3002:3000"
    healthcheck:
      <<: *default-healthcheck
      test: ["CMD", "sh", "./health-check.sh"]
    depends_on:
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
      llm-gateway:
        condition: service_healthy
    logging: *default-logging
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

    build:
      context: ./agents/agent-backend
      dockerfile: Dockerfile
    container_name: diyapp-agent-backend
    restart: unless-stopped

      - NODE_ENV=production
      - LOG_LEVEL=info
      - AGENT_NAME=BACKEND
      - REDIS_HOST=redis
      - POSTGRES_HOST=postgres
      - API_PORT=3000
    ports:
      - "3003:3000"
    healthcheck:
      <<: *default-healthcheck
      test: ["CMD", "sh", "./health-check.sh"]

        condition: service_healthy

        condition: service_healthy

      context: ./agents/agent-pm

    container_name: diyapp-agent-pm

      - LOG_LEVEL=info
      - AGENT_NAME=PM
      - REDIS_HOST=redis
      - POSTGRES_HOST=postgres
    ports:
      - "3005:3000"
    healthcheck:
      <<: *default-healthcheck
      test: ["CMD", "sh", "./health-check.sh"]
    depends_on:
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy
    logging: *default-logging
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  agent-continuous:
    build:
      context: ./agents/agent-continuous
      dockerfile: Dockerfile
    container_name: diyapp-agent-continuous
    restart: unless-stopped
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=production
      - LOG_LEVEL=info
      - AGENT_NAME=CONTINUOUS
      - REDIS_HOST=redis
      - POSTGRES_HOST=postgres
    ports:
      - "3006:3000"
    healthcheck:
      <<: *default-healthcheck
      test: ["CMD", "sh", "./health-check.sh"]
    depends_on:
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy
    logging: *default-logging
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  # --- INFRAESTRUTURA ---
  nginx:
    image: nginx:alpine
    container_name: diyapp-nginx
    restart: unless-stopped
    ports:
      - "80:80"
      - "443:443"
    volumes:
      - ./nginx/nginx.conf:/etc/nginx/nginx.conf:ro
      - ./ssl:/etc/nginx/ssl:ro
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "nginx", "-t"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
    depends_on:
      - agent-sre
      - agent-aiops
      - agent-backend
      - agent-infra
      - agent-pm
      - agent-continuous
    logging: *default-logging
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  postgres:
    image: postgres:15-alpine
    container_name: diyapp-postgres
    restart: unless-stopped
    environment:
      - POSTGRES_DB=diyapp
      - POSTGRES_USER=${DB_USER:-diyapp}
      - POSTGRES_PASSWORD=${DB_PASSWORD:-diyapp123}
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
      - ./init-db.sql:/docker-entrypoint-initdb.d/init-db.sql:ro
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U ${DB_USER:-diyapp}"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 40s
    logging: *default-logging
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    container_name: diyapp-redis
    restart: unless-stopped
    command: redis-server --appendonly yes --requirepass ${REDIS_PASSWORD:-diyapp123}
    volumes:
      - redis_data:/data
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "redis-cli", "--raw", "incr", "ping"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 40s
    logging: *default-logging
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  llm-gateway:
    image: ghcr.io/llm-gateway/llm-gateway:latest
    container_name: diyapp-llm-gateway
    restart: unless-stopped
    environment:
      - OPENAI_API_KEY=${OPENAI_API_KEY}
      - ANTHROPIC_API_KEY=${ANTHROPIC_API_KEY}
      - GOOGLE_API_KEY=${GOOGLE_API_KEY}
      - GATEWAY_PORT=8080
    ports:
      - "8080:8080"
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:8080/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 40s
    logging: *default-logging
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  # --- MONITORING & LOGGING ---
  prometheus:
    image: prom/prometheus:latest
    container_name: diyapp-prometheus
    restart: unless-stopped
    volumes:
      - ./monitoring/prometheus/prometheus.yml:/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml:ro
      - prometheus_data:/prometheus
    command:
      - '--config.file=/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml'
      - '--storage.tsdb.path=/prometheus'
      - '--web.console.libraries=/etc/prometheus/console_libraries'
      - '--web.console.templates=/etc/prometheus/consoles'
      - '--storage.tsdb.retention.time=200h'
      - '--web.enable-lifecycle'
    ports:
      - "9090:9090"
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "wget", "--no-verbose", "--tries=1", "--spider", "http://localhost:9090/-/healthy"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
    logging: *default-logging
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  grafana:
    image: grafana/grafana:latest
    container_name: diyapp-grafana
    restart: unless-stopped
    environment:
      - GF_SECURITY_ADMIN_USER=${GRAFANA_USER:-admin}
      - GF_SECURITY_ADMIN_PASSWORD=${GRAFANA_PASSWORD:-admin123}
      - GF_INSTALL_PLUGINS=grafana-piechart-panel
    volumes:
      - grafana_data:/var/lib/grafana
      - ./monitoring/grafana/provisioning:/etc/grafana/provisioning:ro
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:3000/api/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 60s
    depends_on:
      - prometheus
      - loki
    logging: *default-logging
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  loki:
    image: grafana/loki:latest
    container_name: diyapp-loki
    restart: unless-stopped
    command: -config.file=/etc/loki/local-config.yaml
    volumes:
      - ./logging/loki-config.yml:/etc/loki/local-config.yaml:ro
      - loki_data:/loki
    ports:
      - "3100:3100"
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:3100/ready"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 40s
    logging: *default-logging
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  promtail:
    image: grafana/promtail:latest
    container_name: diyapp-promtail
    restart: unless-stopped
    volumes:
      - /var/run/docker.sock:/var/run/docker.sock
      - ./logging/promtail-config.yml:/etc/promtail/config.yml:ro
      - /var/lib/docker/containers:/var/lib/docker/containers:ro
    command: -config.file=/etc/promtail/config.yml
    depends_on:
      - loki
    logging: *default-logging
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

networks:
  diyapp-network:
    driver: bridge
    name: diyapp-network

volumes:
  postgres_data:
    driver: local
  redis_data:
    driver: local
  prometheus_data:
    driver: local
  grafana_data:
    driver: local
  loki_data:
    driver: local
```

## 2. Dockerfile Template para Agentes

**agents/agent-sre/Dockerfile:**
```dockerfile
FROM node:18-alpine

WORKDIR /app

# Instalar dependências do sistema
RUN apk add --no-cache \
    curl \
    bash \
    postgresql-client \
    redis

# Copiar package.json e instalar dependências
COPY package*.json ./
RUN npm ci --only=production

# Copiar código da aplicação
COPY . .

# Criar usuário não-root
RUN addgroup -g 1001 -S nodejs && \
    adduser -S nodejs -u 1001 && \
    chown -R nodejs:nodejs /app

USER nodejs

# Expor porta
EXPOSE 3000

# Health check script
COPY health-check.sh ./health-check.sh
RUN chmod +x ./health-check.sh

# Comando de inicialização
CMD ["node", "index.js"]
```

## 3. Scripts de Health Check

**agents/agent-sre/health-check.sh:**
```bash
#!/bin/bash

# Health check para agente SRE
# Verifica se o serviço está respondendo e se as dependências estão saudáveis

set -e

# URL do health check do próprio agente
AGENT_URL="http://localhost:3000/health"

# Verificar se o agente está respondendo
echo "Checking agent health..."
if ! curl -f --max-time 5 "$AGENT_URL"; then
    echo "Agent health check failed"
    exit 1
fi

# Verificar conexão com Redis
if [ -n "$REDIS_HOST" ]; then
    echo "Checking Redis connection..."
    if ! redis-cli -h "$REDIS_HOST" -a "${REDIS_PASSWORD:-}" ping | grep -q "PONG"; then
        echo "Redis connection failed"
        exit 1
    fi
fi

# Verificar conexão com PostgreSQL
if [ -n "$POSTGRES_HOST" ]; then
    echo "Checking PostgreSQL connection..."
    if ! PGPASSWORD="${DB_PASSWORD:-}" psql -h "$POSTGRES_HOST" -U "${DB_USER:-}" -d diyapp -c "SELECT 1" > /dev/null 2>&1; then
        echo "PostgreSQL connection failed"
        exit 1
    fi
fi

echo "All health checks passed"
exit 0
```

## ADR 001: Arquitetura de Microsserviços

**docs/adrs/001-microservices-architecture.md**
```markdown
# ADR-001: Arquitetura Baseada em Microsserviços

## Status
Aceito

## Data
2024-01-15

## Autores
Tech Lead, Especialista Infra

## Contexto
O DIYAPP precisa evoluir para uma arquitetura escalável que permita:
1. Desenvolvimento paralelo por múltiplas squads
2. Deploy independente de componentes
3. Isolamento de falhas
4. Escala seletiva de serviços

## Decisão
Adotar arquitetura de microsserviços com os seguintes princípios:
- Cada serviço é responsável por um domínio específico
- Comunicação via HTTP/REST para síncrono, eventos para assíncrono
- Banco de dados por serviço (Database per Service)
- Containerização com Docker
- Orquestração com Kubernetes

## Opções Consideradas
### Opção A: Monolito Modular
- Prós: Simplicidade inicial, transações ACID fáceis
- Contras: Acoplamento alto, deploy único, escala limitada

### Opção B: Microsserviços Leves
- Prós: Escala independente, resiliência, deploy contínuo
- Contras: Complexidade operacional, consistência eventual

### Opção C: Arquitetura em Camadas
- Prós: Separação de responsabilidades
- Contras: Acoplamento ainda presente

## Escolha: Opção B
Justificativa: Alinha com objetivo de autonomia das squads e permite crescimento sustentável.

## Consequências
### Positivas
- Desenvolvimento paralelo acelerado
- Escala seletiva de serviços críticos
- Tecnologias específicas por domínio
- Falhas isoladas

### Negativas
- Complexidade de deploy e monitoramento
- Consistência eventual
- Overhead de comunicação
- Necessidade de expertise em containers

### Riscos
1. Latência em chamadas entre serviços
   - Mitigação: Cache estratégico, padrões CQRS
2. Gerenciamento de transações distribuídas
   - Mitigação: Saga pattern, compensação
3. Observabilidade distribuída
   - Mitigação: OpenTelemetry, logs centralizados

## Revisão
Reavaliar em 6 meses ou após 50 serviços implantados
```

## Template de Serviço

**templates/service-template/src/index.js**
```javascript
const express = require('express');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const cors = require('cors');
const { diyLogger, metrics, tracer } = require('./utils/observability');
const { errorHandler } = require('./middleware/errorHandler');
const { requestLogger } = require('./middleware/requestLogger');
const { validateEnv } = require('./utils/envValidator');
const healthRoutes = require('./controllers/healthController');
const apiRoutes = require('./controllers/apiController');

class Service {
  constructor() {
    this.app = express();
    this.port = process.env.PORT || 3000;
    
    // Validar variáveis de ambiente
    validateEnv();
    
    // Inicializar observabilidade
    this.setupObservability();
    
    // Configurar middleware
    this.setupMiddleware();
    
    // Configurar rotas
    this.setupRoutes();
    
    // Configurar handlers de erro
    this.setupErrorHandling();
  }
  
  setupObservability() {
    // Inicializar tracer OpenTelemetry
    tracer.init({
      serviceName: process.env.SERVICE_NAME,
      environment: process.env.NODE_ENV
    });
    
    // Inicializar métricas
    metrics.init();
    
    diyLogger.info('Observabilidade configurada', {
      service: process.env.SERVICE_NAME,
      env: process.env.NODE_ENV
    });
  }
  
  setupMiddleware() {
    // Segurança
    this.app.use(helmet());
    this.app.use(cors({
      origin: process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS?.split(',') || [],
      credentials: true
    }));
    
    // Parsing
    this.app.use(express.json({ limit: '10mb' }));
    this.app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true }));
    
    // Logging de requests
    this.app.use(requestLogger);
    
    // Health check básico
    this.app.get('/health', (req, res) => {
      res.json({ 
        status: 'healthy',
        service: process.env.SERVICE_NAME,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      });
    });
  }
  
  setupRoutes() {
    // Rotas de health com métricas
    this.app.use('/api/health', healthRoutes);
    
    // Rotas da API
    this.app.use('/api/v1', apiRoutes);
    
    // 404 handler
    this.app.use('*', (req, res) => {
      res.status(404).json({
        error: 'Route not found',
        path: req.originalUrl,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      });
    });
  }
  
  setupErrorHandling() {
    this.app.use(errorHandler);
  }
  
  start() {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      const server = this.app.listen(this.port, () => {
        diyLogger.info(`Serviço ${process.env.SERVICE_NAME} iniciado`, {
          port: this.port,
          env: process.env.NODE_ENV,
          pid: process.pid
        });
        
        // Registrar métrica de startup
        metrics.recordCounter('service_startup_total', 1, {
          service: process.env.SERVICE_NAME
        });
        
        resolve(server);
      });
      
      server.on('error', (error) => {
        diyLogger.error('Erro ao iniciar serviço', {
          error: error.message,
          service: process.env.SERVICE_NAME,
          stack: error.stack
        });
        reject(error);
      });
    });
  }
  
  async gracefulShutdown(signal) {
    diyLogger.info(`Recebido sinal ${signal}, iniciando shutdown gracioso`, {
      service: process.env.SERVICE_NAME
    });
    
    // Parar de aceitar novas conexões
    this.server.close(() => {
      diyLogger.info('Servidor HTTP fechado', {
        service: process.env.SERVICE_NAME
      });
      
      // Fechar conexões com banco, etc.
      process.exit(0);
    });
    
    // Timeout forçado após 30 segundos
    setTimeout(() => {
      diyLogger.error('Shutdown gracioso timeout, forçando saída', {
        service: process.env.SERVICE_NAME
      });
      process.exit(1);
    }, 30000);
  }
}

// Inicialização
if (require.main === module) {
  const service = new Service();
  
  service.start().then(server => {
    service.server = server;
    
    // Handlers de shutdown
    process.on('SIGTERM', () => service.gracefulShutdown('SIGTERM'));
    process.on('SIGINT', () => service.gracefulShutdown('SIGINT'));
  }).catch(error => {
    diyLogger.error('Falha ao iniciar serviço', {
      error: error.message,
      stack: error.stack
    });
    process.exit(1);
  });
}

module.exports = Service;
```

## Utilitários de Observabilidade

**templates/service-template/src/utils/observability.js**
```javascript
const winston = require('winston');
const { createLogger, format, transports } = winston;
const { combine, timestamp, json, errors } = format;
const { Resource } = require('@opentelemetry/resources');
const { SemanticResourceAttributes } = require('@opentelemetry/semantic-conventions');
const { NodeTracerProvider } = require('@opentelemetry/sdk-trace-node');
const { SimpleSpanProcessor } = require('@opentelemetry/sdk-trace-base');
const { OTLPTraceExporter } = require('@opentelemetry/exporter-trace-otlp-http');
const { MeterProvider } = require('@opentelemetry/sdk-metrics');
const { OTLPMetricExporter } = require('@opentelemetry/exporter-metrics-otlp-http');
const { PeriodicExportingMetricReader } = require('@opentelemetry/sdk-metrics');

class DIYLogger {
  constructor(serviceName) {
    this.logger = createLogger({
      level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
      format: combine(
        errors({ stack: true }),
        timestamp(),
        json()
      ),
      defaultMeta: {
        service: serviceName,
        environment: process.env.NODE_ENV || 'development',
        version: process.env.APP_VERSION || '1.0.0'
      },
      transports: [
        new transports.Console(),
        new transports.File({ 
          filename: `logs/${serviceName}-error.log`, 
          level: 'error' 
        }),
        new transports.File({ 
          filename: `logs/${serviceName}-combined.log` 
        })
      ]
    });
  }

  info(message, meta = {}) {
    this.logger.info(message, meta);
  }

  error(message, meta = {}) {
    this.logger.error(message, meta);
  }

  warn(message, meta = {}) {
    this.logger.warn(message, meta);
  }

  debug(message, meta = {}) {
    this.logger.debug(message, meta);
  }

  audit(event, userId, details = {}) {
    this.logger.info('AUDIT', {
      event,
      userId,
      ...details,
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      ip: details.ip || 'unknown'
    });
  }
}

class Metrics {
  constructor() {
    this.meterProvider = null;
    this.meters = new Map();
  }

  init() {
    const resource = new Resource({
      [SemanticResourceAttributes.SERVICE_NAME]: process.env.SERVICE_NAME,
      [SemanticResourceAttributes.DEPLOYMENT_ENVIRONMENT]: process.env.NODE_ENV
    });

    this.meterProvider = new MeterProvider({ resource });

    const metricExporter = new OTLPMetricExporter({
      url: process.env.OTLP_ENDPOINT || 'http://collector:4318/v1/metrics'
    });

    const metricReader = new PeriodicExportingMetricReader({
      exporter: metricExporter,
      exportIntervalMillis: 60000
    });

    this.meterProvider.addMetricReader(metricReader);
  }

  getMeter(name) {
    if (!this.meters.has(name)) {
      this.meters.set(name, this.meterProvider.getMeter(name));
    }
    return this.meters.get(name);
  }

  recordCounter(name, value, attributes = {}) {
    const meter = this.getMeter('default');
    const counter = meter.createCounter(name, {
      description: `Counter for ${name}`
    });
    counter.add(value, attributes);
  }

  recordHistogram(name, value, attributes = {}) {
    const meter = this.getMeter('default');
    const histogram = meter.createHistogram(name, {
      description: `Histogram for ${name}`,
      unit: 'ms'
    });
    histogram.record(value, attributes);
  }
}

class Tracer {
  constructor() {
    this.provider = null;
  }

  init(config) {
    const resource = new Resource({
      [SemanticResourceAttributes.SERVICE_NAME]: config.serviceName,
      [SemanticResourceAttributes.DEPLOYMENT_ENVIRONMENT]: config.environment
    });

    this.provider = new NodeTracerProvider({ resource });

    const traceExporter = new OTLPTraceExporter({
      url: process.env.OTLP_ENDPOINT || 'http://collector:4318/v1/traces'
    });

    this.provider.addSpanProcessor(new SimpleSpanProcessor(traceExporter));
    this.provider.register();
  }

  getTracer(name) {
    return require('@opentelemetry/api').trace.getTracer(name);
  }
}

// Instâncias singleton
const diyLogger = new DIYLogger(process.env.SERVICE_NAME || 'unknown-service');
const metrics = new Metrics();
const tracer = new Tracer();

module.exports = {
  diyLogger,
  metrics,
  tracer
};
```

## Middleware de Logging

**templates/service-template/src/middleware/requestLogger.js**
```javascript
const { diyLogger, metrics } = require('../utils/observability');

const requestLogger = (req, res, next) => {
  const startTime = Date.now();
  const requestId = req.headers['x-request-id'] || require('crypto').randomUUID();
  
  // Adicionar requestId ao objeto req
  req.requestId = requestId;
  
  // Log da requisição recebida
  diyLogger.info('Request received', {
    requestId,
    method: req.method,
    url: req.originalUrl,
    ip: req.ip,
    userAgent: req.get('user-agent'),
    contentType: req.get('content-type')
  });
  
  // Hook para log da resposta
  const originalSend = res.send;
  res.send = function(body) {
    const responseTime = Date.now() - startTime;
    
    // Log da resposta
    diyLogger.info('Response sent', {
      requestId,
      method: req.method,
      url: req.originalUrl,
      statusCode: res.statusCode,
      responseTime,
      contentLength: res.get('content-length')
    });
    
    // Registrar métricas
    metrics.recordHistogram('http_request_duration_ms', responseTime, {
      method: req.method,
      route: req.route?.path || req.originalUrl,
      status_code: res.statusCode,
      service: process.env.SERVICE_NAME
    });
    
    metrics.recordCounter('http_requests_total', 1, {
      method: req.method,
      status_code: res.statusCode,
      service: process.env.SERVICE_NAME
    });
    
    return originalSend.call(this, body);
  };
  
  next();
};

module.exports = { requestLogger };
```

## Dockerfile

**templates/service-template/Dockerfile**
```dockerfile
# Build stage
FROM node:18-alpine AS builder

WORKDIR /app

# Copiar arquivos de dependências
COPY package*.json ./
COPY .npmrc ./

# Instalar dependências
RUN npm ci --only=production

# Runtime stage
FROM node:18-alpine

WORKDIR /app

# Criar usuário não-root
RUN addgroup -g 1001 -S nodejs && \
    adduser -S nodejs -u 1001

# Copiar dependências do builder
COPY --from=builder --chown=nodejs:nodejs /app/node_modules ./node_modules

# Copiar código da aplicação
COPY --chown=nodejs:nodejs . .

# Criar diretório de logs
RUN mkdir -p logs && chown nodejs:nodejs logs

# Mudar para usuário não-root
USER nodejs

# Health check
HEALTHCHECK --interval=30s --timeout=3s --start-period=5s --retries=3 \
  CMD node -e "require('http').get('http://localhost:${PORT:-3000}/health', (r) => {if(r.statusCode !== 200) throw new Error()})"

# Expor porta
EXPOSE ${PORT:-3000}

# Comando de inicialização
CMD ["node", "src/index.js"]
```

## docker-compose.yml para Desenvolvimento

**templates/service-template/docker-compose.yml**
```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  app:
    build: .
    ports:
      - "${PORT:-3000}:3000"
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=development
      - SERVICE_NAME=${SERVICE_NAME}
      - PORT=3000
      - LOG_LEVEL=debug
      - OTLP_ENDPOINT=http://collector:4318
    volumes:
      - ./logs:/app/logs
      - ./src:/app/src
    depends_on:
      - collector
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  collector:
    image: otel/opentelemetry-collector-contrib:latest
    command: ["--config=/etc/otel-collector-config.yaml"]
    volumes:
      - ./otel-collector-config.yaml:/etc/otel-collector-config.yaml
    ports:
      - "4317:4317"  # OTLP gRPC
      - "4318:4318"  # OTLP HTTP
      - "8888:8888"  # Prometheus metrics
      - "8889:8889"  # Prometheus exporter
      - "13133:13133" # Health check
      - "55679:55679" # zPages
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  jaeger:
    image: jaegertracing

# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Sistema de Design

Vou criar um sistema de design completo com tokens, componentes de alta-fidelidade, protótipo interativo e foco em acessibilidade WCAG AA.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v10-design-system/
├── index.html              # Dashboard principal
├── design-tokens.css       # Tokens de design
├── components.css          # Componentes estilizados
├── prototype.js           # Interatividade do protótipo
├── accessibility-checker.js # Verificador de acessibilidade
├── assets/
│   ├── icons/             # Ícones do sistema
│   └── fonts/             # Fontes personalizadas
└── README.md              # Documentação do sistema
```

### [Sessão Paralela: Backend]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Serviços Backend

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v10-core/
├── package.json
├── tsconfig.json
├── .env.example
├── docker-compose.yml

POSTGRES_PASSWORD=diyapp_password

## 4. docker-compose.yml

```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  postgres:
    image: postgres:15-alpine
    container_name: diyapp-postgres
    environment:
      POSTGRES_USER: diyapp_user
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: diyapp_password
      POSTGRES_DB: diyapp_v10
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
      - ./src/migrations:/docker-entrypoint-initdb.d
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U diyapp_user"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    container_name: diyapp-redis
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"
    volumes:
      - redis_data:/data
    command: redis-server --appendonly yes
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "redis-cli", "ping"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  api-gateway:
    build:
      context: .
      dockerfile: Dockerfile.api-gateway
    container_name: diyapp-api-gateway
    ports:
      - "8080:8080"
    environment:
      NODE_ENV: production
      API_GATEWAY_PORT: 8080
      AUTH_SERVICE_URL: http://auth-service:3001
      PROJECT_SERVICE_URL: http://project-service:3002
      REDIS_HOST: redis
      REDIS_PORT: 6379
    depends_on:
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
      auth-service:
        condition: service_started
      project-service:
        condition: service_started
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  auth-service:
    build:
      context: .
      dockerfile: Dockerfile.auth-service
    container_name: diyapp-auth-service
    ports:
      - "3001:3001"
    environment:
      NODE_ENV: production
      AUTH_SERVICE_PORT: 3001
      POSTGRES_HOST: postgres
      POSTGRES_PORT: 5432
      REDIS_HOST: redis
      REDIS_PORT: 6379
      JWT_SECRET: ${JWT_SECRET:-default-secret-change-me}
      JWT_REFRESH_SECRET: ${JWT_REFRESH_SECRET:-default-refresh-secret-change-me}
    depends_on:
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  project-service:
    build:
      context: .
      dockerfile: Dockerfile.project-service
    container_name: diyapp-project-service
    ports:
      - "3002:3002"
    environment:
      NODE_ENV: production
      PROJECT_SERVICE_PORT: 3002
      POSTGRES_HOST: postgres
      POSTGRES_PORT: 5432
      REDIS_HOST: redis
      REDIS_PORT: 6379
    depends_on:
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

volumes:
  postgres_data:
  redis_data:

networks:
  diyapp-network:
    driver: bridge
```

## 5. src/shared/utils/logger.ts

```typescript
import winston from 'winston';
import DailyRotateFile from 'winston-daily-rotate-file';
import path from 'path';

const logDir = 'logs';

const levels = {
  error: 0,
  warn: 1,
  info: 2,
  http: 3,
  debug: 4,
};

const colors = {
  error: 'red',
  warn: 'yellow',
  info: 'green',
  http: 'magenta',
  debug: 'white',
};

winston.addColors(colors);

const format = winston.format.combine(
  winston.format.timestamp({ format: 'YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss:ms' }),
  winston.format.errors({ stack: true }),
  winston.format.json(),
  winston.format.printf((info) => {
    const { timestamp, level, message, correlationId, userId, endpoint, durationMs, status, ...rest } = info;
    
    const logEntry: any = {
      level,
      timestamp,
      correlation_id: correlationId,
      user_id: userId,
      endpoint,
      duration_ms: durationMs,
      status,
      message,
    };

    // Mask sensitive data
    if (rest.email) logEntry.email = maskEmail(rest.email);
    if (rest.token) logEntry.token = '***';
    if (rest.password) logEntry.password = '***';
    if (rest.cpf) logEntry.cpf = maskCPF(rest.cpf);
    if (rest.card) logEntry.card = maskCard(rest.card);

    // Add other fields
    Object.keys(rest).forEach(key => {
      if (!['email', 'token', 'password', 'cpf', 'card'].includes(key)) {
        logEntry[key] = rest[key];
      }
    });

    return JSON.stringify(logEntry);
  })
);

function maskEmail(email: string): string {
  const [local, domain] = email.split('@');
  if (local.length <= 2) return `${local[0]}***@${domain}`;
  return `${local[0]}***${local[local.length - 1]}@${domain}`;
}

function maskCPF(cpf: string): string {
  return cpf.replace(/(\d{3})\.(\d{3})\.(\d{3})-(\d{2})/, '***.***.***-**');
}

function maskCard(card: string): string {
  return card.replace(/(\d{4})-(\d{4})-(\d{4})-(\d{4})/, '****-****-****-$4');
}

const transports = [
  new DailyRotateFile({
    filename: path.join(logDir, 'error-%DATE%.log'),
    datePattern: 'YYYY-MM-DD',
    level: 'error',
    maxSize: '10m',
    maxFiles: '14d',
  }),
  new DailyRotateFile({
    filename: path.join(logDir, 'combined-%DATE%.log'),
    datePattern: 'YYYY-MM-DD',
    maxSize: '10m',
    maxFiles: '14d',
  }),
  new winston.transports.Console({
    format: winston.format.combine(
      winston.format.colorize({ all: true }),
      winston.format.simple()
    ),
  }),
];

const logger = winston.createLogger({
  level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
  levels,
  format,
  transports,
  exceptionHandlers: [
    new DailyRotateFile({
      filename: path.join(logDir, 'exceptions-%DATE%.log'),
      datePattern: 'YYYY-MM-DD',
      maxSize: '10m',
      maxFiles: '14d',
    }),
  ],
  rejectionHandlers: [
    new DailyRotateFile({
      filename: path.join(logDir, 'rejections-%DATE%.log'),
      datePattern: 'YYYY-MM-DD',
      maxSize: '10m',
      maxFiles: '14d',
    }),
  ],
});

export default logger;
```

## 6. src/shared/database/postgres.ts

```typescript
import { Pool, PoolConfig, QueryResult } from 'pg';
import logger from '../utils/logger';

class PostgreSQLClient {
  private pool: Pool;
  private static instance: PostgreSQLClient;

  private constructor(config: PoolConfig) {
    this.pool = new Pool({
      ...config,
      max: 20,
      idleTimeoutMillis: 30000,
      connectionTimeoutMillis: 10000,
    });

    this.pool.on('error', (err: Error) => {
      logger.error('Unexpected error on idle PostgreSQL client', {
        error: err.message,
        stack: err.stack,
      });
    });

    this.testConnection();
  }

  public static getInstance(config?: PoolConfig): PostgreSQLClient {
    if (!PostgreSQLClient.instance) {
      if (!config) {
        throw new Error('PostgreSQL configuration required for first initialization');
      }
      PostgreSQLClient.instance = new PostgreSQLClient(config);
    }
    return PostgreSQLClient.instance;
  }

  private async testConnection(): Promise<void> {
    try {
      const client = await this.pool.connect();
      const result = await client.query('SELECT NOW()');
      client.release();
      
      logger.info('PostgreSQL connection established successfully', {
        timestamp: result.

```typescript
// src/app/layout.tsx
import type { Metadata } from 'next'
import { Inter } from 'next/font/google'
import './globals.css'
import { Providers } from '@/providers'

const inter = Inter({ subsets: ['latin'] })

export const metadata: Metadata = {
  title: 'DIYAPP Evolution V10',
  description: 'Next generation autonomous application platform',
}

export default function RootLayout({
  children,
}: {
  children: React.ReactNode
}) {
  return (
    <html lang="en" className="h-full">
      <body className={`${inter.className} h-full bg-gray-50`}>
        <Providers>
          <div className="min-h-full">
            {children}
          </div>
        </Providers>
      </body>
    </html>
  )
}

```css
/* src/app/globals.css */
@tailwind base;
@tailwind components;
@tailwind utilities;

@layer base {
  :root {
    /* Performance optimizations */
    scroll-behavior: smooth;
  }

  /* Focus styles for accessibility */
  *:focus {
    @apply outline-2 outline-primary-600 outline-offset-2;
  }

  /* Remove focus outline for mouse users */
  *:focus:not(:focus-visible) {
    @apply outline-none;
  }
}

@layer components {
  /* Design System utility classes */
  .container-narrow {
    @apply max-w-4xl mx-auto px-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8;
  }

  .container-wide {
    @apply max-w-7xl mx-auto px-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8;
  }
}

/* Performance optimizations */
img {
  @apply max-w-full h-auto;
}

/* Prevent layout shifts */
.aspect-ratio-box {
  position: relative;
  width: 100%;
  padding-top: 56.25%; /* 16:9 Aspect Ratio */
}

.aspect-ratio-content {
  position: absolute;
  top: 0;
  left: 0;
  width: 100%;
  height: 100%;
}

```typescript
// src/providers/index.tsx
'use client'

import { QueryClient, QueryClientProvider } from '@tanstack/react-query'
import { ReactQueryDevtools } from '@tanstack/react-query-devtools'
import { ReactNode, useState } from 'react'

interface ProvidersProps {
  children: ReactNode
}

export function Providers({ children }: ProvidersProps) {
  const [queryClient] = useState(() => new QueryClient({
    defaultOptions: {
      queries: {
        staleTime: 60 * 1000, // 1 minute
        gcTime: 5 * 60 * 1000, // 5 minutes
        retry: 3,
        retryDelay: (attemptIndex) => Math.min(1000 * 2 ** attemptIndex, 30000),
      },
    },
  }))

  return (
    <QueryClientProvider client={queryClient}>
      {children}
      {process.env.NODE_ENV === 'development' && (
        <ReactQueryDevtools initialIsOpen={false} />
      )}
    </QueryClientProvider>
  )
}
```

```typescript
// src/components/atoms/Button/Button.tsx
import { ButtonHTMLAttributes, forwardRef } from 'react'
import { Loader2 } from 'lucide-react'
import { cn } from '@/utils/cn'

export type ButtonVariant = 'primary' | 'secondary' | 'outline' | 'ghost' | 'destructive'
export type ButtonSize = 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg'

export interface ButtonProps extends ButtonHTMLAttributes<HTMLButtonElement> {
  variant?: ButtonVariant
  size?: ButtonSize
  loading?: boolean
  fullWidth?: boolean
}

const variantClasses: Record<ButtonVariant, string> = {
  primary: 'bg-primary-600 text-white hover:bg-primary-700 focus:ring-primary-600',
  secondary: 'bg-secondary-600 text-white hover:bg-secondary-700 focus:ring-secondary-600',
  outline: 'border-2 border-primary-600 text-primary-600 hover:bg-primary-50 focus:ring-primary-600',
  ghost: 'text-secondary-700 hover:bg-secondary-100 focus:ring-secondary-600',
  destructive: 'bg-error-500 text-white hover:bg-error-600 focus:ring-error-500',
}

const sizeClasses: Record<ButtonSize, string> = {
  sm: 'px-3 py-1.5 text-sm',
  md: 'px-4 py-2 text-base',
  lg: 'px-6 py-3 text-lg',
}

export const Button = forwardRef<HTMLButtonElement, ButtonProps>(({
  className,
  variant = 'primary',
  size = 'md',
  loading = false,
  disabled,
  fullWidth = false,
  children,
  ...props
}, ref) => {
  return (
    <button
      ref={ref}
      className={cn(
        'inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md font-medium transition-colors',
        'focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-offset-2',
        'disabled:opacity-50 disabled:cursor-not-allowed',
        variantClasses[variant],
        sizeClasses[size],
        fullWidth && 'w-full',
        className
      )}
      disabled={disabled || loading}
      aria-busy={loading}
      {...props}
    >
      {loading && (
        <Loader2 className="mr-2 h-4 w-4 animate-spin" aria-hidden="true" />
      )}
      {children}
    </button>
  )
})

Button.displayName = 'Button'
```

```typescript
// src/components/atoms/Button/Button.test.tsx
import { describe, it, expect, vi } from 'vitest'
import { render, screen, fireEvent } from '@testing-library/react'
import { Button } from './Button'

describe('Button', () => {
  it('renders with default props', () => {
    render(<Button>Click me</Button>)
    const button = screen.getByRole('button', { name: /click me/i })
    expect(button).toBeInTheDocument()
    expect(button).toHaveClass('bg-primary-600')
  })

  it('renders loading state', () => {
    render(<Button loading>Loading</Button>)
    const button = screen.getByRole('button', { name: /loading/i })
    expect(button).toBeDisabled()
    expect(button).toHaveAttribute('aria-busy', 'true')
    expect(screen.getByRole('img', { hidden: true })).toBeInTheDocument()
  })

  it('handles click events', () => {
    const handleClick = vi.fn()
    render(<Button onClick={handleClick}>Click</Button>)
    fireEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button'))
    expect(handleClick).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(1)
  })

  it('renders different variants', () => {
    const { rerender } = render(<Button variant="secondary">Secondary</Button>)
    expect(screen.getByRole('button')).toHaveClass('bg-secondary-600')

    rerender(<Button variant="outline">Outline</Button>)
    expect(screen.getByRole('button')).toHaveClass('border-primary-600')
  })

  it('renders different sizes', () => {
    render(<Button size="lg">Large</Button>)
    expect(screen.getByRole('button')).toHaveClass('px-6 py-3 text-lg')
  })
})
```

```typescript
// src/components/atoms/Input/Input.tsx
import { InputHTMLAttributes, forwardRef } from 'react'
import { AlertCircle } from 'lucide-react'
import { cn } from '@/utils/cn'

export interface InputProps extends InputHTMLAttributes<HTMLInputElement> {
  label?: string
  error?: string
  helperText?: string
}

export const Input = forwardRef<HTMLInputElement, InputProps>(({
  className,
  label,
  error,
  helperText,
  id,
  required,
  ...props
}, ref) => {
  const inputId = id || `input-${Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9)}`

  return (
    <div className="space-y-2">
      {label && (
        <label
          htmlFor={inputId}
          className="block text-sm font-medium text-secondary-700"
        >
          {label}
          {required && <span className="text-error-500 ml-1">*</span>}
        </label>
      )}
      <div className="relative">
        <input
          ref={ref}
          id={inputId}
          className={cn(
            'block w-full rounded-md border-2 px-3 py-2 text-secondary-900',
            'placeholder:text-secondary-400',
            'focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-primary-600 focus:border-transparent',
            error
              ? 'border-error-300 focus:ring-error-500'
              : 'border-secondary-300',
            'disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:bg-secondary-100 disabled:text-secondary-500',
            className
          )}
          aria-invalid={!!error}
          aria-describedby={
            error ? `${inputId}-error` : helperText ? `${inputId}-helper` : undefined
          }
          required={required}
          {...props}
        />
        {error && (
          <div className="pointer-events-none absolute inset-y-0 right-0 flex items-center pr-3">
            <AlertCircle className="h-5 w-5 text-error-500" aria-hidden="true" />
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
      {error && (
        <p id={`${inputId}-error`} className="text-sm text-error-600">
          {error}
        </p>
      )}
      {helperText && !error && (
        <p id={`${inputId}-helper`} className="text-sm text-secondary-500">
          {helperText}
        </p>
      )}
    </div>
  )
})

Input.displayName = 'Input'
```

```typescript
// src/components/molecules/Card/Card.tsx
import { ReactNode } from 'react'
import { cn } from '@/utils/cn'

interface CardProps {
  children: ReactNode
  className?: string
}

interface CardHeaderProps {
  children: ReactNode
  className?: string
}

interface CardContentProps {
  children: ReactNode
  className?: string
}

interface CardFooterProps {
  children: ReactNode
  className?: string
}

export const Card = ({ children, className }: CardProps) => {
  return (
    <div
      className={cn(
        'bg-white rounded-lg shadow-sm border border-secondary-200',
        'overflow-hidden',
        className
      )}
    >
      {children}
    </div>
  )
}

export const CardHeader = ({ children, className }: CardHeaderProps) => {
  return (
    <div className={cn('px-6 py-4 border-b border-secondary-200', className)}>
      {children}
    </div>
  )
}

export const CardContent = ({ children, className }: CardContentProps) => {
  return (
    <div className={cn('px-6 py-4', className)}>
      {children}
    </div>
  )
}

export const CardFooter = ({ children, className }: CardFooterProps) => {
  return (
    <div className={cn('px-6 py-4 border-t border-secondary-200', className)}>
      {children}
    </div>
  )
}

# Configuração de Auto-scaling Horizontal Pod Autoscaler (HPA)
resource "kubernetes_manifest" "hpa_diyapp" {
  manifest = {
    apiVersion = "autoscaling/v2"
    kind       = "HorizontalPodAutoscaler"
    metadata = {
      name      = "diyapp-hpa"
      namespace = "default"
    }
    spec = {
      scaleTargetRef = {
        apiVersion = "apps/v1"
        kind       = "Deployment"
        name       = "diyapp-deployment"
      }
      minReplicas = var.min_pod_replicas
      maxReplicas = var.max_pod_replicas
      metrics = [
        {
          type = "Resource"
          resource = {
            name = "cpu"
            target = {
              type                = "Utilization"
              averageUtilization  = 70
            }
          }
        },
        {
          type = "Resource"
          resource = {
            name = "memory"
            target = {
              type                = "Utilization"
              averageUtilization  = 80
            }
          }
        }
      ]
      behavior = {
        scaleUp = {
          stabilizationWindowSeconds = 60
          policies = [
            {
              type          = "Pods"
              value         = 4
              periodSeconds = 60
            }
          ]
        }
        scaleDown = {
          stabilizationWindowSeconds = 300
          policies = [
            {
              type          = "Pods"
              value         = 2
              periodSeconds = 60
            }
          ]
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

# Configuração de Cluster Autoscaler

              memory = "2Gi"

# PrometheusRule para alertas baseados em SLOs
resource "kubernetes_manifest" "prometheus_rule_slo" {
  manifest = {
    apiVersion = "monitoring.coreos.com/v1"
    kind       = "PrometheusRule"
    metadata = {
      name      = "diyapp-slo-alerts"
      namespace = "monitoring"
      labels = {
        release = "prometheus"
      }
    }
    spec = {
      groups = [
        {
          name = "diyapp-slo"
          rules = [
            {
              alert: "APIAvailabilityBelowSLO"
              expr: |-
                sum(rate(http_requests_total{status=~"5..", job="diyapp"}[5m])) 
                / sum(rate(http_requests_total{job="diyapp"}[5m])) > 0.001
              for: "2m"
              labels:
                severity: "critical"
                squad: "sre"
              annotations:
                summary: "API Error Rate above SLO (0.1%)"
                description: "Error rate is {{ $value }}. Error budget is being consumed rapidly."
                runbook_url: "https://runbooks.diyapp.com/api-error-rate"
            },
            {
              alert: "APILatencyAboveSLO"
              expr: |-
                histogram_quantile(0.95, rate(http_request_duration_seconds_bucket{job="diyapp"}[5m])) > 0.3
              for: "3m"
              labels:
                severity: "warning"
                squad: "sre"
              annotations:
                summary: "API P95 Latency above SLO (300ms)"
                description: "P95 latency is {{ $value }}s"
                runbook_url: "https://runbooks.diyapp.com/api-latency"
            },
            {
              alert: "LLMLatencyAboveSLO"
              expr: |-
                histogram_quantile(0.95, rate(llm_request_duration_seconds_bucket{job="diyapp"}[5m])) > 8
              for: "2m"
              labels:
                severity: "critical"
                squad: "sre"
              annotations:
                summary: "LLM P95 Latency above SLO (8s)"
                description: "LLM P95 latency is {{ $value }}s"
                runbook_url: "https://runbooks.diyapp.com/llm-latency"
            },
            {
              alert: "ErrorBudgetBurnRateHigh"
              expr: |-
                (
                  sum(rate(http_requests_total{status=~"5..", job="diyapp"}[1h]))
                  / sum(rate(http_requests_total{job="diyapp"}[1h]))
                ) > (0.001 * 2)
              for: "5m"
              labels:
                severity: "critical"
                squad: "sre"
              annotations:
                summary: "Error budget burn rate 2x faster than allowed"
                description: "Burn rate is {{ $value }}. Error budget will be exhausted in {{ $value / 0.001 }} hours at this rate."
                runbook_url: "https://runbooks.diyapp.com/error-budget-burn"
            }
          ]
        }
      ]
    }
  }
}

# Configuração de Grafana Dashboard via ConfigMap
resource "kubernetes_config_map" "grafana_dashboard_diyapp" {
  metadata {
    name      = "diyapp-dashboard"
    namespace = "monitoring"
    labels = {
      grafana_dashboard = "1"
    }
  }

  data = {
    "diyapp-slo-dashboard.json" = jsonencode({
      "dashboard" = {
        "title" = "DIYAPP SLO Dashboard",
        "panels" = [
          {
            "title" = "Error Rate vs SLO",
            "type" = "graph",
            "targets" = [
              {
                "expr" = "sum(rate(http_requests_total{status=~'5..', job='diyapp'}[5m])) / sum(rate(http_requests_total{job='diyapp'}[5m]))",
                "legendFormat" = "Error Rate"
              },
              {
                "expr" = "0.001",
                "legendFormat" = "SLO (0.1%)"
              }
            ],
            "thresholds" = [
              {
                "value" = 0.001,
                "color" = "red"
              }
            ]
          },
          {
            "title" = "Error Budget Remaining",
            "type" = "stat",
            "targets" = [
              {
                "expr" = "1 - ((sum(increase(http_requests_total{status=~'5..', job='diyapp'}[30d])) / 0.001) / sum(increase(http_requests_total{job='diyapp'}[30d])))",
                "format" = "percentunit"
              }
            ],
            "thresholds" = {
              "steps" = [
                {"color" = "red", "value" = 0.2},
                {"color" = "yellow", "value" = 0.5},
                {"color" = "green", "value" = 0}
              ]
            }
          }
        ]
      }
    })
  }
}

  version    = "5.0.2"

  }

  set {
    name  = "configuration.backupStorageLocation.name"
    value = "aws"
  }

    name  = "configuration.backupStorageLocation.bucket"
    value = module.backup.backup_bucket_name
  }

    name  = "configuration.backupStorageLocation.config.region"
    value = var.aws_region
  }

  set {
    name  = "configuration.volumeSnapshotLocation.name"
    value = "aws"
  }

  set {
    name  = "configuration.volumeSnapshotLocation.config.region"
    value = var.aws_region
  }

  set {
    name  = "initContainers[0].name"
    value = "velero-plugin-for-aws"

  set {

    name  = "initContainers[0].volumeMounts[0].mountPath"
    value = "/target"

  set {
    name  = "initContainers[0].volumeMounts[0].name"
    value = "plugins"
  }

  set {
    name  = "credentials.existingSecret"
    value = "velero-aws-credentials"
  }

  set {
    name  = "schedules.daily-backup.schedule"
    value = "0 2 * * *"
  }

  set {
    name  = "schedules.daily-backup.template.ttl"
    value = "720h"
  }

  set {
    name  = "schedules.daily-backup.template.includedNamespaces[0]"
    value = "default"
  }

  set {
    name  = "schedules.daily-backup.template.includedNamespaces[1]"
    value = "monitoring"
  }
}
