### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
```yaml
# ADR-001: Arquitetura de Microsserviços e Observabilidade
# Arquivo: architecture/decisions/ADR-001-microsservices-observability.md

---
# Architecture Decision Record

## ADR-001: Arquitetura de Microsserviços com Observabilidade Nativa

**Data**: 2024-01-15
**Status**: Aceita
**Autores**: Tech Lead, Especialista Infra, Especialista Segurança

### CONTEXTO
O DIYAPP evoluiu para uma plataforma complexa com múltiplos componentes que precisam:
1. Escalar independentemente
2. Ser implantados e atualizados sem downtime
3. Ter visibilidade completa do sistema em produção
4. Manter estabilidade 100% autônoma
5. Permitir refatoração paralela usando Modo Hive

### DECISÃO
Adotar arquitetura de microsserviços baseada em containers com:
1. **Orquestração**: Kubernetes com Helm charts
2. **Service Mesh**: Istio para comunicação entre serviços
3. **Observabilidade**: OpenTelemetry + Prometheus + Grafana stack
4. **Logs**: Estruturação JSON com contexto distribuído
5. **CI/CD**: GitOps com ArgoCD e pipelines multi-estágio

### OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS

**Opção A: Monólito Modular**
- Prós: Simplicidade inicial, debugging mais fácil
- Contras: Escalabilidade limitada, acoplamento alto, dificulta refatoração paralela

**Opção B: Microsserviços Leves (Serverless)**
- Prós: Escalabilidade automática, custo variável
- Contras: Vendor lock-in, cold starts, debugging distribuído complexo

**Opção C: Microsserviços Containerizados (ESCOLHIDA)**
- Prós: Escala independente, deploy isolado, portabilidade, observabilidade nativa
- Contras: Complexidade operacional, necessidade de service mesh

### CONSEQUÊNCIAS
**Positivas**:
- Cada squad pode desenvolver e deployar independentemente
- Isolamento de falhas entre serviços
- Observabilidade granular por serviço
- Refatoração paralela possível com Modo Hive

**Negativas**:
- Overhead de rede entre serviços
- Complexidade aumentada em testes E2E
- Necessidade de expertise em Kubernetes

**Riscos**:
1. **Latência de rede**: Mitigação com cache Redis e connection pooling
2. **Consistência de dados**: Mitigação com padrão Saga e compensações
3. **Complexidade operacional**: Mitigação com automação completa via GitOps

### REVISÃO
Reavaliar em 6 meses (2024-07-15) ou após 50% de crescimento de tráfego
```

```yaml
# Engineering Standards - Arquitetura e Observabilidade
# Arquivo: docs/engineering-standards.md

---
# Engineering Standards - DIYAPP V10

## 1. Padrões de Código

### 1.1 Estrutura de Microsserviço
```
service-name/
├── src/
│   ├── api/           # Controladores e rotas
│   ├── domain/        # Lógica de negócio
│   ├── infrastructure/# Repositórios, clients externos
│   ├── shared/        # Utilitários compartilhados
│   └── main.ts        # Ponto de entrada
├── tests/
│   ├── unit/          # Testes unitários
│   ├── integration/   # Testes de integração
│   └── e2e/           # Testes end-to-end
├── Dockerfile
├── helm/              # Templates Helm
├── docker-compose.yml # Para desenvolvimento
└── package.json
```

### 1.2 Convenções de Nomenclatura
- **Serviços**: `kebab-case` (ex: `user-service`, `payment-service`)
- **Variáveis**: `camelCase`
- **Classes**: `PascalCase`
- **Constantes**: `UPPER_SNAKE_CASE`
- **Interfaces**: Prefixo `I` (ex: `IUserRepository`)

### 1.3 Padrões de Commit
```
<type>(<scope>): <subject>

<body>

<footer>
```

**Types**: `feat`, `fix`, `docs`, `style`, `refactor`, `test`, `chore`
**Scope**: Nome do microsserviço ou `shared` para libs compartilhadas

## 2. Observabilidade

### 2.1 Logs Estruturados
```typescript
// Padrão obrigatório para todos os logs
interface StructuredLog {
  timestamp: string;      // ISO 8601
  level: 'DEBUG' | 'INFO' | 'WARN' | 'ERROR';
  service: string;        // Nome do serviço
  traceId: string;        // ID do trace distribuído
  spanId: string;         // ID do span atual
  message: string;        // Mensagem descritiva
  context: Record<string, any>; // Contexto adicional
  userId?: string;        // ID do usuário (se aplicável)
  requestId?: string;     // ID da requisição HTTP
}

// Exemplo de uso
logger.info('Processando pagamento', {
  context: {
    paymentId: 'pay_123',
    amount: 99.90,
    currency: 'BRL'
  },
  userId: 'user_456',
  traceId: span.context().traceId
});
```

### 2.2 OpenTelemetry Configuration
```yaml
# opentelemetry-config.yaml
instrumentation:
  http:
    enabled: true
    ignoreIncomingPaths:
      - /health
      - /metrics
  grpc:
    enabled: true
  redis:
    enabled: true
  postgres:
    enabled: true

exporters:
  jaeger:
    endpoint: "jaeger-collector:14250"
    enabled: true
  prometheus:
    port: 9464
    enabled: true

sampling:
  probability: 0.1  # 10% das requisições
```

### 2.3 Métricas Obrigatórias
Cada serviço DEVE expor:
- `http_server_duration_seconds` (histogram)
- `http_server_requests_total` (counter)
- `service_error_total` (counter por tipo de erro)
- `service_processing_duration_seconds` (histogram)
- `queue_size_current` (para serviços com filas)

## 3. Template de Microsserviço

```typescript
// Arquivo: templates/service-template/src/main.ts
import express from 'express';
import { trace, context, SpanStatusCode } from '@opentelemetry/api';
import { logger } from './shared/logger';
import { metrics } from './shared/metrics';
import { errorHandler } from './shared/error-handler';
import { requestIdMiddleware } from './shared/middleware';

const app = express();
const PORT = process.env.PORT || 3000;

// Middlewares obrigatórios
app.use(requestIdMiddleware);
app.use(express.json());

// Health check (obrigatório)
app.get('/health', (req, res) => {
  res.json({
    status: 'healthy',
    service: process.env.SERVICE_NAME,
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
    uptime: process.uptime()
  });
});

// Metrics endpoint (obrigatório)
app.get('/metrics', async (req, res) => {
  res.set('Content-Type', 'text/plain');
  res.end(await metrics.register.metrics());
});

// Rota de exemplo com tracing
app.get('/api/:id', async (req, res, next) => {
  const tracer = trace.getTracer('default');
  const span = tracer.startSpan('process_request');
  
  try {
    const contextWithSpan = trace.setSpan(context.active(), span);
    
    await context.with(contextWithSpan, async () => {
      logger.info('Processando requisição', {
        context: { id: req.params.id },
        requestId: req.headers['x-request-id']
      });
      
      // Lógica do serviço
      const result = await processBusinessLogic(req.params.id);
      
      span.setStatus({ code: SpanStatusCode.OK });
      res.json(result);
    });
  } catch (error) {
    span.setStatus({
      code: SpanStatusCode.ERROR,
      message: error.message
    });
    span.recordException(error);
    next(error);
  } finally {
    span.end();
  }
});

// Error handler (obrigatório)
app.use(errorHandler);

app.listen(PORT, () => {
  logger.info(`Serviço ${process.env.SERVICE_NAME} iniciado`, {
    context: { port: PORT, nodeEnv: process.env.NODE_ENV }
  });
});
```

## 4. Dockerfile Padrão

```dockerfile
# Arquivo: templates/service-template/Dockerfile
FROM node:18-alpine AS builder

WORKDIR /app

# Instala dependências de build
RUN apk add --no-cache python3 make g++

# Copia arquivos de dependências
COPY package*.json ./
COPY tsconfig.json ./

# Instala dependências
RUN npm ci --only=production && npm cache clean --force

# Copia código fonte
COPY src/ ./src/

# Build
RUN npm run build

# Runtime image
FROM node:18-alpine

WORKDIR /app

# Instala runtime dependencies
RUN apk add --no-cache tini curl

# Copia node_modules e build do builder
COPY --from=builder /app/node_modules ./node_modules
COPY --from=builder /app/dist ./dist

# Copia arquivos de configuração
COPY package.json ./
COPY opentelemetry-config.yaml ./

# Cria usuário não-root
RUN addgroup -g 1001 -S nodejs && \
    adduser -S nodejs -u 1001 && \
    chown -R nodejs:nodejs /app

USER nodejs

# Health check
HEALTHCHECK --interval=30s --timeout=3s --start-period=5s --retries=3 \
  CMD curl -f http://localhost:3000/health || exit 1

# Entrypoint com Tini para signal handling
ENTRYPOINT ["/sbin/tini", "--"]

# Comando de inicialização com OpenTelemetry
CMD ["node", "-r", "./dist/shared/tracing.js", "./dist/main.js"]

EXPOSE 3000
```

## 5. Pipeline CI/CD

```yaml
# Arquivo: .github/workflows/pipeline.yml
name: CI/CD Pipeline

on:
  push:
    branches: [ main, develop ]
  pull_request:
    branches: [ main ]

env:
  REGISTRY: ghcr.io
  IMAGE_NAME: ${{ github.repository }}

jobs:
  quality-gate:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3
      
      - name: Setup Node.js
        uses: actions/setup-node@v3
        with:
          node-version: '18'
          cache: 'npm'
      
      - name: Install dependencies
        run: npm ci
      
      - name: Lint
        run: npm run lint
      
      - name: Type check
        run: npm run type-check
      
      - name: Unit tests
        run: npm test -- --coverage
      
      - name: Upload coverage
        uses: codecov/codecov-action@v3
        with:
          file: ./coverage/lcov.info
          fail_ci_if_error: true

  security-scan:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3
      
      - name: Run Snyk to check for vulnerabilities
        uses: snyk/actions/node@master
        env:
          SNYK_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.SNYK_TOKEN }}
        with:
          args: --severity-threshold=high
      
      - name: Run Trivy vulnerability scanner
        uses: aquasecurity/trivy-action@master
        with:
          scan-type: 'fs'
          scan-ref: '.'
          format: 'sarif'
          output: 'trivy-results.sarif'
      
      - name: Upload Trivy scan results to GitHub Security tab
        uses: github/codeql-action/upload-sarif@v2
        with:
          sarif_file: 'trivy-results.sarif'

  build-and-push:
    needs: [quality-gate, security-scan]
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    if: github.event_name == 'push' && github.ref == 'refs/heads/main'
    
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3
      
      - name: Set up Docker Buildx
        uses: docker/setup-buildx-action@v2
      
      - name: Log in to Container Registry
        uses: docker/login-action@v2
        with:
          registry: ${{ env.REGISTRY }}
          username: ${{ github.actor }}
          password: ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
      
      - name: Extract metadata
        id: meta
        uses: docker/metadata-action@v4
        with:
          images: ${{ env.REGISTRY }}/${{ env.IMAGE_NAME }}
          tags: |
            type=sha,prefix={{branch}}-
            type=ref,event=branch
            type=ref,event=pr
            type=semver,pattern={{version}}
            type=semver,pattern={{major}}.{{minor}}
      
      - name: Build and push
        uses: docker/build-push-action@v4
        with:
          context: .
          push: true
          tags: ${{ steps.meta.outputs.tags }}
          labels: ${{ steps.meta.outputs.labels }}
          cache-from: type=gha
          cache-to: type=gha,mode=max

  deploy-staging:
    needs: build-and-push
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    environment: staging
    
    steps:
      - name: Deploy to Staging
        run: |
          echo "Deploying to staging..."
          # Aqui viria o comando para atualizar o ArgoCD
          # ou aplicar os manifests Kubernetes
        env:
          KUBECONFIG: ${{ secrets.KUBECONFIG_STAGING }}

  integration-tests:
    needs: deploy-staging
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    environment: staging
    
    steps:
      - name: Run integration tests
        run: |
          npm run test:integration
          # Testes contra o ambiente de staging
        env:
          API_URL: ${{ secrets.STAGING_API_URL }}

  deploy-production:
    needs: integration-tests
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    environment: production
    if: github.ref == 'refs/heads/main'
    
    steps:
      - name: Approve production deployment
        uses: trstringer/manual-approval@v1
        with:
          secret: ${{ github.token }}
          approvers: ${{ vars.PRODUCTION_APPROVERS }}
          minimum-approvals: 2
          issue-title: "Approve production deployment"
          issue-body: "Please review and approve this deployment"
      
      - name: Deploy to Production
        run: |
          echo "Deploying to production..."
          # Rollout progressivo com Istio
          kubectl apply -f k8s/production/
        env:
          KUBECONFIG: ${{ secrets.KUBECONFIG_PRODUCTION }}
```

## 6. Helm Chart Template

```yaml
# Arquivo: templates/service-template/helm/templates/deployment.yaml
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: {{ include "service.fullname" . }}
  labels:
    {{- include "service.labels" . | nindent 4 }}
    app.kubernetes.io/component: api
spec:
  replicas: {{ .Values.replicaCount }}
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      {{- include "service.selectorLabels" . | nindent 6 }}
  strategy:
    type: RollingUpdate
    rollingUpdate:
      maxSurge: {{ .Values.strategy.rollingUpdate.maxSurge }}
      maxUnavailable: {{ .Values.strategy.rollingUpdate.maxUnavailable }}
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        {{- include "service.selectorLabels" . | nindent 8 }}
        version: {{ .Chart.AppVersion }}
      annotations:
        prometheus.io/scrape: "true"
        prometheus.io/port: "9464"
        prometheus.io/path: "/metrics"
    spec:
      serviceAccountName: {{ include "service.serviceAccountName" . }}
      securityContext:
        {{- toYaml .Values.podSecurityContext | nindent 8 }}
      containers:
        - name: {{ .Chart.Name }}
          securityContext:
            {{- toYaml .Values.securityContext | nindent 12 }}
          image: "{{ .Values.image.repository }}:{{ .Values.image.tag | default .Chart.AppVersion }}"
          imagePullPolicy: {{ .Values.image.pullPolicy }}
          ports:
            - name: http
              containerPort: 3000
              protocol: TCP
            - name: metrics
              containerPort: 9464
              protocol: TCP
          env:
            - name: NODE_ENV
              value: {{ .Values.env.nodeEnv }}
            - name: SERVICE_NAME
              value: {{ include "service.fullname" . }}
            - name: OTEL_SERVICE_NAME
              value: {{ include "service.fullname" . }}
            - name: OTEL_EXPORTER_JAEGER_ENDPOINT
              value: {{ .Values.env.otel.jaegerEndpoint }}
            - name: OTEL_EXPORTER_PROMETHEUS_PORT
              value: "9464"
          resources:
            {{- toYaml .Values.resources | nindent 12 }}
          livenessProbe:
            httpGet:
              path: /health
              port: http
            initialDelaySeconds: 30
            periodSeconds: 10
            timeoutSeconds: 5
            failureThreshold: 3
          readinessProbe:
            httpGet:
              path: /health
              port: http

## 2. Componentes de Botões (components/buttons.css)

```css
/* ===== BOTÕES BASE ===== */
.btn {
  display: inline-flex;
  align-items: center;
  justify-content: center;
  gap: var(--spacing-2);
  font-family: var(--font-family-sans);
  font-weight: var(--font-weight-medium);
  font-size: var(--font-size-sm);
  line-height: var(--line-height-normal);
  padding: var(--spacing-2) var(--spacing-4);
  border-radius: var(--radius-md);
  border: 1px solid transparent;
  cursor: pointer;
  transition: all var(--transition-fast);
  outline: 2px solid transparent;
  outline-offset: 2px;
  position: relative;
  overflow: hidden;
}

.btn:focus-visible {
  outline: 2px solid var(--color-primary-500);
  outline-offset: 2px;
}

.btn:disabled {
  opacity: 0.5;
  cursor: not-allowed;
  pointer-events: none;
}

/* ===== BOTÃO PRIMÁRIO ===== */
.btn-primary {
  background-color: var(--color-primary-600);
  color: white;
}

.btn-primary:hover:not(:disabled) {
  background-color: var(--color-primary-700);
  transform: translateY(-1px);
  box-shadow: var(--shadow-md);
}

.btn-primary:active:not(:disabled) {
  background-color: var(--color-primary-800);
  transform: translateY(0);
}

.btn-primary.loading::after {
  content: '';
  position: absolute;
  width: 16px;
  height: 16px;
  border: 2px solid rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.3);

  border-radius: 50%;

}

  to { transform: rotate(360deg); }
}

  50% { opacity: 0.5; }
}

}

## 3. Componentes de Formulários (components/forms.css)

```css
/* ===== GRUPO DE FORMULÁRIO ===== */
.form-group {
  margin-bottom: var(--spacing-4);
}

### [Sessão Paralela: Backend]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Serviços Backend

Vou implementar os serviços core com foco em estabilidade, observabilidade e resiliência. Vou estruturar em três serviços principais com API Gateway.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v10-core/
├── packages/
│   ├── api-gateway/
│   ├── auth-service/
│   ├── project-service/
│   └── shared/
├── docker-compose.yml
├── package.json
└── README.md
```

## 1. Configuração Inicial (Root)

**package.json**
```json
{
  "name": "diyapp-v10-core",
  "version": "1.0.0",
  "private": true,
  "workspaces": [
    "packages/*"
  ],
  "scripts": {
    "dev": "concurrently \"npm run dev --workspace=api-gateway\" \"npm run dev --workspace=auth-service\" \"npm run dev --workspace=project-service\"",
    "build": "npm run build --workspaces",
    "test": "npm run test --workspaces",
    "lint": "npm run lint --workspaces",
    "docker:up": "docker-compose up -d",
    "docker:down": "docker-compose down",
    "migrate:up": "npm run migrate:up --workspaces",
    "migrate:down": "npm run migrate:down --workspaces"
  },
  "devDependencies": {
    "concurrently": "^8.2.2",
    "typescript": "^5.3.3",
    "@types/node": "^20.10.5"
  }
}
```

**docker-compose.yml**
```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  postgres:
    image: postgres:15-alpine
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: diyapp
      POSTGRES_USER: diyapp
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: diyapp_password
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
      - ./init-db:/docker-entrypoint-initdb.d
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U diyapp"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"
    volumes:
      - redis_data:/data
    command: redis-server --appendonly yes
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "redis-cli", "ping"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  auth-service:
    build:
      context: ./packages/auth-service
      dockerfile: Dockerfile
    environment:
      NODE_ENV: production
      DATABASE_URL: postgresql://diyapp:diyapp_password@postgres:5432/diyapp
      REDIS_URL: redis://redis:6379
      JWT_SECRET: ${JWT_SECRET:-your-super-secret-jwt-key-change-in-production}
      PORT: 3001
    ports:
      - "3001:3001"
    depends_on:
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
    restart: unless-stopped

  project-service:
    build:
      context: ./packages/project-service
      dockerfile: Dockerfile
    environment:
      NODE_ENV: production
      DATABASE_URL: postgresql://diyapp:diyapp_password@postgres:5432/diyapp
      REDIS_URL: redis://redis:6379
      PORT: 3002
    ports:
      - "3002:3002"
    depends_on:
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
    restart: unless-stopped

  api-gateway:
    build:
      context: ./packages/api-gateway
      dockerfile: Dockerfile
    environment:
      NODE_ENV: production
      AUTH_SERVICE_URL: http://auth-service:3001
      PROJECT_SERVICE_URL: http://project-service:3002
      PORT: 3000
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    depends_on:
      - auth-service
      - project-service
    restart: unless-stopped

volumes:
  postgres_data:
  redis_data:
```

**packages/shared/src/utils/logger.ts**
```typescript
import winston from 'winston';
import { v4 as uuidv4 } from 'uuid';

const { combine, timestamp, json, errors } = winston.format;

class Logger {
  private logger: winston.Logger;
  private correlationId: string;

  constructor() {
    this.correlationId = uuidv4();
    
    this.logger = winston.createLogger({
      level: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production' ? 'info' : 'debug',
      format: combine(
        errors({ stack: true }),
        timestamp(),
        json()
      ),
      defaultMeta: { service: 'diyapp-core', correlation_id: this.correlationId },
      transports: [
        new winston.transports.Console(),
        new winston.transports.File({ 
          filename: 'logs/error.log', 
          level: 'error',
          maxsize: 5242880, // 5MB
          maxFiles: 5,
        }),
        new winston.transports.File({ 
          filename: 'logs/combined.log',
          maxsize: 5242880,
          maxFiles: 5,
        }),
      ],
    });
  }

  setCorrelationId(id: string) {
    this.correlationId = id;
    this.logger.defaultMeta = { 
      ...this.logger.defaultMeta, 
      correlation_id: id 
    };
  }

  info(message: string, meta?: Record<string, any>) {
    this.logger.info(message, meta);
  }

  error(message: string, error?: Error, meta?: Record<string, any>) {
    this.logger.error(message, { error, ...meta });
  }

  warn(message: string, meta?: Record<string, any>) {
    this.logger.warn(message, meta);
  }

  debug(message: string, meta?: Record<string, any>) {
    this.logger.debug(message, meta);
  }

  http(message: string, meta?: Record<string, any>) {
    this.logger.http(message, meta);
  }
}

export const logger = new Logger();
```

**packages/shared/src/utils/validation.ts**
```typescript
import Joi from 'joi';

export const authSchemas = {
  register: Joi.object({
    email: Joi.string().email().required(),
    password: Joi.string().min(8).required(),
    name: Joi.string().min(2).required(),
  }),

  login: Joi.object({
    email: Joi.string().email().required(),
    password: Joi.string().required(),
  }),

  refreshToken: Joi.object({
    refreshToken: Joi.string().required(),
  }),
};

export const projectSchemas = {
  create: Joi.object({
    name: Joi.string().min(3).max(100).required(),
    description: Joi.string().max(500).optional(),
    status: Joi.string().valid('draft', 'active', 'completed', 'archived').optional(),
    metadata: Joi.object().optional(),
  }),

  update: Joi.object({
    name: Joi.string().min(3).max(100).optional(),
    description: Joi.string().max(500).optional(),
    status: Joi.string().valid('draft', 'active', 'completed', 'archived').optional(),
    metadata: Joi.object().optional(),
  }),

  list: Joi.object({
    page: Joi.number().min(1).default(1),
    limit: Joi.number().min(1).max(100).default(20),
    status: Joi.string().valid('draft', 'active', 'completed', 'archived').optional(),
    search: Joi.string().optional(),
  }),
};

export const validate = (schema: Joi.Schema, data: any) => {
  const { error, value } = schema.validate(data, {
    abortEarly: false,
    stripUnknown: true,
  });

  if (error) {
    throw new Error(`Validation error: ${error.details.map(d => d.message).join(', ')}`);
  }

  return value;
};
```

**packages/shared/src/utils/security.ts**
```typescript
import bcrypt from 'bcryptjs';
import jwt from 'jsonwebtoken';
import { JwtPayload } from '../types';

export class SecurityUtils {
  private static readonly SALT_ROUNDS = 10;
  private static readonly JWT_SECRET = process.env.JWT_SECRET || 'your-super-secret-jwt-key-change-in-production';
  private static readonly ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRY = '15m';
  private static readonly REFRESH_TOKEN_EXPIRY = '7d';

  static async hashPassword(password: string): Promise<string> {
    return bcrypt.hash(password, this.SALT_ROUNDS);
  }

  static async verifyPassword(password: string, hash: string): Promise<boolean> {
    return bcrypt.compare(password, hash);
  }

  static generateAccessToken(payload: { userId: string; email: string; role: string }): string {
    return jwt.sign(payload, this.JWT_SECRET, { expiresIn: this.ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRY });
  }

  static generateRefreshToken(payload: { userId: string; email: string; role: string }): string {
    return jwt.sign(payload, this.JWT_SECRET, { expiresIn: this.REFRESH_TOKEN_EXPIRY });
  }

  static verifyToken(token: string): JwtPayload {
    try {
      return jwt.verify(token, this.JWT_SECRET) as JwtPayload;
    } catch (error) {
      throw new Error('Invalid or expired token');
    }
  }

  static maskSensitiveData(data: string): string {
    if (!data || data.length < 4) return '***';
    return data.substring(0, 2) + '***' + data.substring(data.length - 2);
  }

  static sanitizeForLogs(data: any): any {
    if (typeof data !== 'object' || data === null) return data;

    const sensitiveFields = ['password', 'token', 'refreshToken', 'authorization', 'cardNumber', 'cvv', 'cpf', 'ssn'];
    const sanitized = { ...data };

    for (const field of sensitiveFields) {
      if (sanitized[field]) {
        sanitized[field] = this.maskSensitiveData(String(sanitized[field]));
      }
    }

    return sanitized;
  }
}
```

**packages/shared/src/utils/cache.ts**
```typescript
import { createClient, RedisClientType } from 'redis';
import { logger } from './logger';

export class CacheService {
  private client: RedisClientType;
  private isConnected = false;

  constructor() {
    const redisUrl = process.env.REDIS_URL || 'redis://localhost:6379';
    this.client = createClient({ url: redisUrl });

    this.client.on('error', (err) => {
      logger.error('Redis connection error', err);
      this.isConnected = false;
    });

    this.client.on('connect', () => {
      logger.info('Redis connected successfully');
      this.isConnected = true;
    });

    this.client.on('reconnecting', () => {
      logger.warn('Redis reconnecting...');
    });
  }

  async connect(): Promise<void> {
    if (!this.isConnected) {
      await this.client.connect();
    }
  }

  async disconnect(): Promise<void> {
    if (this.isConnected) {
      await this.client.quit();
      this.isConnected = false;
    }
  }

  async get<T>(key: string): Promise<T | null> {
    try {
      if (!this.isConnected) {
        await this.connect();
      }

      const data = await this.client.get(key);
      return data ? JSON.parse(data) : null;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error(`Cache get error for key: ${key}`, error as Error);
      return null;
    }
  }

  async set(key: string, value: any, ttlSeconds?: number): Promise<void> {
    try {
      if (!this.isConnected) {
        await this.connect();
      }

      const stringValue = JSON.stringify(value);
      
      if (ttlSeconds) {
        await this.client.setEx(key, ttlSeconds, stringValue);
      } else {
        await this.client.set(key, stringValue);
      }
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error(`Cache set error for key: ${key}`, error as Error);
    }
  }

  async delete(key: string): Promise<void> {
    try {
      if (!this.isConnected) {
        await this.connect();
      }

      await this.client.del(key);
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error(`Cache delete error for key: ${key}`, error as Error);
    }
  }

  async deletePattern(pattern: string): Promise<void> {
    try {
      if (!this.isConnected) {
        await this.connect();
      }

      const keys = await this.client.keys(pattern);
      if (keys.length > 0) {
        await this.client.del(keys);
      }
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error(`Cache delete pattern error: ${pattern}`, error as Error);
    }
  }

  async increment(key: string): Promise<number> {
    try {
      if (!this.isConnected) {
        await this.connect();
      }

      return await this.client.incr(key);
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error(`Cache increment error for key: ${key}`, error as Error);
      return 0;
    }
  }

  async withCache<T>(
    key: string,
    ttlSeconds: number,
    fallback: () => Promise<T>
  ): Promise<T> {
    const cached = await this.get<T>(key);
    if (cached !== null) {
      logger.debug(`Cache hit for key: ${key}`);
      return cached;
    }

    logger.debug(`Cache miss for key: ${key}`);
    const data = await fallback();
    await this.set(key, data, ttlSeconds);
    return data;
  }
}

export const cacheService = new CacheService();
```

**packages/shared/src/utils/resilience.ts**
```typescript
import { logger } from './logger';

export class CircuitBreaker {
  private failures = 0;
  private lastFailureTime = 0;
  private state: 'CLOSED' | 'OPEN' | 'HALF_OPEN' = 'CLOSED';
  private readonly failureThreshold: number;
  private readonly resetTimeout: number;
  private readonly name: string;

  constructor(name: string, failureThreshold = 5, resetTimeout = 60000) {
    this.name = name;
    this.failureThreshold = failureThreshold;
    this.resetTimeout = resetTimeout;
  }

  async execute<T>(fn: () => Promise<T>): Promise<T> {
    if (this.state === 'OPEN') {
      const now = Date.now();
      if (now - this.lastFailureTime > this.resetTimeout) {
        this.state = 'HALF_OPEN';
        logger.warn(`Circuit breaker ${this.name} transitioning to HALF_OPEN`);
      } else {
        throw new Error(`Circuit breaker ${this.name} is OPEN`);
      }
    }

    try {
      const result = await fn();
      
      if (this.state === 'HALF_OPEN') {
        this.reset();
      }
      
      return result;
    } catch (error) {
      this.recordFailure();
      throw error;
    }
  }

  private recordFailure(): void {
    this.failures++;
    this.lastFailureTime = Date.now();
    
    if (this.failures >= this.failureThreshold && this.state !== 'OPEN') {
      this.state = 'OPEN';
      logger.error(`Circuit breaker ${this.name} opened after ${this.failures} failures`);
    }
  }

  private reset(): void {
    this.failures = 0;
    this.state = 'CLOSED';
    logger.info(`Circuit breaker ${this.name} reset`);
  }

  getState(): string {
    return this.state;
  }
}

export async function retryWithBackoff<T>(


### [Sessão Paralela: Frontend]

```bash

### [Sessão Paralela: SRE]
```terraform
# ============================================
# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core
# Infrastructure as Code - AWS EKS Cluster
# SRE Senior: Provisioning for 100% Autonomous Stability
# ============================================

# ============================================
# 1. PROVIDER CONFIGURATION
# ============================================
terraform {
  required_version = ">= 1.5.0"
  
  required_providers {
    aws = {
      source  = "hashicorp/aws"
      version = "~> 5.0"
    }
    kubernetes = {
      source  = "hashicorp/kubernetes"
      version = "~> 2.23.0"
    }
    helm = {
      source  = "hashicorp/helm"
      version = "~> 2.11.0"
    }
    kubectl = {
      source  = "gavinbunney/kubectl"
      version = "~> 1.14.0"
    }
  }

  backend "s3" {
    bucket         = "diyapp-v10-tfstate"
    key            = "prod/terraform.tfstate"
    region         = "us-east-1"
    encrypt        = true
    dynamodb_table = "diyapp-v10-tfstate-lock"
  }
}

provider "aws" {
  region = var.aws_region
  default_tags {
    tags = {
      Project     = "DIYAPP-V10"
      Environment = var.environment
      ManagedBy   = "Terraform"
      Squad       = "Autonomous-Senior-Squad"
      SLO_Tier    = "99.9"
    }
  }
}

provider "kubernetes" {
  host                   = module.eks.cluster_endpoint
  cluster_ca_certificate = base64decode(module.eks.cluster_certificate_authority_data)
  token                  = data.aws_eks_cluster_auth.this.token
}

provider "helm" {
  kubernetes {
    host                   = module.eks.cluster_endpoint
    cluster_ca_certificate = base64decode(module.eks.cluster_certificate_authority_data)
    token                  = data.aws_eks_cluster_auth.this.token
  }
}

provider "kubectl" {
  apply_retry_count      = 3
  host                   = module.eks.cluster_endpoint
  cluster_ca_certificate = base64decode(module.eks.cluster_certificate_authority_data)
  token                  = data.aws_eks_cluster_auth.this.token
  load_config_file       = false
}

data "aws_eks_cluster_auth" "this" {
  name = module.eks.cluster_name
}

# ============================================
# 2. VARIABLES
# ============================================
variable "aws_region" {
  description = "AWS region"
  type        = string
  default     = "us-east-1"
}

variable "environment" {
  description = "Environment name"
  type        = string
  default     = "production"
}

variable "cluster_name" {
  description = "EKS cluster name"
  type        = string
  default     = "diyapp-v10-core"
}

variable "cluster_version" {
  description = "Kubernetes version"
  type        = string
  default     = "1.28"
}

variable "vpc_cidr" {
  description = "VPC CIDR block"
  type        = string
  default     = "10.0.0.0/16"
}

variable "slo_availability" {
  description = "SLO Availability target"
  type        = string
  default     = "99.9"
}

# ============================================
# 3. NETWORKING (VPC, SUBNETS, SECURITY)
# ============================================
module "vpc" {
  source  = "terraform-aws-modules/vpc/aws"
  version = "~> 5.0"

  name = "diyapp-v10-vpc"
  cidr = var.vpc_cidr

  azs             = ["${var.aws_region}a", "${var.aws_region}b", "${var.aws_region}c"]
  private_subnets = ["10.0.1.0/24", "10.0.2.0/24", "10.0.3.0/24"]
  public_subnets  = ["10.0.101.0/24", "10.0.102.0/24", "10.0.103.0/24"]

  enable_nat_gateway     = true
  single_nat_gateway     = false
  one_nat_gateway_per_az = true
  enable_dns_hostnames   = true
  enable_dns_support     = true

  public_subnet_tags = {
    "kubernetes.io/role/elb" = "1"
  }

  private_subnet_tags = {
    "kubernetes.io/role/internal-elb" = "1"
    "karpenter.sh/discovery"          = var.cluster_name
  }

  tags = {
    "karpenter.sh/discovery" = var.cluster_name
  }
}

# ============================================
# 4. EKS CLUSTER WITH MANAGED NODE GROUPS
# ============================================
module "eks" {
  source  = "terraform-aws-modules/eks/aws"
  version = "~> 19.0"

  cluster_name                   = var.cluster_name
  cluster_version                = var.cluster_version
  cluster_endpoint_public_access = true

  vpc_id     = module.vpc.vpc_id
  subnet_ids = module.vpc.private_subnets

  # EKS Managed Node Groups
  eks_managed_node_groups = {
    # System node group for critical system pods
    system = {
      name            = "system"
      use_name_prefix = true

      instance_types = ["t3.medium"]
      capacity_type  = "ON_DEMAND"

      min_size     = 2
      max_size     = 4
      desired_size = 2

      # SLO-based scaling policies
      scaling_config = {
        min_size         = 2
        max_size         = 4
        desired_capacity = 2
      }

      update_config = {
        max_unavailable_percentage = 33
      }

      labels = {
        role        = "system"
        dedicated   = "system"
        environment = var.environment
      }

      taints = {
        dedicated = {
          key    = "dedicated"
          value  = "system"
          effect = "NO_SCHEDULE"
        }
      }

      tags = {
        "k8s.io/cluster-autoscaler/enabled"               = "true"
        "k8s.io/cluster-autoscaler/${var.cluster_name}" = "owned"
      }
    }

    # Application node group for DIYAPP workloads
    app = {
      name            = "app"
      use_name_prefix = true

      instance_types = ["t3.large", "t3a.large"]
      capacity_type  = "SPOT"

      min_size     = 3
      max_size     = 10
      desired_size = 3

      # SLO-based scaling policies
      scaling_config = {
        min_size         = 3
        max_size         = 10
        desired_capacity = 3
      }

      update_config = {
        max_unavailable_percentage = 25
      }

      labels = {
        role        = "app"
        environment = var.environment
      }

      tags = {
        "k8s.io/cluster-autoscaler/enabled"               = "true"
        "k8s.io/cluster-autoscaler/${var.cluster_name}" = "owned"
      }
    }
  }

  # Cluster security group
  cluster_security_group_additional_rules = {
    ingress_nodes_443 = {
      description                = "Node groups to cluster API"
      protocol                   = "tcp"
      from_port                  = 443
      to_port                    = 443
      type                       = "ingress"
      source_node_security_group = true
    }
  }

  node_security_group_additional_rules = {
    ingress_self_all = {
      description = "Node to node all ports"
      protocol    = "-1"
      from_port   = 0
      to_port     = 0
      type        = "ingress"
      self        = true
    }
    egress_all = {
      description      = "Node all egress"
      protocol         = "-1"
      from_port        = 0
      to_port          = 0
      type             = "egress"
      cidr_blocks      = ["0.0.0.0/0"]
      ipv6_cidr_blocks = ["::/0"]
    }
  }

  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
    Project     = "DIYAPP-V10"
    SLO         = var.slo_availability
  }
}

# ============================================
# 5. KARPENTER FOR ADVANCED AUTOSCALING
# ============================================
module "karpenter" {
  source  = "terraform-aws-modules/eks/aws//modules/karpenter"
  version = "~> 19.0"

  cluster_name = module.eks.cluster_name

  # IAM Role for Karpenter
  create_iam_role = true
  iam_role_name   = "karpenter-controller-${var.cluster_name}"

  # Node IAM Role
  create_node_iam_role   = true
  node_iam_role_name     = "karpenter-node-${var.cluster_name}"
  node_iam_role_use_name_prefix = false

  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
    Project     = "DIYAPP-V10"
  }
}

resource "helm_release" "karpenter" {
  namespace        = "karpenter"
  create_namespace = true

  name       = "karpenter"
  repository = "https://charts.karpenter.sh"
  chart      = "karpenter"
  version    = "0.32.1"

  set {
    name  = "serviceAccount.annotations.eks\\.amazonaws\\.com/role-arn"
    value = module.karpenter.iam_role_arn
  }

  set {
    name  = "clusterName"
    value = module.eks.cluster_name
  }

  set {
    name  = "clusterEndpoint"
    value = module.eks.cluster_endpoint
  }

  set {
    name  = "aws.defaultInstanceProfile"
    value = module.karpenter.node_iam_role_name
  }

  values = [<<-YAML
    settings:
      clusterName: ${module.eks.cluster_name}
      interruptionQueueName: ${module.karpenter.queue_name}
    controller:
      resources:
        requests:
          cpu: 1
          memory: "1Gi"
        limits:
          cpu: 1
          memory: "1Gi"
    YAML
  ]

  depends_on = [module.eks]
}

# Karpenter Provisioner for SLO-based scaling
resource "kubectl_manifest" "karpenter_provisioner" {
  yaml_body = <<-YAML
  apiVersion: karpenter.sh/v1alpha5
  kind: Provisioner
  metadata:
    name: diyapp-slo-provisioner
  spec:
    requirements:
      - key: "karpenter.sh/capacity-type"
        operator: In
        values: ["spot", "on-demand"]
      - key: "node.kubernetes.io/instance-type"
        operator: In
        values: ["t3.large", "t3a.large", "t3.xlarge", "t3a.xlarge", "c6i.large", "c6a.large"]
      - key: "topology.kubernetes.io/zone"
        operator: In
        values: ${jsonencode(module.vpc.azs)}
      - key: "kubernetes.io/arch"
        operator: In
        values: ["amd64"]
    
    limits:
      resources:
        cpu: 100
        memory: 400Gi
    
    providerRef:
      name: diyapp-default
    
    ttlSecondsAfterEmpty: 60
    ttlSecondsUntilExpired: 604800
    
    labels:
      environment: ${var.environment}
      project: diyapp-v10
      slo-tier: ${var.slo_availability}
    
    annotations:
      scheduler.alpha.kubernetes.io/defaultTolerations: '[{"key":"dedicated","operator":"Equal","value":"system","effect":"NoSchedule"}]'
  YAML

  depends_on = [helm_release.karpenter]
}

resource "kubectl_manifest" "karpenter_node_template" {
  yaml_body = <<-YAML
  apiVersion: karpenter.k8s.aws/v1alpha1
  kind: AWSNodeTemplate
  metadata:
    name: diyapp-default
  spec:
    subnetSelector:
      karpenter.sh/discovery: ${var.cluster_name}
    securityGroupSelector:
      karpenter.sh/discovery: ${var.cluster_name}
    tags:
      Environment: ${var.environment}
      Project: DIYAPP-V10
      SLO: ${var.slo_availability}
      ManagedBy: Karpenter
    blockDeviceMappings:
      - deviceName: /dev/xvda
        ebs:
          volumeSize: 50Gi
          volumeType: gp3
          encrypted: true
          deleteOnTermination: true
  YAML

  depends_on = [helm_release.karpenter]
}

## 1. Configurações

### `config/database.js`
```javascript
module.exports = {
  postgres: {
    host: process.env.POSTGRES_HOST || 'localhost',
    port: process.env.POSTGRES_PORT || 5432,
    database: process.env.POSTGRES_DB || 'diyapp_v10',
    user: process.env.POSTGRES_USER || 'diyapp_user',
    password: process.env.POSTGRES_PASSWORD || 'secure_password',
    max: 20, // max number of clients in pool
    idleTimeoutMillis: 30000,
    connectionTimeoutMillis: 2000,
  },
  redis: {
    host: process.env.REDIS_HOST || 'localhost',
    port: process.env.REDIS_PORT || 6379,
    password: process.env.REDIS_PASSWORD || '',
    db: process.env.REDIS_DB || 0,
    keyPrefix: 'diyapp:v10:',
    ttl: {
      context: 86400, // 24 hours
      metrics: 300,   // 5 minutes
      session: 7200,  // 2 hours
    }
  }
};
```

### `config/redis.js`
```javascript
module.exports = {
  host: process.env.REDIS_HOST || 'localhost',
  port: process.env.REDIS_PORT || 6379,
  password: process.env.REDIS_PASSWORD || '',
  db: process.env.REDIS_DB || 0,
  retryStrategy: function(times) {
    const delay = Math.min(times * 50, 2000);
    return delay;
  },
  maxRetriesPerRequest: 3,
  enableReadyCheck: true,
  enableOfflineQueue: true,
};
```

## 2. Schema PostgreSQL

### `src/persistence/database/postgres/schema.sql`
```sql
-- =============================================
-- DIYAPP V10 Core - Persistence Schema
-- =============================================

-- Enable UUID extension
CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS "uuid-ossp";

-- =============================================
-- Table: execution_history
-- Purpose: Track all agent execution sessions
-- =============================================
CREATE TABLE execution_history (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    session_id VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    agent_id VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    agent_version VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
    squad_id VARCHAR(100),
    
    -- Execution context
    task_description TEXT NOT NULL,
    input_parameters JSONB,
    execution_context JSONB,
    
    -- Status tracking
    status VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL CHECK (status IN ('pending', 'running', 'completed', 'failed', 'cancelled')),
    start_time TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    end_time TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    duration_ms INTEGER,
    
    -- Results and outputs
    output_result JSONB,
    error_details JSONB,
    artifacts_generated TEXT[], -- Array of artifact paths/URLs
    
    -- Performance metadata
    token_count INTEGER,
    model_used VARCHAR(100),
    cost_estimate DECIMAL(10,6),
    
    -- System metadata
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    created_by VARCHAR(100),
    
    -- Indexes for common queries
    INDEX idx_execution_session_id (session_id),
    INDEX idx_execution_agent_id (agent_id),
    INDEX idx_execution_status (status),
    INDEX idx_execution_start_time (start_time DESC),
    INDEX idx_execution_squad_id (squad_id),
    INDEX idx_execution_created_at (created_at DESC)
);

-- =============================================
-- Table: performance_metrics
-- Purpose: Store granular performance metrics
-- =============================================
CREATE TABLE performance_metrics (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    execution_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES execution_history(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    metric_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL CHECK (metric_type IN (
        'latency', 'throughput', 'accuracy', 'cost', 
        'token_usage', 'cache_hit', 'error_rate', 'custom'
    )),
    
    -- Metric values
    metric_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    metric_value DECIMAL(15,6) NOT NULL,
    metric_unit VARCHAR(50),
    
    -- Context
    phase VARCHAR(50) CHECK (phase IN ('ingestion', 'processing', 'generation', 'validation', 'delivery')),
    component VARCHAR(100),
    
    -- Timing
    measured_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    time_window_start TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    time_window_end TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    
    -- Metadata
    tags JSONB,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    
    -- Indexes
    INDEX idx_metrics_execution_id (execution_id),
    INDEX idx_metrics_type (metric_type),
    INDEX idx_metrics_name (metric_name),
    INDEX idx_metrics_measured_at (measured_at DESC),
    INDEX idx_metrics_component (component),
    UNIQUE idx_unique_metric (execution_id, metric_type, metric_name, phase, component, measured_at)
);

-- =============================================
-- Table: session_context
-- Purpose: Cache context between sessions
-- =============================================
CREATE TABLE session_context (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    context_key VARCHAR(500) NOT NULL,
    context_hash VARCHAR(64) NOT NULL, -- SHA-256 hash of the key
    
    -- Context data
    context_data JSONB NOT NULL,
    context_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL CHECK (context_type IN (
        'conversation', 'task', 'agent_state', 'environment', 'user_preferences', 'custom'
    )),
    
    -- Ownership and scope
    agent_id VARCHAR(100),
    squad_id VARCHAR(100),
    user_id VARCHAR(100),
    session_id VARCHAR(255),
    
    -- Validity and freshness
    is_active BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT TRUE,
    ttl_seconds INTEGER, -- Time to live in seconds
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    last_accessed_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    expires_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    
    -- Usage statistics
    access_count INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    hit_count INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Metadata
    metadata JSONB,
    version INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
    
    -- Indexes
    INDEX idx_context_key_hash (context_hash),
    INDEX idx_context_agent_id (agent_id),
    INDEX idx_context_squad_id (squad_id),
    INDEX idx_context_user_id (user_id),
    INDEX idx_context_session_id (session_id),
    INDEX idx_context_type (context_type),
    INDEX idx_context_is_active (is_active),
    INDEX idx_context_expires_at (expires_at),
    INDEX idx_context_last_accessed (last_accessed_at DESC),
    UNIQUE idx_unique_context (context_hash, agent_id, squad_id, user_id, session_id)
);

-- =============================================
-- Table: agent_squad_mapping
-- Purpose: Track agent-squad relationships
-- =============================================
CREATE TABLE agent_squad_mapping (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    agent_id VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    squad_id VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    role VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    is_active BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT TRUE,
    joined_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    left_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    
    -- Indexes
    INDEX idx_mapping_agent_id (agent_id),
    INDEX idx_mapping_squad_id (squad_id),
    INDEX idx_mapping_active (is_active),
    UNIQUE idx_unique_active_mapping (agent_id, squad_id) WHERE is_active = TRUE
);

-- =============================================
-- Table: data_quality_metrics
-- Purpose: Track data quality for pipeline monitoring
-- =============================================
CREATE TABLE data_quality_metrics (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    pipeline_id VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    pipeline_name VARCHAR(200) NOT NULL,
    
    -- Quality dimensions
    completeness DECIMAL(5,2) CHECK (completeness >= 0 AND completeness <= 100),
    uniqueness DECIMAL(5,2) CHECK (uniqueness >= 0 AND uniqueness <= 100),
    validity DECIMAL(5,2) CHECK (validity >= 0 AND validity <= 100),
    consistency DECIMAL(5,2) CHECK (consistency >= 0 AND consistency <= 100),
    timeliness DECIMAL(5,2) CHECK (timeliness >= 0 AND timeliness <= 100),
    
    -- Count metrics
    total_records BIGINT,
    valid_records BIGINT,
    invalid_records BIGINT,
    duplicate_count BIGINT,
    
    -- Timing
    measured_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    time_window_start TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE NOT NULL,
    time_window_end TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE NOT NULL,
    
    -- Status
    sla_status VARCHAR(20) CHECK (sla_status IN ('met', 'warning', 'violated')),
    alert_triggered BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    
    -- Details
    details JSONB,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    
    -- Indexes
    INDEX idx_quality_pipeline_id (pipeline_id),
    INDEX idx_quality_measured_at (measured_at DESC),
    INDEX idx_quality_sla_status (sla_status),
    INDEX idx_quality_window (time_window_start, time_window_end)
);

-- =============================================
-- Functions and Triggers
-- =============================================

-- Function to update updated_at timestamp
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column()
RETURNS TRIGGER AS $$
BEGIN
    NEW.updated_at = NOW();
    RETURN NEW;
END;
$$ language 'plpgsql';

-- Triggers for updated_at
CREATE TRIGGER update_execution_history_updated_at 
    BEFORE UPDATE ON execution_history 
    FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();

CREATE TRIGGER update_session_context_updated_at 
    BEFORE UPDATE ON session_context 
    FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();

-- Function to update last_accessed_at
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION update_last_accessed_at()
RETURNS TRIGGER AS $$
BEGIN
    NEW.last_accessed_at = NOW();
    NEW.access_count = NEW.access_count + 1;
    RETURN NEW;
END;
$$ language 'plpgsql';

CREATE TRIGGER update_session_context_access 
    BEFORE UPDATE ON session_context 
    FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION update_last_accessed_at();

-- Function to calculate and set expires_at
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION set_context_expiry()
RETURNS TRIGGER AS $$
BEGIN
    IF NEW.ttl_seconds IS NOT NULL THEN
        NEW.expires_at = NEW.created_at + (NEW.ttl_seconds || ' seconds')::INTERVAL;
    END IF;
    RETURN NEW;
END;
$$ language 'plpgsql';

CREATE TRIGGER set_session_context_expiry 
    BEFORE INSERT ON session_context 
    FOR EACH ROW EXECUTE FUNCTION set_context_expiry();

-- Function to clean up expired contexts
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION cleanup_expired_contexts()
RETURNS VOID AS $$
BEGIN
    UPDATE session_context 
    SET is_active = FALSE 
    WHERE expires_at < NOW() 
    AND is_active = TRUE;
END;
$$ language 'plpgsql';

-- =============================================
-- Views for common queries
-- =============================================

-- View for execution summary
CREATE VIEW execution_summary AS
SELECT 
    eh.id,
    eh.session_id,
    eh.agent_id,
    eh.squad_id,
    eh.status,
    eh.start_time,
    eh.end_time,
    eh.duration_ms,
    eh.token_count,
    eh.cost_estimate,
    COUNT(pm.id) as metric_count,
    AVG(CASE WHEN pm.metric_type = 'latency' THEN pm.metric_value END) as avg_latency,
    AVG(CASE WHEN pm.metric_type = 'accuracy' THEN pm.metric_value END) as avg_accuracy
FROM execution_history eh
LEFT JOIN performance_metrics pm ON eh.id = pm.execution_id
GROUP BY eh.id, eh.session_id, eh.agent_id, eh.squad_id, eh.status, 
         eh.start_time, eh.end_time, eh.duration_ms, eh.token_count, eh.cost_estimate;

-- View for squad performance
CREATE VIEW squad_performance AS
SELECT 
    squad_id,
    COUNT(DISTINCT id) as total_executions,
    COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN status = 'completed' THEN id END) as successful_executions,
    COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN status = 'failed' THEN id END) as failed_executions,
    AVG(duration_ms) as avg_duration_ms,
    SUM(token_count) as total_tokens,
    SUM(cost_estimate) as total_cost,
    MIN(start_time) as first_execution,
    MAX(start_time) as last_execution
FROM execution_history
WHERE squad_id IS NOT NULL
GROUP BY squad_id;

-- View for data quality dashboard
CREATE VIEW data_quality_dashboard AS
SELECT 
    pipeline_id,
    pipeline_name,
    measured_at,
    completeness,
    uniqueness,
    validity,
    consistency,
    timeliness,
    sla_status,
    alert_triggered,
    CASE 
        WHEN completeness < 98 THEN 'CRITICAL'
        WHEN completeness < 99.5 THEN 'WARNING'
        ELSE 'HEALTHY'
    END as completeness_status,
    CASE 
        WHEN timeliness < 95 THEN 'CRITICAL'
        WHEN timeliness < 98 THEN 'WARNING'
        ELSE 'HEALTHY'
    END as timeliness_status
FROM data_quality_metrics
WHERE measured_at > NOW() - INTERVAL '7 days'
ORDER BY measured_at DESC;
```

## 3. Conexão PostgreSQL

### `src/persistence/database/postgres/connection.js`
```javascript
const { Pool } = require('pg');
const config = require('../../../config/database');
const logger = require('../../../utils/logger');

class PostgreSQLConnection {
  constructor() {
    this.pool = null;
    this.isConnected = false;
    this.connectionStats = {
      totalConnections: 0,
      activeConnections: 0,
      idleConnections: 0,
      waitingConnections: 0,
      errors: 0,
      lastError: null
    };
  }

  async connect() {
    try {
      this.pool = new Pool(config.postgres);
      
      // Test connection
      const client = await this.pool.connect();
      const result = await client.query('SELECT NOW() as time, version() as version');
      client.release();
      
      this.isConnected = true;
      logger.info('PostgreSQL connected successfully', {
        time: result.rows[0].time,
        version: result.rows[0].version
      });
      
      // Set up pool event listeners
      this.pool.on('connect', (client) => {
        this.connectionStats.totalConnections++;
        logger.debug('New PostgreSQL client connected');
      });
      
      this.pool.on('acquire', (client) => {
        this.connectionStats.activeConnections++;
        this.connectionStats.idleConnections--;
      });
      
      this.pool.on('release', (client) => {
        this.connectionStats.activeConnections--;
        this.connectionStats.idleConnections++;
      });
      
      this.pool.on('error', (err, client) => {
        this.connectionStats.errors++;
        this.connectionStats.lastError = err.message;
        logger.error('PostgreSQL pool error', { error: err.message });
      });
      
      return this.pool;
    } catch (error) {
      this.isConnected = false;
      logger.error('Failed to connect to PostgreSQL', { error: error.message });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async query(text, params) {
    if (!this.isConnected) {
      await this.connect();
    }
    
    const startTime = Date.now();
    try {
      const result = await this.pool.query(text, params);
      const duration = Date.now() - startTime;
      
      logger.debug('PostgreSQL query executed', {
        query: text.substring(0, 200),
        duration,
        rowCount: result.rowCount
      });
      
      return result;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('PostgreSQL query failed', {
        query: text.substring(0, 200),
        error: error.message,
        duration: Date.now() - startTime
      });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async transaction(callback) {
    const client = await this.pool.connect();
    
    try {
      await client.query('BEGIN');
      const result = await callback(client);
      await client.query('COMMIT');
      return result;
    } catch (error) {
      await client.query('ROLLBACK');
      throw

### [Sessão Paralela: AI Ops]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Sistema de Auto-Correção

Vou implementar um sistema completo de auto-correção com monitor de exceções, classificador de falhas, reinicialização de agentes e fallback para funcionalidades degradadas.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-auto-correction/
├── index.html
├── package.json
├── src/
│   ├── core/
│   │   ├── exception-monitor.js
│   │   ├── failure-classifier.js
│   │   ├── agent-manager.js
│   │   └── fallback-system.js
│   ├── agents/
│   │   ├── base-agent.js
│   │   ├── llm-agent.js
│   │   ├── database-agent.js
│   │   └── api-agent.js
│   ├── dashboard/

│   │   └── dashboard-ui.js
│   ├── config/
│   │   └── settings.js
│   └── utils/

│       └── metrics.js
├── public/
│   ├── css/
│   │   └── style.css

├── logs/
│   └── auto-correction.log

## 2. index.html (Dashboard Principal)

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="pt-BR">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>DIYAPP V10 - Sistema de Auto-Correção</title>
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="public/css/style.css">
    <script src="/socket.io/socket.io.js"></script>
    <script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/chart.js"></script>
</head>
<body>
    <div class="container">
        <header class="dashboard-header">
            <h1>🛠️ DIYAPP V10 - Sistema de Auto-Correção</h1>
            <div class="system-status">
                <span id="system-status" class="status-indicator status-healthy">SISTEMA SAUDÁVEL</span>
                <span class="last-update" id="last-update">Última atualização: --:--:--</span>
            </div>
        </header>

        <div class="dashboard-grid">
            <!-- Painel de Status dos Agentes -->
            <div class="card agent-status">

                    <!-- Agentes serão carregados dinamicamente -->
                </div>

                        <h3>Avisos</h3>
                        <span id="warning-count" class="stat-count">0</span>

                </div>

                    <h3>Últimas Exceções</h3>

                        <!-- Exceções serão carregadas dinamicamente -->

                </div>
            </div>

            <!-- Sistema de Fallback -->

                <h2>🔄 Sistema de Fallback</h2>
                <div class="fallback-status">
                    <h3>Status Atual</h3>
                    <div id="fallback-status" class="fallback-indicator active">
                        SISTEMA DE FALLBACK ATIVO
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="fallback-history">
                    <h3>Histórico de Ativações</h3>
                    <div class="history-scroll" id="fallback-history">
                        <!-- Histórico será carregado dinamicamente -->
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>

            <!-- Métricas de Performance -->
            <div class="card performance-metrics">
                <h2>📈 Métricas de Performance</h2>
                <div class="metrics-chart">
                    <canvas id="performance-chart"></canvas>
                </div>
                <div class="metrics-stats">
                    <div class="metric">
                        <span class="metric-label">Uptime:</span>
                        <span id="uptime-metric" class="metric-value">100%</span>
                    </div>
                    <div class="metric">
                        <span class="metric-label">Latência Média:</span>
                        <span id="latency-metric" class="metric-value">0ms</span>
                    </div>
                    <div class="metric">
                        <span class="metric-label">Taxa de Erro:</span>
                        <span id="error-rate" class="metric-value">0%</span>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>

            <!-- Controles do Sistema -->
            <div class="card system-controls">
                <h2>🎛️ Controles do Sistema</h2>
                <div class="control-group">
                    <h3>Sensibilidade do Monitor</h3>
                    <div class="slider-container">
                        <input type="range" min="1" max="10" value="5" class="slider" id="sensitivity-slider">
                        <span id="sensitivity-value">Média (5)</span>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="control-group">
                    <h3>Limites de Reinicialização</h3>
                    <div class="threshold-controls">
                        <div class="threshold">
                            <label>Máx. Reinicializações/hora:</label>
                            <input type="number" id="max-restarts" value="3" min="1" max="10">
                        </div>
                        <div class="threshold">
                            <label>Timeout (ms):</label>
                            <input type="number" id="agent-timeout" value="5000" min="1000" max="30000">
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="control-buttons">
                    <button class="btn btn-success" onclick="saveSettings()">Salvar Configurações</button>
                    <button class="btn btn-danger" onclick="emergencyStop()">Parada de Emergência</button>
                    <button class="btn btn-info" onclick="exportLogs()">Exportar Logs</button>
                </div>
            </div>

            <!-- Logs do Sistema -->
            <div class="card system-logs">
                <h2>📋 Logs do Sistema</h2>
                <div class="log-controls">
                    <select id="log-level" onchange="filterLogs()">
                        <option value="all">Todos os Níveis</option>
                        <option value="error">Erros</option>
                        <option value="warn">Avisos</option>
                        <option value="info">Informações</option>
                        <option value="debug">Debug</option>
                    </select>
                    <button class="btn btn-secondary" onclick="clearLogs()">Limpar Logs</button>
                </div>
                <div class="log-scroll" id="system-logs">
                    <!-- Logs serão carregados dinamicamente -->
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>

        <footer class="dashboard-footer">
            <p>DIYAPP Evolution V10 - Sistema de Auto-Correção | AI Ops Monitor</p>
            <p class="version">Versão 1.0.0 | Modo Hive Ativo</p>
        </footer>
    </div>

    <script src="public/js/dashboard.js"></script>
</body>
</html>
```
