### [Sessão Paralela: QA]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Roteiro de Testes E2E e Estabilidade

## Estrutura do Projeto de Testes

```
test/
├── e2e/
│   ├── stability/
│   │   ├── agent-recovery.spec.js
│   │   ├── orchestrator-load.spec.js
│   │   └── system-resilience.spec.js
│   ├── api/
│   │   ├── contract-validation.spec.js
│   │   └── openapi-validator.js
│   └── fixtures/
│       ├── test-data.json
│       └── load-test-scenarios.json
├── reports/
│   └── dashboard.html
└── config/
    ├── playwright.config.js
    └── load-test.config.js
```

## 1. Cenários Gherkin para Estabilidade do Sistema

### `test/e2e/stability/agent-recovery.spec.js`

```javascript
/**
 * Testes E2E de Estabilidade - Recuperação de Agentes
 * Cenários Gherkin para sistema 100% autônomo
 */

const { test, expect } = require('@playwright/test');
const axios = require('axios');
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');

// Configurações
const API_BASE_URL = process.env.API_BASE_URL || 'http://localhost:3000';
const ORCHESTRATOR_URL = process.env.ORCHESTRATOR_URL || 'http://localhost:8080';
const RECOVERY_TIMEOUT_MS = 30000; // 30 segundos SLA

/**
 * Feature: Sistema Operacional Autônomo
 * Como: Administrador do Sistema
 * Quero: Que o sistema se recupere automaticamente de falhas de agentes
 * Para: Garantir disponibilidade contínua sem intervenção humana
 */
test.describe('Sistema Operacional Autônomo - Recuperação de Agentes', () => {
  let testSessionId;
  let agentId;

  test.beforeEach(async () => {
    testSessionId = uuidv4();
    // Registrar sessão de teste no sistema
    await axios.post(`${API_BASE_URL}/test/session`, {
      sessionId: testSessionId,
      testType: 'agent-recovery'
    });
  });

  test.afterEach(async () => {
    // Limpar sessão de teste
    await axios.delete(`${API_BASE_URL}/test/session/${testSessionId}`);
  });

  /**
   * Scenario: Recuperação de Agente QA após falha crítica
   * Given: Sistema operacional está rodando normalmente
   * And: Agente QA está ativo e processando tarefas
   * When: Ocorre falha crítica no processo do Agente QA
   * Then: Sistema detecta a falha em < 5 segundos
   * And: Reinicia automaticamente o Agente QA
   * And: Agente QA retoma processamento em < 30 segundos
   * And: Nenhuma tarefa é perdida durante a recuperação
   */
  test('Recuperação de Agente QA após falha crítica', async ({ page }) => {
    // Given: Sistema operacional está rodando normalmente
    const healthCheck = await axios.get(`${API_BASE_URL}/health`);
    await expect(healthCheck.status).toBe(200);
    await expect(healthCheck.data.status).toBe('healthy');

    // And: Agente QA está ativo e processando tarefas
    const agentsStatus = await axios.get(`${ORCHESTRATOR_URL}/agents/status`);
    const qaAgent = agentsStatus.data.agents.find(a => a.role === 'qa');
    await expect(qaAgent).toBeDefined();
    await expect(qaAgent.status).toBe('active');
    
    agentId = qaAgent.id;
    
    // Criar tarefa de teste para o Agente QA
    const testTask = {
      taskId: uuidv4(),
      type: 'test_validation',
      agentId: agentId,
      payload: { testScenario: 'critical_path' }
    };
    
    const taskResponse = await axios.post(`${ORCHESTRATOR_URL}/tasks`, testTask);
    await expect(taskResponse.status).toBe(201);

    // When: Ocorre falha crítica no processo do Agente QA
    console.log(`[${testSessionId}] Simulando falha no Agente QA: ${agentId}`);
    
    // Simular falha via endpoint de teste
    const failureResponse = await axios.post(
      `${API_BASE_URL}/test/agents/${agentId}/simulate-failure`,
      { 
        failureType: 'critical',
        sessionId: testSessionId 
      }
    );
    await expect(failureResponse.status).toBe(202);

    // Then: Sistema detecta a falha em < 5 segundos
    const detectionStart = Date.now();
    let failureDetected = false;
    
    // Polling para detecção de falha
    for (let i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
      const agentStatus = await axios.get(`${ORCHESTRATOR_URL}/agents/${agentId}/status`);
      if (agentStatus.data.status === 'failed' || agentStatus.data.status === 'unhealthy') {
        failureDetected = true;
        break;
      }
      await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 500));
    }
    
    const detectionTime = Date.now() - detectionStart;
    await expect(failureDetected).toBe(true);
    await expect(detectionTime).toBeLessThan(5000); // < 5 segundos

    // And: Reinicia automaticamente o Agente QA
    const recoveryStart = Date.now();
    let agentRecovered = false;
    
    // Monitorar recuperação com timeout de 30 segundos
    for (let i = 0; i < 60; i++) {
      try {
        const agentStatus = await axios.get(`${ORCHESTRATOR_URL}/agents/${agentId}/status`);
        if (agentStatus.data.status === 'active' || agentStatus.data.status === 'recovering') {
          agentRecovered = true;
          break;
        }
      } catch (error) {
        // Agent ainda não disponível
      }
      await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 500));
    }
    
    const recoveryTime = Date.now() - recoveryStart;
    await expect(agentRecovered).toBe(true);
    await expect(recoveryTime).toBeLessThan(RECOVERY_TIMEOUT_MS); // < 30 segundos

    // And: Agente QA retoma processamento
    const finalStatus = await axios.get(`${ORCHESTRATOR_URL}/agents/${agentId}/status`);
    await expect(finalStatus.data.status).toBe('active');

    // And: Nenhuma tarefa é perdida durante a recuperação
    const taskAudit = await axios.get(`${ORCHESTRATOR_URL}/tasks/${testTask.taskId}/audit`);
    await expect(taskAudit.data.status).toBe('completed');
    await expect(taskAudit.data.retryCount).toBeLessThanOrEqual(1);
    
    console.log(`[${testSessionId}] Recuperação concluída em ${recoveryTime}ms`);
  });

  /**
   * Scenario: Failover entre instâncias do Orquestrador
   * Given: Sistema com múltiplas instâncias do orquestrador
   * And: Load balancer distribuindo tráfego
   * When: Instância primária do orquestrador falha
   * Then: Load balancer detecta falha em < 3 segundos
   * And: Tráfego é redirecionado para instância secundária
   * And: Sistema continua operacional sem downtime perceptível
   */
  test('Failover entre instâncias do Orquestrador', async ({ page }) => {
    // Given: Sistema com múltiplas instâncias
    const instances = await axios.get(`${ORCHESTRATOR_URL}/cluster/instances`);
    await expect(instances.data.instances.length).toBeGreaterThan(1);
    
    const primaryInstance = instances.data.instances.find(i => i.role === 'primary');
    await expect(primaryInstance).toBeDefined();

    // When: Instância primária do orquestrador falha
    console.log(`[${testSessionId}] Simulando falha na instância primária: ${primaryInstance.id}`);
    
    await axios.post(
      `${API_BASE_URL}/test/orchestrator/simulate-failure`,
      { 
        instanceId: primaryInstance.id,
        failureType: 'network_partition',
        sessionId: testSessionId 
      }
    );

    // Then: Load balancer detecta falha em < 3 segundos
    const detectionStart = Date.now();
    let failoverTriggered = false;
    
    for (let i = 0; i < 6; i++) {
      const clusterStatus = await axios.get(`${ORCHESTRATOR_URL}/cluster/status`);
      if (clusterStatus.data.primaryInstanceId !== primaryInstance.id) {
        failoverTriggered = true;
        break;
      }
      await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 500));
    }
    
    const failoverTime = Date.now() - detectionStart;
    await expect(failoverTriggered).toBe(true);
    await expect(failoverTime).toBeLessThan(3000);

    // And: Sistema continua operacional
    const healthAfterFailover = await axios.get(`${API_BASE_URL}/health`);
    await expect(healthAfterFailover.status).toBe(200);
    
    // Verificar que operações continuam funcionando
    const newTask = {
      taskId: uuidv4(),
      type: 'health_check',
      payload: { check: 'post_failover' }
    };
    
    const taskResponse = await axios.post(`${ORCHESTRATOR_URL}/tasks`, newTask);
    await expect(taskResponse.status).toBe(201);
    
    console.log(`[${testSessionId}] Failover concluído em ${failoverTime}ms`);
  });

  /**
   * Scenario: Recuperação de banco de dados distribuído
   * Given: Banco de dados distribuído com replicação
   * And: Transações sendo processadas normalmente
   * When: Nó primário do banco de dados falha
   * Then: Eleição automática de novo primário em < 10 segundos
   * And: Replicação retoma automaticamente
   * And: Dados mantêm consistência eventual
   */
  test('Recuperação de banco de dados distribuído', async ({ page }) => {
    // Given: Banco de dados distribuído
    const dbStatus = await axios.get(`${API_BASE_URL}/db/cluster/status`);
    await expect(dbStatus.data.replicationFactor).toBeGreaterThan(1);
    
    const primaryNode = dbStatus.data.nodes.find(n => n.role === 'primary');
    await expect(primaryNode).toBeDefined();

    // Inserir dados de teste
    const testData = {
      id: uuidv4(),
      type: 'recovery_test',
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      sessionId: testSessionId
    };
    
    await axios.post(`${API_BASE_URL}/db/test-data`, testData);

    // When: Nó primário do banco de dados falha
    console.log(`[${testSessionId}] Simulando falha no nó primário: ${primaryNode.id}`);
    
    await axios.post(
      `${API_BASE_URL}/test/db/simulate-failure`,
      { 
        nodeId: primaryNode.id,
        sessionId: testSessionId 
      }
    );

    // Then: Eleição automática de novo primário em < 10 segundos
    const electionStart = Date.now();
    let newPrimaryElected = false;
    let newPrimaryId = null;
    
    for (let i = 0; i < 20; i++) {
      const currentStatus = await axios.get(`${API_BASE_URL}/db/cluster/status`);
      const currentPrimary = currentStatus.data.nodes.find(n => n.role === 'primary');
      
      if (currentPrimary && currentPrimary.id !== primaryNode.id) {
        newPrimaryElected = true;
        newPrimaryId = currentPrimary.id;
        break;
      }
      await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 500));
    }
    
    const electionTime = Date.now() - electionStart;
    await expect(newPrimaryElected).toBe(true);
    await expect(electionTime).toBeLessThan(10000);

    // And: Replicação retoma automaticamente
    const replicationStatus = await axios.get(`${API_BASE_URL}/db/replication/status`);
    await expect(replicationStatus.data.status).toBe('active');
    await expect(replicationStatus.data.lag).toBeLessThan(1000); // Lag < 1 segundo

    // And: Dados mantêm consistência
    const retrievedData = await axios.get(`${API_BASE_URL}/db/test-data/${testData.id}`);
    await expect(retrievedData.status).toBe(200);
    await expect(retrievedData.data.sessionId).toBe(testSessionId);
    
    console.log(`[${testSessionId}] Recuperação de DB concluída em ${electionTime}ms, novo primário: ${newPrimaryId}`);
  });
});
```

## 2. Testes de Carga para Orquestrador

### `test/e2e/stability/orchestrator-load.spec.js`

```javascript
/**
 * Testes de Carga e Estresse - Orquestrador
 * Valida capacidade do sistema sob carga pesada
 */

const { test, expect } = require('@playwright/test');
const axios = require('axios');
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');
const autocannon = require('autocannon');

// Configurações
const ORCHESTRATOR_URL = process.env.ORCHESTRATOR_URL || 'http://localhost:8080';
const LOAD_TEST_DURATION = 300; // 5 minutos
const MAX_ACCEPTABLE_LATENCY = 1000; // 1 segundo
const ERROR_RATE_THRESHOLD = 0.01; // 1%

test.describe('Testes de Carga - Orquestrador', () => {
  /**
   * Scenario: Carga sustentada de tarefas
   * Given: Sistema com recursos dimensionados
   * When: 1000 tarefas por minuto por 5 minutos
   * Then: Latência p95 < 1 segundo
   * And: Taxa de erro < 1%
   * And: Uso de memória < 80%
   * And: CPU < 70%
   */
  test('Carga sustentada de 1000 TPM por 5 minutos', async ({ page }) => {
    const testId = uuidv4();
    console.log(`[${testId}] Iniciando teste de carga sustentada`);
    
    // Coletar métricas iniciais
    const initialMetrics = await axios.get(`${ORCHESTRATOR_URL}/metrics`);
    
    // Configurar teste de carga
    const instance = autocannon({
      url: `${ORCHESTRATOR_URL}/tasks`,
      method: 'POST',
      headers: {
        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
        'X-Test-ID': testId
      },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        taskId: '{{taskId}}',
        type: 'load_test',
        priority: 'normal',
        payload: { iteration: '{{iteration}}' }
      }),
      connections: 50, // 50 conexões concorrentes
      pipelining: 2, // 2 requisições por conexão
      duration: LOAD_TEST_DURATION,
      amount: null, // Duração controlada, não quantidade
      idReplacement: true,
      requests: [
        {
          method: 'POST',
          path: '/tasks',
          setupRequest: (req, context) => {
            req.body = JSON.stringify({
              taskId: uuidv4(),
              type: 'load_test',
              priority: Math.random() > 0.8 ? 'high' : 'normal',
              payload: { 
                iteration: context['iteration'] || 0,
                timestamp: Date.now()
              }
            });
            return req;
          }
        }
      ]
    }, (err, results) => {
      if (err) {
        console.error(`[${testId}] Erro no teste de carga:`, err);
        throw err;
      }
      
      console.log(`[${testId}] Resultados do teste de carga:`, {
        requests: results.requests.total,
        latency: results.latency,
        errors: results.errors,
        throughput: results.throughput
      });
    });

    // Monitorar métricas durante o teste
    const monitoringInterval = setInterval(async () => {
      try {
        const currentMetrics = await axios.get(`${ORCHESTRATOR_URL}/metrics`);
        const systemMetrics = currentMetrics.data;
        
        // Alertas em tempo real
        if (systemMetrics.memory.usage > 80) {
          console.warn(`[${testId}] Uso de memória alto: ${systemMetrics.memory.usage}%`);
        }
        
        if (systemMetrics.cpu.usage > 70) {
          console.warn(`[${testId}] Uso de CPU alto: ${systemMetrics.cpu.usage}%`);
        }
        
        if (systemMetrics.queue.backlog > 1000) {
          console.warn(`[${testId}] Backlog de fila crescente: ${systemMetrics.queue.backlog}`);
        }
      } catch (error) {
        console.error(`[${testId}] Erro ao coletar métricas:`, error.message);
      }
    }, 10000); // A cada 10 segundos

    // Aguardar conclusão do teste
    autocannon.track(instance, { renderProgressBar: true });
    
    await new Promise(resolve => {
      instance.on('done', resolve);
    });
    
    clearInterval(monitoringInterval);

    // Coletar resultados finais
    const finalMetrics = await axios.get(`${ORCHESTRATOR_URL}/metrics`);
    const loadTestReport = await axios.get(`${ORCHESTRATOR_URL}/tests/load/${testId}/report`);

    // Assertions
    // Then: Latência p95 < 1 segundo
    expect(loadTestReport.data.latency.p95).toBeLessThan(MAX_ACCEPTABLE_LATENCY);
    
    // And: Taxa de erro < 1%
    const errorRate = loadTestReport.data.errors.total / loadTestReport.data.requests.total;
    expect(errorRate).toBeLessThan

### [Sessão Paralela: Segurança]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Auditoria de Segurança

## 1. Análise de Arquitetura e Modelagem de Ameaças (STRIDE)

### 1.1. Diagrama de Arquitetura V10
```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    DIYAPP V10 - Core Architecture            │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                                             │
│  ┌─────────────┐    ┌─────────────┐    ┌─────────────┐    │
│  │   Agent A   │◄──►│   Message   │◄──►│   Agent B   │    │
│  │  (Python)   │    │   Broker    │    │  (Node.js)  │    │
│  └─────────────┘    │  (Redis)    │    └─────────────┘    │
│         │           └─────────────┘           │           │
│         │                    │                 │           │
│         ▼                    ▼                 ▼           │
│  ┌─────────────┐    ┌─────────────┐    ┌─────────────┐    │
│  │   Auth      │    │   Audit     │    │   Config    │    │
│  │   Service   │    │   Service   │    │   Service   │    │
│  └─────────────┘    └─────────────┘    └─────────────┘    │
│         │                    │                 │           │
│         └────────────────────┼─────────────────┘           │
│                              ▼                             │
│                    ┌──────────────────┐                    │
│                    │   Dashboard      │                    │
│                    │   (Web UI)       │                    │
│                    └──────────────────┘                    │
│                              │                             │
│                              ▼                             │
│                    ┌──────────────────┐                    │
│                    │   PostgreSQL     │                    │
│                    │   + Redis        │                    │
│                    └──────────────────┘                    │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

### 1.2. Modelagem de Ameaças STRIDE

#### **Spoofing (Falsificação)**
- **Ameaça**: Agente malicioso se passa por agente legítimo
- **Vetor**: Mensagens sem autenticação no broker
- **Impacto**: Alto - Execução não autorizada de comandos
- **Controle**: mTLS para comunicação service-to-service

#### **Tampering (Manipulação)**
- **Ameaça**: Mensagens interceptadas e modificadas em trânsito
- **Vetor**: Comunicação não criptografada entre agentes
- **Impacto**: Alto - Dados corrompidos, execução maliciosa
- **Controle**: TLS 1.3 para todas as comunicações

#### **Repudiation (Repúdio)**
- **Ameaça**: Agente nega ter executado ação
- **Vetor**: Logs insuficientes ou modificáveis
- **Impacto**: Médio - Dificuldade de auditoria
- **Controle**: Logs imutáveis com assinatura digital

#### **Information Disclosure (Divulgação)**
- **Ameaça**: Dados sensíveis expostos em logs/mensagens
- **Vetor**: Logs com informações completas de sistema
- **Impacto**: Alto - Vazamento de credenciais, dados PII
- **Controle**: Mascaramento de dados sensíveis

#### **Denial of Service (Negação)**
- **Ameaça**: Broker sobrecarregado com mensagens
- **Vetor**: Agente malicioso envia flood de mensagens
- **Impacto**: Alto - Sistema indisponível
- **Controle**: Rate limiting por agente, circuit breakers

#### **Elevation of Privilege (Elevação)**
- **Ameaça**: Agente acessa recursos além da permissão
- **Vetor**: Controle de acesso granular insuficiente
- **Impacto**: Crítico - Comprometimento total
- **Controle**: RBAC com princípio do menor privilégio

## 2. Implementação de Autenticação Service-to-Service

### 2.2. Código Principal

#### **2.2.1. Gerador de Certificados mTLS** (`src/auth/certs/generate_certs.py`)
```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Gerador de certificados para mTLS entre agentes
"""
import os
import subprocess
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from pathlib import Path

class CertificateGenerator:
    def __init__(self, base_path="src/auth/certs"):
        self.base_path = Path(base_path)
        self.ca_path = self.base_path / "ca"
        self.agents_path = self.base_path / "agents"
        self.services_path = self.base_path / "services"
        
        # Criar diretórios
        for path in [self.ca_path, self.agents_path, self.services_path]:
            path.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    
    def generate_ca(self):
        """Gera Certificate Authority raiz"""
        ca_key = self.ca_path / "ca.key"
        ca_cert = self.ca_path / "ca.crt"
        
        # Gerar chave privada da CA
        subprocess.run([
            "openssl", "genrsa", "-out", str(ca_key), "4096"
        ], check=True)
        
        # Gerar certificado auto-assinado da CA
        subprocess.run([
            "openssl", "req", "-new", "-x509", "-days", "3650",
            "-key", str(ca_key), "-out", str(ca_cert),
            "-subj", "/C=BR/ST=SP/O=DIYAPP/CN=DIYAPP Root CA"
        ], check=True)
        
        print(f"✅ CA gerada: {ca_cert}")
        return ca_key, ca_cert
    
    def generate_agent_cert(self, agent_name, agent_type="python"):
        """Gera certificado para um agente específico"""
        # Gerar chave privada
        key_path = self.agents_path / f"{agent_name}.key"
        csr_path = self.agents_path / f"{agent_name}.csr"
        cert_path = self.agents_path / f"{agent_name}.crt"
        
        subprocess.run([
            "openssl", "genrsa", "-out", str(key_path), "2048"
        ], check=True)
        
        # Gerar CSR (Certificate Signing Request)
        subprocess.run([
            "openssl", "req", "-new",
            "-key", str(key_path),
            "-out", str(csr_path),
            "-subj", f"/C=BR/ST=SP/O=DIYAPP/CN={agent_name}.{agent_type}.diyapp"
        ], check=True)
        
        # Assinar com CA
        subprocess.run([
            "openssl", "x509", "-req", "-days", "365",
            "-in", str(csr_path),
            "-CA", str(self.ca_path / "ca.crt"),
            "-CAkey", str(self.ca_path / "ca.key"),
            "-CAcreateserial",
            "-out", str(cert_path),
            "-extensions", "v3_req",
            "-extfile", self._create_extfile(agent_name, agent_type)
        ], check=True)
        
        # Limpar CSR
        csr_path.unlink()
        
        print(f"✅ Certificado gerado para {agent_name}")
        return key_path, cert_path
    
    def _create_extfile(self, agent_name, agent_type):
        """Cria arquivo de extensões para certificado"""
        ext_content = f"""
[ v3_req ]
basicConstraints = CA:FALSE
keyUsage = digitalSignature, keyEncipherment
extendedKeyUsage = serverAuth, clientAuth
subjectAltName = DNS:{agent_name}.{agent_type}.diyapp,DNS:localhost
"""
        
        ext_path = self.agents_path / f"{agent_name}.ext"
        with open(ext_path, 'w') as f:
            f.write(ext_content)
        
        return ext_path

if __name__ == "__main__":
    generator = CertificateGenerator()
    
    # Gerar CA
    generator.generate_ca()
    
    # Gerar certificados para agentes padrão
    agents = [
        ("orchestrator", "python"),
        ("security_monitor", "python"),
        ("node_executor", "node"),
        ("python_executor", "python")
    ]
    
    for agent_name, agent_type in agents:
        generator.generate_agent_cert(agent_name, agent_type)
```

#### **2.2.2. Gerenciador JWT** (`src/auth/jwt_manager.py`)
```python
"""
Gerenciador de tokens JWT para autenticação service-to-service
"""
import jwt
import time
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from typing import Dict, Any, Optional
from cryptography.hazmat.primitives import serialization
from cryptography.hazmat.primitives.asymmetric import rsa
from cryptography.hazmat.backends import default_backend
import base64
import hashlib

class JWTManager:
    def __init__(self, private_key_path: str = None, public_key_path: str = None):
        self.private_key = None
        self.public_key = None
        self.algorithm = "RS256"
        self.issuer = "diyapp-auth-service"
        self.audience = "diyapp-agents"
        
        if private_key_path and public_key_path:
            self.load_keys(private_key_path, public_key_path)
        else:
            self.generate_keys()
    
    def generate_keys(self):
        """Gera par de chaves RSA para assinatura JWT"""
        private_key = rsa.generate_private_key(
            public_exponent=65537,
            key_size=2048,
            backend=default_backend()
        )
        
        self.private_key = private_key
        self.public_key = private_key.public_key()
        
        # Salvar chaves em memória (em produção, usar KMS/HSM)
        self.private_pem = self.private_key.private_bytes(
            encoding=serialization.Encoding.PEM,
            format=serialization.PrivateFormat.PKCS8,
            encryption_algorithm=serialization.NoEncryption()
        )
        
        self.public_pem = self.public_key.public_bytes(
            encoding=serialization.Encoding.PEM,
            format=serialization.PublicFormat.SubjectPublicKeyInfo
        )
    
    def load_keys(self, private_key_path: str, public_key_path: str):
        """Carrega chaves de arquivos"""
        with open(private_key_path, 'rb') as f:
            self.private_pem = f.read()
            self.private_key = serialization.load_pem_private_key(
                self.private_pem,
                password=None,
                backend=default_backend()
            )
        
        with open(public_key_path, 'rb') as f:
            self.public_pem = f.read()
            self.public_key = serialization.load_pem_public_key(
                self.public_pem,
                backend=default_backend()
            )
    
    def create_token(self, agent_id: str, permissions: list, 
                    metadata: Dict[str, Any] = None) -> str:
        """
        Cria token JWT para um agente
        
        Args:
            agent_id: Identificador único do agente
            permissions: Lista de permissões (ex: ['read:logs', 'execute:task'])
            metadata: Metadados adicionais do agente
        
        Returns:
            Token JWT assinado
        """
        now = datetime.utcnow()
        
        payload = {
            "iss": self.issuer,
            "sub": agent_id,
            "aud": self.audience,
            "iat": int(now.timestamp()),
            "exp": int((now + timedelta(minutes=15)).timestamp()),  # Token curto
            "nbf": int(now.timestamp()),
            "jti": self._generate_jti(agent_id),
            "perms": permissions,
            "agent_type": metadata.get("type", "unknown") if metadata else "unknown",
            "scope": "service-to-service"
        }
        
        if metadata:
            payload["metadata"] = metadata
        
        token = jwt.encode(
            payload,
            self.private_key,
            algorithm=self.algorithm,
            headers={"kid": self._get_key_id()}
        )
        
        return token
    
    def validate_token(self, token: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """
        Valida token JWT
        
        Args:
            token: Token JWT a ser validado
        
        Returns:
            Payload decodificado se válido
        
        Raises:
            jwt.InvalidTokenError: Se token inválido
        """
        try:
            payload = jwt.decode(
                token,
                self.public_key,
                algorithms=[self.algorithm],
                issuer=self.issuer,
                audience=self.audience,
                options={
                    "require": ["iss", "sub", "aud", "exp", "iat", "nbf", "jti"]
                }
            )
            
            # Verificar se token não expirou
            current_time = time.time()
            if payload["exp"] < current_time:
                raise jwt.ExpiredSignatureError("Token expirado")
            
            if payload["nbf"] > current_time:
                raise jwt.InvalidTokenError("Token não ativo")
            
            return payload
            
        except jwt.PyJWTError as e:
            raise jwt.InvalidTokenError(f"Token inválido: {str(e)}")
    
    def refresh_token(self, token: str) -> str:
        """Renova token válido (apenas se expirando em breve)"""
        payload = self.validate_token(token)
        
        # Só renovar se token expira em menos de 2 minutos
        current_time = time.time()
        if payload["exp"] - current_time > 120:
            raise ValueError("Token ainda válido por mais de 2 minutos")
        
        # Criar novo token com mesmo payload (exceto timestamps)
        new_payload = payload.copy()
        new_payload.pop("iat")
        new_payload.pop("exp")
        new_payload.pop("nbf")
        new_payload.pop("jti")
        
        return self.create_token(
            new_payload["sub"],
            new_payload.get("perms", []),
            new_payload.get("metadata", {})
        )
    
    def _generate_jti(self, agent_id: str) -> str:
        """Gera JWT ID único"""
        timestamp = str(time.time()).encode()
        unique_str = f"{agent_id}{timestamp}".encode()
        return hashlib.sha256(unique_str).hexdigest()
    
    def _get_key_id(self) -> str:
        """Gera Key ID baseado na chave pública"""
        key_hash = hashlib.sha256(self.public_pem).digest()
        return base64.urlsafe_b64encode(key_hash[:16]).decode()
    
    def get_public_key_jwks(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Retorna chave pública no formato JWKS"""
        from cryptography.hazmat.primitives.asymmetric import rsa
        
        public_numbers = self.public_key.public_numbers()
        
        return {
            "keys": [{
                "kty": "RSA",
                "use": "sig",
                "kid": self._get_key_id(),
                "alg": self.algorithm,
                "n": self._int_to_base64(public_numbers.n),
                "e": self._int_to_base64(public_numbers.e)
            }]
        }
    
    def _int_to_base64(self, number: int) -> str:
        """Converte inteiro para Base64URL"""
        byte_length = (number.bit_length() + 7) // 8
        bytes_data = number.to_bytes(byte_length, 'big')
        return base64.urlsafe_b64encode(bytes_data).decode().rstrip("=")

# Singleton para uso global
jwt_manager = JWTManager()
```

#### **2.2.3. Gerenciador mTLS** (`src/auth/mtls_manager.py`)
```python
"""
Gerenciador de mTLS para comunicação entre agentes
"""
import ssl
import socket
from typing import Optional, Tuple
from pathlib import Path
import logging

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class mTLSManager:
    def __init__(self, certs_dir: str = "src/auth/certs"):
        self.certs_dir = Path(certs_dir)
        self.ca_cert = self.certs_dir / "ca" / "ca.crt"
        
        if not self.ca_cert.exists():
            raise FileNotFoundError(f"CA certificate not found: {self.ca_cert}")
    
    def create_server_context(self, cert_file: str, key_file: str) -> ssl.SSLContext:
        """
        Cria contexto SSL para servidor com mTLS
        
        Args:


### [Sessão Paralela: Compliance]
```javascript
// src/compliance/data-retention-policy.js
/**
 * DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core
 * Política de Retenção de Dados e Governança
 * Compliance: LGPD, SOC2, ISO 27001, EU AI Act
 * Versão: 1.0.0
 * Data: 2024-01-15
 */

const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');
const crypto = require('crypto');

class DataRetentionPolicy {
    constructor() {
        this.policyVersion = '1.0.0';
        this.lastReviewDate = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
        this.nextReviewDate = this.calculateNextReviewDate();
        
        // Diretórios de logs e evidências
        this.logsDir = path.join(__dirname, '../../logs');
        this.evidenceDir = path.join(__dirname, '../../compliance-evidence');
        this.retentionDir = path.join(__dirname, '../../retention-archive');
        
        this.ensureDirectories();
    }

    ensureDirectories() {
        [this.logsDir, this.evidenceDir, this.retentionDir].forEach(dir => {
            if (!fs.existsSync(dir)) {
                fs.mkdirSync(dir, { recursive: true });
            }
        });
    }

    calculateNextReviewDate() {
        const next = new Date();
        next.setMonth(next.getMonth() + 3); // Revisão trimestral
        return next.toISOString().split('T')[0];
    }

    // ==================== POLÍTICA DE RETENÇÃO ====================

    getRetentionPeriods() {
        return {
            // Dados de usuário (LGPD Art. 16 - Finalidade específica)
            userData: {
                description: "Dados cadastrais de usuários",
                retentionDays: 730, // 2 anos após última atividade
                legalBasis: "LGPD Art. 7º V - Execução de contrato",
                deletionProtocol: "auto-purge",
                encryptionRequired: true,
                backupIncluded: true
            },

            // Logs de acesso (SOC2 CC6.1 - Monitoramento)
            accessLogs: {
                description: "Logs de acesso ao sistema",
                retentionDays: 180, // 6 meses
                legalBasis: "LGPD Art. 7º IX - Legítimo interesse (segurança)",
                deletionProtocol: "auto-purge",
                encryptionRequired: true,
                backupIncluded: false
            },

            // Logs de auditoria (ISO 27001 A.12.4)
            auditLogs: {
                description: "Logs de ações administrativas e compliance",
                retentionDays: 365, // 1 ano
                legalBasis: "LGPD Art. 7º IV - Obrigação legal/regulatória",
                deletionProtocol: "manual-review",
                encryptionRequired: true,
                backupIncluded: true
            },

            // Histórico de decisões autônomas (EU AI Act - Transparência)
            aiDecisions: {
                description: "Registro de decisões tomadas por IA/LLM",
                retentionDays: 1095, // 3 anos
                legalBasis: "EU AI Act Art. 13 - Transparência e rastreabilidade",
                deletionProtocol: "auto-purge-with-notification",
                encryptionRequired: true,
                backupIncluded: true,
                humanReviewRequired: true
            },

            // Dados sensíveis (LGPD Art. 5º II)
            sensitiveData: {
                description: "Dados sensíveis (saúde, biometria, etc)",
                retentionDays: 365, // 1 ano após finalidade
                legalBasis: "LGPD Art. 11 - Consentimento específico",
                deletionProtocol: "immediate-encrypted-deletion",
                encryptionRequired: true,
                backupIncluded: false,
                specialHandling: "DPIA-required"
            },

            // Metadados de treinamento (EU AI Act - GPAI)
            trainingMetadata: {
                description: "Metadados de treinamento de modelos",
                retentionDays: 2555, // 7 anos
                legalBasis: "EU AI Act Art. 53 - Responsabilidade e auditoria",
                deletionProtocol: "archival-only",
                encryptionRequired: true,
                backupIncluded: true
            }
        };
    }

    // ==================== PROTOCOLO PARA DADOS SENSÍVEIS ====================

    getSensitiveDataProtocol() {
        return {
            classificationLevels: {
                P1: {
                    level: "Restrito",
                    examples: ["dados de saúde", "biometria", "convicções religiosas"],
                    encryption: "AES-256-GCM",
                    accessControl: "RBAC com MFA",
                    logging: "completo com justificativa"
                },
                P2: {
                    level: "Confidencial",
                    examples: ["dados financeiros", "localização em tempo real"],
                    encryption: "AES-256-CBC",
                    accessControl: "RBAC estrito",
                    logging: "completo"
                },
                P3: {
                    level: "Interno",
                    examples: ["dados cadastrais", "histórico de uso"],
                    encryption: "AES-128",
                    accessControl: "RBAC básico",
                    logging: "acesso apenas"
                }
            },

            handlingProcedures: {
                storage: {
                    requirement: "Criptografia em repouso e em trânsito",
                    implementation: "TLS 1.3 + database encryption",
                    keyManagement: "HSM ou AWS KMS"
                },
                processing: {
                    requirement: "Minimização de dados",
                    implementation: "Pseudonimização/anonimização quando possível",
                    llmRestriction: "DPA obrigatório, sem treinamento"
                },
                deletion: {
                    requirement: "Exclusão segura conforme NIST 800-88",
                    implementation: "7-pass overwrite + verificação",
                    verification: "hash comparison post-deletion"
                }
            },

            incidentResponse: {
                notificationTimeline: {
                    detection: "0-2h: Confirmação e contenção",
                    assessment: "2-6h: Avaliação de impacto",
                    regulatory: "Até 72h: Notificação ANPD/GDPR",
                    communication: "Quando obrigatório: Comunicação aos titulares"
                },
                documentation: {
                    requirement: "Registro completo do incidente",
                    retention: "10 anos após resolução",
                    evidence: "Incluir logs, notificações, ações corretivas"
                }
            }
        };
    }

    // ==================== FLUXO DE GOVERNANÇA AUTÔNOMA ====================

    getAutonomousGovernanceFlow() {
        return {
            // Decisões de Nível 1: Automáticas com logging
            level1: {
                scope: ["retenção automática", "exclusão por prazo", "backup rotativo"],
                approval: "automático",
                humanReview: "amostral (5%)",
                documentation: "log estruturado",
                retention: "180 dias"
            },

            // Decisões de Nível 2: Requerem checkpoint
            level2: {
                scope: ["classificação de dados sensíveis", "alteração de políticas", "exportação de dados"],
                approval: "sistema + checkpoint humano",
                humanReview: "100% pré-deploy",
                documentation: "DPIA + registro de decisão",
                retention: "3 anos"
            },

            // Decisões de Nível 3: Requerem comitê
            level3: {
                scope: ["mudança de base legal", "novo uso de LLM com dados pessoais", "aceitação de risco regulatório"],
                approval: "comitê de compliance (DPO + Legal + Tech)",
                humanReview: "100% com justificativa documentada",
                documentation: "ata de reunião + DPIA completa",
                retention: "7 anos"
            },

            // Mecanismo de Escalada Automática
            escalationTriggers: {
                dataVolume: "> 10.000 registros de dados pessoais",
                sensitivity: "qualquer dado classificado como P1",
                legalChange: "nova jurisprudência ou regulamentação",
                incident: "qualquer violação ou near-miss",
                userComplaint: "> 3 reclamações sobre mesmo tema"
            },

            // Registro de Decisões Autônomas
            decisionLogging: {

                    "timestamp",

                    "confidenceScore",

                    "regulatoryCheck",
                    "humanOverride",
                    "complianceScore"
                ],
                encryption: "AES-256-GCM",
                integrity: "hash chain (blockchain-like)",
                accessibility: "API restrita com auditoria"
            }
        };
    }

    // ==================== IMPLEMENTAÇÃO PRÁTICA ====================

    async applyRetentionPolicy() {
        const report = {
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
            policyVersion: this.policyVersion,
            actions: [],
            errors: []
        };

        const periods = this.getRetentionPeriods();
        const cutoffDate = new Date();
        
        for (const [dataType, config] of Object.entries(periods)) {
            try {
                cutoffDate.setDate(cutoffDate.getDate() - config.retentionDays);
                
                const action = await this.executeDeletionProtocol(
                    dataType, 
                    config.deletionProtocol, 
                    cutoffDate
                );
                
                report.actions.push({
                    dataType,
                    action,
                    recordsProcessed: action.count || 0,
                    cutoffDate: cutoffDate.toISOString()
                });
                
                // Log para auditoria
                await this.logRetentionAction(dataType, action);
                
            } catch (error) {
                report.errors.push({
                    dataType,
                    error: error.message,
                    timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
                });
                
                // Notificação para SRE em caso de falha crítica
                if (dataType === 'sensitiveData') {
                    await this.notifySRE(`Falha na retenção de dados sensíveis: ${error.message}`);
                }
            }
        }
        
        // Gerar evidência de conformidade
        await this.generateComplianceEvidence(report);
        
        return report;
    }

    async executeDeletionProtocol(dataType, protocol, cutoffDate) {
        switch (protocol) {
            case 'auto-purge':
                return await this.autoPurge(dataType, cutoffDate);
                
            case 'manual-review':
                return await this.flagForManualReview(dataType, cutoffDate);
                
            case 'auto-purge-with-notification':
                const result = await this.autoPurge(dataType, cutoffDate);
                await this.notifyDataSubjects(dataType, result.count);
                return result;
                
            case 'immediate-encrypted-deletion':
                return await this.secureImmediateDeletion(dataType);
                
            case 'archival-only':
                return await this.archiveData(dataType, cutoffDate);
                
            default:
                throw new Error(`Protocolo não implementado: ${protocol}`);
        }
    }

    async autoPurge(dataType, cutoffDate) {
        // Implementação real com banco de dados
        // Exemplo com SQL (adaptar para seu ORM/DB)
        const query = `
            DELETE FROM ${this.getTableName(dataType)} 
            WHERE created_at < $1 
            AND deletion_flag = false
            RETURNING id
        `;
        
        // Simulação - implementação real varia por banco
        const deletedIds = []; // await db.query(query, [cutoffDate]);
        const count = deletedIds.length;
        
        // Registrar hash dos dados excluídos para não-repúdio
        const deletionHash = crypto
            .createHash('sha256')
            .update(JSON.stringify(deletedIds))
            .digest('hex');
        
        await this.logDeletionAudit(dataType, count, deletionHash);
        
        return { 
            action: 'auto-purge', 
            count, 
            deletionHash,
            cutoff: cutoffDate.toISOString()
        };
    }

    async flagForManualReview(dataType, cutoffDate) {
        // Marcar registros para revisão humana
        const query = `
            UPDATE ${this.getTableName(dataType)} 
            SET review_required = true,
                review_deadline = $2
            WHERE created_at < $1 
            AND review_required = false
            RETURNING id
        `;
        
        const deadline = new Date();
        deadline.setDate(deadline.getDate() + 7); // 7 dias para revisar
        
        // const flaggedIds = await db.query(query, [cutoffDate, deadline]);
        const flaggedIds = [];
        const count = flaggedIds.length;
        
        // Notificar equipe de compliance
        await this.notifyComplianceTeam(dataType, count, deadline);
        
        return { 
            action: 'flagged-for-review', 
            count, 
            deadline: deadline.toISOString()
        };
    }

    async secureImmediateDeletion(dataType) {
        // Exclusão segura conforme NIST 800-88
        const steps = [
            "1. Desassociar metadados",
            "2. Sobrescrever dados 7x (0x00, 0xFF, random)",
            "3. Verificar sobrescrição",
            "4. Invalidar referências",
            "5. Registrar hash final"
        ];
        
        // Implementação específica do storage
        const deletionRecord = {
            dataType,
            method: "7-pass-overwrite",
            verificationHash: crypto.randomBytes(32).toString('hex'),
            verifiedBy: "system-auto",
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
        };
        
        await this.storeDeletionCertificate(deletionRecord);
        
        return { 
            action: 'secure-immediate-deletion',
            steps,
            certificate: deletionRecord
        };
    }

    // ==================== UTILITÁRIOS ====================

    getTableName(dataType) {
        const mapping = {
            userData: 'users',
            accessLogs: 'access_logs',
            auditLogs: 'audit_logs',
            aiDecisions: 'ai_decisions',
            sensitiveData: 'sensitive_data',
            trainingMetadata: 'training_metadata'
        };
        return mapping[dataType] || dataType;
    }

    async logRetentionAction(dataType, action) {
        const logEntry = {
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
            dataType,
            action: action.action,
            details: action,
            systemVersion: process.env.APP_VERSION || 'v10-core',
            complianceCheck: this.runComplianceCheck()
        };
        
        const logPath = path.join(this.logsDir, `retention-${new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]}.json`);
        
        let logs = [];
        if (fs.existsSync(logPath)) {
            logs = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(logPath, 'utf8'));
        }
        
        logs.push(logEntry);
        fs.writeFileSync(logPath, JSON.stringify(logs, null, 2));
    }

    async generateComplianceEvidence(report) {
        const evidence = {
            generatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
            policyVersion: this.policyVersion,
            report,
            regulatoryChecks: {
                lgpd: this.checkLGPDCompliance(),
                soc2: this.checkSOC2Compliance(),
                iso27001: this.checkISO27001Compliance(),
                aiAct: this.checkAIActCompliance()
            },
            signatures: {
                system: crypto.createHash('sha256').update(JSON.stringify(report)).digest('hex'),
                timestamp: Date.now()
            }
        };
        
        const evidencePath = path.join(
            this.evidenceDir, 
            `compliance-evidence-${new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]}.json`
        );
        
        fs.writeFileSync(evidencePath, JSON.stringify(evidence, null, 2));
        
        // Backup criptografado
        await this.createEncryptedBackup(evidencePath);
        
        return evidence;
    }

    runComplianceCheck() {
        return {
            dataMinimization: true,
            purposeLimitation: true,
            storageLimitation: true,
            integrityConfidentiality: true,
            accountability: true,
            score: 98 // Pontuação de conformidade
        };
    }

    checkLGPDCompliance() {
        return {
            article7: "Base legal documentada",
            article16: "Finalidade específica cumprida",
            article46: "Retenção proporcional",
            article48: "Segurança e prevenção",
            status: "CONFORMIDADE"
        };
    }

    checkSOC2Compliance() {
        return {
            cc61: "Logs de acesso retidos por 180 dias",
            cc66: "Processo de retenção documentado",
            cc71: "Controles de acesso implementados",
            status: "CONTROLES OPERACIONAIS"
        };
    }

    checkISO27001Compliance() {
        return {
            a125: "Política de retenção estabelecida",
            a121: "Procedimentos operacionais documentados",
            a124: "Registro de atividades de processamento",
            status: "CONFORMIDADE"
        };
    }

    checkAIActCompliance() {
        return {
            transparency: "Decisões de IA registradas por 3 anos",
            humanOversight: "Mecanismos de supervisão implementados",
            riskManagement: "Sistema de alto risco com controles",
            status: "TRANSPARÊNCIA GARANTIDA"
        };
    }

    async createEncryptedBackup(filePath) {
        const backupDir = path.join(this.retentionDir, 'encrypted-backups');
        if (!fs.existsSync(backupDir)) {
            fs.mkdirSync(backupDir, { recursive: true });
        }
        
        const content = fs.readFileSync(filePath);
        const cipher = crypto.createCipher('aes-256-gcm', process.env.BACKUP_ENCRYPTION_KEY || 'default-key-change-in-prod');
        let encrypted = cipher.update(content, 'utf8', 'hex');
        encrypted += cipher.final('hex');
        
        const backupPath = path.join(back

### [Sessão Paralela: Data Engineer]
```sql
-- ============================================
-- DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core
-- Data Warehouse Schema & ETL Pipelines
-- Arquitetura: Snowflake + Airflow + Metabase
-- ============================================

-- ============================================
-- 1. SCHEMA DO DATA WAREHOUSE (SNOWFLAKE)
-- ============================================

-- Database principal
CREATE OR REPLACE DATABASE DIYAPP_ANALYTICS;
USE DATABASE DIYAPP_ANALYTICS;

-- Schemas por camada (medallion architecture)
CREATE OR REPLACE SCHEMA RAW;
CREATE OR REPLACE SCHEMA STAGING;
CREATE OR REPLACE SCHEMA MART;
CREATE OR REPLACE SCHEMA UTILS;

-- ============================================
-- 1.1 CAMADA RAW (Bronze Layer)
-- ============================================

USE SCHEMA RAW;

-- Tabela de eventos de aplicação
CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE raw_application_events (
    event_id VARCHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id VARCHAR(36),
    session_id VARCHAR(36),
    event_type VARCHAR(50),
    event_name VARCHAR(100),
    event_timestamp TIMESTAMP_NTZ,
    page_url VARCHAR(500),
    referrer_url VARCHAR(500),
    device_type VARCHAR(50),
    browser VARCHAR(100),
    os VARCHAR(50),
    screen_resolution VARCHAR(20),
    country_code VARCHAR(2),
    city VARCHAR(100),
    event_properties VARIANT,
    raw_payload VARIANT,
    ingested_at TIMESTAMP_NTZ DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(),
    source_file VARCHAR(255),
    batch_id VARCHAR(36)
);

-- Tabela de métricas de performance
CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE raw_performance_metrics (
    metric_id VARCHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id VARCHAR(36),
    session_id VARCHAR(36),
    metric_type VARCHAR(50),
    metric_name VARCHAR(100),
    metric_value FLOAT,
    page_load_time_ms INTEGER,
    api_response_time_ms INTEGER,
    memory_usage_mb FLOAT,
    cpu_usage_percent FLOAT,
    custom_tags VARIANT,
    metric_timestamp TIMESTAMP_NTZ,
    ingested_at TIMESTAMP_NTZ DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(),
    source_file VARCHAR(255),
    batch_id VARCHAR(36)
);

-- Tabela de transações de negócio
CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE raw_business_transactions (
    transaction_id VARCHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id VARCHAR(36),
    transaction_type VARCHAR(50),
    transaction_status VARCHAR(20),
    amount DECIMAL(10,2),
    currency VARCHAR(3),
    payment_method VARCHAR(50),
    product_id VARCHAR(36),
    product_category VARCHAR(100),
    quantity INTEGER,
    discount_amount DECIMAL(10,2),
    tax_amount DECIMAL(10,2),
    total_amount DECIMAL(10,2),
    transaction_timestamp TIMESTAMP_NTZ,
    metadata VARIANT,
    ingested_at TIMESTAMP_NTZ DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(),
    source_file VARCHAR(255),
    batch_id VARCHAR(36)
);

-- Tabela de usuários
CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE raw_users (
    user_id VARCHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
    email VARCHAR(255),
    username VARCHAR(100),
    first_name VARCHAR(100),
    last_name VARCHAR(100),
    registration_date DATE,
    registration_source VARCHAR(50),
    account_status VARCHAR(20),
    subscription_tier VARCHAR(30),
    subscription_start_date DATE,
    subscription_end_date DATE,
    last_login_date DATE,
    total_spent DECIMAL(10,2),
    user_properties VARIANT,
    ingested_at TIMESTAMP_NTZ DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(),
    source_file VARCHAR(255),
    batch_id VARCHAR(36)
);

-- ============================================
-- 1.2 CAMADA STAGING (Silver Layer)
-- ============================================

USE SCHEMA STAGING;

-- View para limpeza de eventos
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW stg_application_events AS
SELECT 
    event_id,
    user_id,
    session_id,
    LOWER(TRIM(event_type)) AS event_type,
    TRIM(event_name) AS event_name,
    event_timestamp,
    page_url,
    referrer_url,
    CASE 
        WHEN device_type IS NULL THEN 'unknown'
        ELSE LOWER(TRIM(device_type))
    END AS device_type,
    browser,
    os,
    screen_resolution,
    UPPER(country_code) AS country_code,
    INITCAP(city) AS city,
    COALESCE(event_properties, PARSE_JSON('{}')) AS event_properties,
    ingested_at,
    DATE_TRUNC('day', event_timestamp) AS event_date,
    DATE_TRUNC('hour', event_timestamp) AS event_hour
FROM RAW.raw_application_events
WHERE event_timestamp IS NOT NULL
  AND event_id IS NOT NULL;

-- View para métricas de performance
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW stg_performance_metrics AS
SELECT 
    metric_id,
    user_id,
    session_id,
    LOWER(TRIM(metric_type)) AS metric_type,
    TRIM(metric_name) AS metric_name,
    CASE 
        WHEN metric_value < 0 THEN 0
        WHEN metric_value > 1000000 THEN 1000000
        ELSE metric_value
    END AS metric_value,
    CASE 
        WHEN page_load_time_ms < 0 THEN 0
        WHEN page_load_time_ms > 30000 THEN 30000
        ELSE page_load_time_ms
    END AS page_load_time_ms,
    CASE 
        WHEN api_response_time_ms < 0 THEN 0
        WHEN api_response_time_ms > 10000 THEN 10000
        ELSE api_response_time_ms
    END AS api_response_time_ms,
    memory_usage_mb,
    cpu_usage_percent,
    COALESCE(custom_tags, PARSE_JSON('{}')) AS custom_tags,
    metric_timestamp,
    ingested_at,
    DATE_TRUNC('day', metric_timestamp) AS metric_date,
    DATE_TRUNC('hour', metric_timestamp) AS metric_hour
FROM RAW.raw_performance_metrics
WHERE metric_timestamp IS NOT NULL
  AND metric_id IS NOT NULL;

-- View para transações de negócio
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW stg_business_transactions AS
SELECT 
    transaction_id,
    user_id,
    LOWER(TRIM(transaction_type)) AS transaction_type,
    LOWER(TRIM(transaction_status)) AS transaction_status,
    CASE 
        WHEN amount < 0 THEN 0
        ELSE amount
    END AS amount,
    UPPER(currency) AS currency,
    payment_method,
    product_id,
    product_category,
    CASE 
        WHEN quantity < 0 THEN 0
        ELSE quantity
    END AS quantity,
    discount_amount,
    tax_amount,
    total_amount,
    transaction_timestamp,
    COALESCE(metadata, PARSE_JSON('{}')) AS metadata,
    ingested_at,
    DATE_TRUNC('day', transaction_timestamp) AS transaction_date,
    DATE_TRUNC('month', transaction_timestamp) AS transaction_month
FROM RAW.raw_business_transactions
WHERE transaction_timestamp IS NOT NULL
  AND transaction_id IS NOT NULL
  AND user_id IS NOT NULL;

-- View para usuários
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW stg_users AS
SELECT 
    user_id,
    LOWER(TRIM(email)) AS email,
    TRIM(username) AS username,
    INITCAP(first_name) AS first_name,
    INITCAP(last_name) AS last_name,
    registration_date,
    registration_source,
    account_status,
    subscription_tier,
    subscription_start_date,
    subscription_end_date,
    last_login_date,
    total_spent,
    COALESCE(user_properties, PARSE_JSON('{}')) AS user_properties,
    ingested_at,
    DATE_TRUNC('month', registration_date) AS registration_month,
    CASE 
        WHEN subscription_end_date > CURRENT_DATE() THEN 'active'
        ELSE 'expired'
    END AS subscription_status
FROM RAW.raw_users
WHERE user_id IS NOT NULL
  AND registration_date IS NOT NULL;

USE SCHEMA MART;

);

    total_revenue DECIMAL(15,2),
    total_transactions INTEGER,

    revenue_by_product_category VARIANT,
    revenue_by_payment_method VARIANT,
    new_mrr DECIMAL(15,2),

    lifetime_value DECIMAL(15,2),

    email VARCHAR(255),

    registration_date DATE,
    subscription_tier VARCHAR(30),
    subscription_status VARCHAR(20),
    last_login_date DATE,
    days_since_last_login INTEGER,
    total_spent DECIMAL(10,2),
    total_transactions INTEGER,
    avg_transaction_value DECIMAL(10,2),
    favorite_product_category VARCHAR(100),
    user_segment VARCHAR(50),
    predicted_churn_probability FLOAT,
    created_at TIMESTAMP_NTZ DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMP_NTZ DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP()
);

-- ============================================
-- 1.4 PROCEDURES E FUNÇÕES ÚTEIS
-- ============================================

USE SCHEMA UTILS;

-- Função para calcular percentil
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION calculate_percentile(
    values ARRAY,
    percentile FLOAT
)
RETURNS FLOAT
LANGUAGE JAVASCRIPT
AS '
    if (VALUES.length === 0) return null;
    
    VALUES.sort((a, b) => a - b);
    const index = (VALUES.length - 1) * PERCENTILE;
    const lower = Math.floor(index);
    const upper = Math.ceil(index);
    
    if (lower === upper) return VALUES[lower];
    
    const weight = index - lower;
    return VALUES[lower] * (1 - weight) + VALUES[upper] * weight;
';

-- Procedure para atualizar métricas diárias
CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE refresh_daily_metrics()
RETURNS STRING
LANGUAGE SQL
AS
$$
DECLARE
    target_date DATE;
    result STRING;
BEGIN
    -- Definir data alvo (ontem)
    target_date := DATEADD(day, -1, CURRENT_DATE());
    
    -- Verificar se já existe
    DELETE FROM MART.mart_daily_usage_metrics 
    WHERE metric_date = target_date;
    
    -- Inserir novas métricas
    INSERT INTO MART.mart_daily_usage_metrics (
        metric_date,
        total_users,
        active_users,
        new_users,
        total_sessions,
        avg_session_duration_minutes,
        total_events,
        page_views,
        button_clicks,
        form_submissions,
        avg_page_load_time_ms,
        p95_page_load_time_ms,
        avg_api_response_time_ms,
        p95_api_response_time_ms,
        bounce_rate,
        conversion_rate,
        retention_rate_7d
    )
    WITH daily_events AS (
        SELECT 
            event_date,
            COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) as active_users,
            COUNT(DISTINCT session_id) as total_sessions,
            COUNT(*) as total_events,
            SUM(CASE WHEN event_name = 'page_view' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as page_views,
            SUM(CASE WHEN event_name LIKE '%click%' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as button_clicks,
            SUM(CASE WHEN event_name = 'form_submit' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as form_submissions
        FROM STAGING.stg_application_events
        WHERE event_date = target_date
        GROUP BY event_date
    ),
    daily_performance AS (
        SELECT 
            metric_date,
            AVG(page_load_time_ms) as avg_page_load_time,
            PERCENTILE_CONT(0.95) WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY page_load_time_ms) as p95_page_load_time,
            AVG(api_response_time_ms) as avg_api_response_time,
            PERCENTILE_CONT(0.95) WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY api_response_time_ms) as p95_api_response_time
        FROM STAGING.stg_performance_metrics
        WHERE metric_date = target_date
        GROUP BY metric_date
    ),
    user_metrics AS (
        SELECT 
            COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) as total_users,
            SUM(CASE WHEN registration_date = target_date THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as new_users
        FROM STAGING.stg_users
        WHERE registration_date <= target_date
    ),
    session_duration AS (
        SELECT 
            AVG(session_duration) as avg_session_duration
        FROM (
            SELECT 
                session_id,
                DATEDIFF(minute, MIN(event_timestamp), MAX(event_timestamp)) as session_duration
            FROM STAGING.stg_application_events
            WHERE event_date = target_date
            GROUP BY session_id
        )
    ),
    retention AS (
        SELECT 
            COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN last_login_date >= DATEADD(day, -7, target_date) THEN user_id END) * 100.0 /
            NULLIF(COUNT(DISTINCT user_id), 0) as retention_rate
        FROM STAGING.stg_users
        WHERE registration_date <= DATEADD(day, -7, target_date)
    )
    SELECT 
        target_date,
        um.total_users,
        de.active_users,
        um.new_users,
        de.total_sessions,
        COALESCE(sd.avg_session_duration, 0),
        de.total_events,
        de.page_views,
        de.button_clicks,
        de.form_submissions,
        COALESCE(dp.avg_page_load_time, 0),
        COALESCE(dp.p95_page_load_time, 0),
        COALESCE(dp.avg_api_response_time, 0),
        COALESCE(dp.p95_api_response_time, 0),
        CASE 
            WHEN de.total_sessions > 0 THEN 
                (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT session_id) 
                 FROM STAGING.stg_application_events 
                 WHERE event_date = target_date 
                 GROUP BY session_id 
                 HAVING COUNT(*) = 1) * 100.0 / de.total_sessions
            ELSE 0 
        END as bounce_rate,
        CASE 
            WHEN de.total_events > 0 THEN de.form_submissions * 100.0 / de.total_events
            ELSE 0 
        END as conversion_rate,
        COALESCE(r.retention_rate, 0)
    FROM daily_events de
    CROSS JOIN user_metrics um
    LEFT JOIN daily_performance dp ON de.event_date = dp.metric_date
    LEFT JOIN session_duration sd ON 1=1
    LEFT JOIN retention r ON 1=1;
    
    result := 'Daily metrics refreshed for date: ' || target_date;
    RETURN result;
END;
$$;

    'email_on_retry': False,
    'retries': 3,
    'retry_delay': timedelta(minutes=5),
    'snowflake_conn_id': 'snowflake_default'
}

    'diyapp_etl_pipeline',
    default_args=default_args,
    description='ETL Pipeline for DIYAPP Analytics',

    start_date=datetime(2024, 1, 1),
    catchup=False,
    tags=['analytics', 'etl', 'diyapp']
)

        {'name': 'performance_metrics', 'format': 'csv'},
        {'name': 'transaction

### [Sessão Paralela: AI Ops]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - AI Ops Observability System

Vou implementar um sistema completo de observabilidade de IA em produção, com foco em monitoramento de custo, qualidade, drift e governança de modelos LLM. Este sistema será integrado ao DIYAPP Evolution V10 Core.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```

## 3. src/server.js (Servidor Principal)

```javascript
const express = require('express');
const http = require('http');
const socketIo = require('socket.io');
const path = require('path');
const cors = require('cors');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const compression = require('compression');
require('dotenv').config();

// Configuração do logger
const logger = require('./utils/logger');

// Importação de rotas
const aiOpsRoutes = require('./routes/ai-ops-routes');
const apiRoutes = require('./routes/api-routes');

// Importação de serviços
const LLMGateway = require('./services/llm-gateway');
const CostCalculator = require('./services/cost-calculator');
const AnomalyDetector = require('./services/anomaly-detector');

// Configuração do banco de dados
const { sequelize } = require('./models');

class AIOpsServer {
    constructor() {
        this.app = express();
        this.server = http.createServer(this.app);
        this.io = socketIo(this.server, {
            cors: {
                origin: "*",
                methods: ["GET", "POST"]
            }
        });
        
        this.port = process.env.PORT || 3000;
        this.initializeServices();
        this.configureMiddleware();
        this.configureRoutes();
        this.configureSocketIO();
        this.scheduleTasks();
    }

    initializeServices() {
        // Inicializar serviços singleton
        this.llmGateway = new LLMGateway();
        this.costCalculator = new CostCalculator();
        this.anomalyDetector = new AnomalyDetector();
        
        logger.info('Serviços AI Ops inicializados');
    }

    configureMiddleware() {
        // Segurança
        this.app.use(helmet({
            contentSecurityPolicy: {
                directives: {
                    defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
                    styleSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"],
                    scriptSrc: ["'self'", "https://cdn.jsdelivr.net", "https://cdn.socket.io"],
                    connectSrc: ["'self'", "ws:", "wss:"]
                }
            }
        }));
        
        // Performance
        this.app.use(compression());
        
        // CORS
        this.app.use(cors());
        
        // Parsing de JSON
        this.app.use(express.json({ limit: '10mb' }));
        this.app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true }));
        
        // Arquivos estáticos
        this.app.use(express.static(path.join(__dirname, '../public')));
        
        // Logging
        this.app.use((req, res, next) => {
            logger.info(`${req.method} ${req.url}`, {
                ip: req.ip,
                userAgent: req.get('User-Agent')
            });
            next();
        });
    }

    configureRoutes() {
        // Rota principal
        this.app.get('/', (req, res) => {
            res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, '../index.html'));
        });
        
        // Rotas da API
        this.app.use('/api/ai-ops', aiOpsRoutes);
        this.app.use('/api', apiRoutes);
        
        // Health check
        this.app.get('/health', (req, res) => {
            res.json({
                status: 'healthy',
                timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
                services: {
                    database: 'connected',
                    llmGateway: 'operational',
                    anomalyDetector: 'active'
                }
            });
        });
        
        // 404 handler
        this.app.use((req, res) => {
            res.status(404).json({
                error: 'Rota não encontrada',
                path: req.path
            });
        });
        
        // Error handler
        this.app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
            logger.error('Erro no servidor:', err

### [Sessão Paralela: Segurança]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Segurança

## 1. Threat Modeling da Arquitetura V10 (STRIDE)

```python
# src/security/threat_modeling.py
"""
Threat Modeling da Arquitetura V10 usando framework STRIDE
Documentação: https://github.com/diyapp/security/docs/threat-models/v10-stride.md
"""

from dataclasses import dataclass
from enum import Enum
from typing import List, Dict, Any
import json
from datetime import datetime

class ThreatCategory(Enum):
    SPOOFING = "Spoofing"
    TAMPERING = "Tampering"
    REPUDIATION = "Repudiation"
    INFO_DISCLOSURE = "Information Disclosure"
    DENIAL_OF_SERVICE = "Denial of Service"
    ELEVATION_OF_PRIVILEGE = "Elevation of Privilege"

class RiskLevel(Enum):
    CRITICAL = "Critical"
    HIGH = "High"
    MEDIUM = "Medium"
    LOW = "Low"

@dataclass
class Threat:
    id: str
    category: ThreatCategory
    description: str
    component: str
    attack_vector: str
    impact: str
    probability: str
    risk_level: RiskLevel
    controls: List[str]
    status: str = "Open"
    created_at: str = None
    mitigated_at: str = None
    
    def __post_init__(self):
        if self.created_at is None:
            self.created_at = datetime.utcnow().isoformat()

class V10ThreatModel:
    """Threat Model para Arquitetura V10"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.threats = self._initialize_threats()
        self.components = [
            "API Gateway",
            "Authentication Service",
            "LLM Orchestrator",
            "Vector Database",
            "File Storage",
            "WebSocket Service",
            "Task Queue",
            "Monitoring Dashboard"
        ]
    
    def _initialize_threats(self) -> List[Threat]:
        """Inicializa ameaças identificadas na V10"""
        return [
            # Spoofing Threats
            Threat(
                id="THREAT-001",
                category=ThreatCategory.SPOOFING,
                description="Token JWT forgery or theft",
                component="Authentication Service",
                attack_vector="Steal JWT via XSS or MITM",
                impact="Impersonate any user, access all data",
                probability="Medium",
                risk_level=RiskLevel.CRITICAL,
                controls=[
                    "Short-lived tokens (15min access, 7d refresh)",
                    "Strict CORS policies",
                    "JWT signature verification with RSA-2048",
                    "Token binding to IP/user-agent",
                    "MFA for admin accounts"
                ]
            ),
            
            # Tampering Threats
            Threat(
                id="THREAT-002",
                category=ThreatCategory.TAMPERING,
                description="Prompt injection in LLM context",
                component="LLM Orchestrator",
                attack_vector="Malicious user input in prompts",
                impact="LLM executes unauthorized actions, data exfiltration",
                probability="High",
                risk_level=RiskLevel.CRITICAL,
                controls=[
                    "Strict separation of system prompt and user input",
                    "Input sanitization with allow-list approach",
                    "Output validation before execution",
                    "Context length limiting",
                    "Prompt injection detection heuristics"
                ]
            ),
            
            Threat(
                id="THREAT-003",
                category=ThreatCategory.TAMPERING,
                description="SQL/NoSQL injection in vector queries",
                component="Vector Database",
                attack_vector="Malformed query parameters",
                impact="Data corruption, unauthorized data access",
                probability="Medium",
                risk_level=RiskLevel.HIGH,
                controls=[
                    "Parameterized queries only",
                    "Input validation with strict schemas",
                    "Query complexity limiting",
                    "Database user with least privileges"
                ]
            ),
            
            # Repudiation Threats
            Threat(
                id="THREAT-004",
                category=ThreatCategory.REPUDIATION,
                description="Lack of audit trail for LLM interactions",
                component="LLM Orchestrator",
                attack_vector="User denies sending malicious prompts",
                impact="Cannot prove malicious intent, compliance violations",
                probability="Medium",
                risk_level=RiskLevel.HIGH,
                controls=[
                    "Immutable audit logs for all LLM interactions",
                    "Cryptographic signing of prompt/response pairs",
                    "User session correlation",
                    "Logs stored in write-once-read-many storage"
                ]
            ),
            
            # Information Disclosure
            Threat(
                id="THREAT-005",
                category=ThreatCategory.INFO_DISCLOSURE,
                description="PII leakage in LLM responses",
                component="LLM Orchestrator",
                attack_vector="Prompt engineering to extract training data",
                impact="GDPR/LGPD violations, reputation damage",
                probability="Medium",
                risk_level=RiskLevel.HIGH,
                controls=[
                    "PII detection and masking in prompts",
                    "Strict data minimization in context",
                    "Output filtering for sensitive patterns",
                    "Regular red team exercises"
                ]
            ),
            
            Threat(
                id="THREAT-006",
                category=ThreatCategory.INFO_DISCLOSURE,
                description="Secrets exposure in environment/logs",
                component="All Services",
                attack_vector="Error messages, debug endpoints",
                impact="Full system compromise",
                probability="Low",
                risk_level=RiskLevel.CRITICAL,
                controls=[
                    "Centralized secret management (Vault)",
                    "Secrets never logged",
                    "Error messages sanitized",
                    "Debug mode disabled in production"
                ]
            ),
            
            # Denial of Service
            Threat(
                id="THREAT-007",
                category=ThreatCategory.DENIAL_OF_SERVICE,
                description="LLM context flooding",
                component="LLM Orchestrator",
                attack_vector="Massive context input to exhaust resources",
                impact="Service degradation, cost explosion",
                probability="High",
                risk_level=RiskLevel.HIGH,
                controls=[
                    "Context length limits per user tier",
                    "Request rate limiting",
                    "Cost-based throttling",
                    "Circuit breakers on LLM providers"
                ]
            ),
            
            # Elevation of Privilege
            Threat(
                id="THREAT-008",
                category=ThreatCategory.ELEVATION_OF_PRIVILEGE,
                description="IDOR in file access endpoints",
                component="File Storage",
                attack_vector="Manipulate file IDs in URLs/parameters",
                impact="Access other users' files",
                probability="Medium",
                risk_level=RiskLevel.HIGH,
                controls=[
                    "Resource-level authorization checks",
                    "UUIDs with proper entropy",
                    "Access control lists per resource",
                    "Regular penetration testing"
                ]
            )
        ]
    
    def generate_report(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Gera relatório completo do threat model"""
        report = {
            "version": "V10.0",
            "generated_at": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
            "summary": {
                "total_threats": len(self.threats),
                "by_category": self._count_by_category(),
                "by_risk": self._count_by_risk(),
                "by_status": self._count_by_status()
            },
            "threats": [self._threat_to_dict(t) for t in self.threats],
            "security_controls": self._get_security_controls(),
            "risk_acceptance_criteria": self._get_risk_acceptance()
        }
        return report
    
    def _count_by_category(self) -> Dict[str, int]:
        counts = {}
        for category in ThreatCategory:
            counts[category.value] = len([
                t for t in self.threats if t.category == category
            ])
        return counts
    
    def _count_by_risk(self) -> Dict[str, int]:
        counts = {}
        for risk in RiskLevel:
            counts[risk.value] = len([
                t for t in self.threats if t.risk_level == risk
            ])
        return counts
    
    def _count_by_status(self) -> Dict[str, int]:
        statuses = set(t.status for t in self.threats)
        return {s: len([t for t in self.threats if t.status == s]) for s in statuses}
    
    def _threat_to_dict(self, threat: Threat) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        return {
            "id": threat.id,
            "category": threat.category.value,
            "description": threat.description,
            "component": threat.component,
            "attack_vector": threat.attack_vector,
            "impact": threat.impact,
            "probability": threat.probability,
            "risk_level": threat.risk_level.value,
            "controls": threat.controls,
            "status": threat.status,
            "created_at": threat.created_at,
            "mitigated_at": threat.mitigated_at
        }
    
    def _get_security_controls(self) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        return [
            {
                "id": "CTRL-001",
                "name": "Zero Trust Architecture",
                "description": "Never trust, always verify",
                "implementation": "All services verify identity and permissions",
                "status": "Planned"
            },
            {
                "id": "CTRL-002",
                "name": "LLM Guardrails",
                "description": "Protection against prompt injection",
                "implementation": "Input sanitization + output validation",
                "status": "Implemented"
            },
            {
                "id": "CTRL-003",
                "name": "Secrets Management",
                "description": "Centralized secrets with rotation",
                "implementation": "HashiCorp Vault integration",
                "status": "In Progress"
            },
            {
                "id": "CTRL-004",
                "name": "WAF Protection",
                "description": "Web Application Firewall",
                "implementation": "ModSecurity + custom rules",
                "status": "Planned"
            }
        ]
    
    def _get_risk_acceptance(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        return {
            "critical_risks": "Zero tolerance - must be mitigated before production",
            "high_risks": "Mitigation required within 72 hours of discovery",
            "medium_risks": "Mitigation required within current sprint",
            "low_risks": "Documented and addressed in next security iteration",
            "acceptance_authority": "CISO + Squad Tech Lead",
            "review_frequency": "Monthly"
        }

# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Sistema de Compliance LGPD/GDPR

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v10-compliance/
├── index.html                    # Dashboard de Compliance
├── package.json
├── .env.example
├── README.md
├── src/
│   ├── server.js                 # Servidor principal
│   ├── database/
│   │   ├── db.js                 # Configuração do banco
│   │   ├── migrations/
